10  Kutheni, Yehova, uqhubeka umele kude?Kutheni uqhubeka uzifihlile ngamaxesha okubandezeleka?
2  Ekuziphakamiseni kwakhe ongendawo umsukela ngobushushu lowo uxhwalekileyo;Babanjiswa ziingcamango abazicingileyo.
3  Kuba ongendawo uyazidumisa ngolangazelelo lokuzingca lomphefumlo wakhe,Nalowo wenza ingeniso ngokungafanelekanga uzisikelele;
4  Ngokuziqhenya kwakhe lowo ungendawo akaphandi;Zonke iingcamango zakhe zezokuthi: “Akukho Thixo.”
5  Iindlela zakhe ziyaphumelela lonke ixesha.Izigwebo zakho ziphakamile, zikude kuye;Bonke abo babonisa ubutshaba kuye, uyabafuthela.
6  Uthe entliziyweni yakhe: “Andisayi kugungqiswa;Isizukulwana emva kwesizukulwana ndiya kuba ngulowo ungekho ntlekeleni.”
7  Umlomo wakhe uzaliswe zizifungo nenkohliso nengcinezelo.Ngaphantsi kolwimi lwakhe kukho inkathazo nokwenzakalisayo.
8  Uhlala elalele imizi;Ekwindawo efihlakeleyo uya kubulala umntu omsulwa.
9  Uqhubeka elalele endaweni efihlakeleyo njengengonyama esekusithekeni.Uqhubeka elalele ukuze amthi hlasi oxhwalekileyo.Umthi hlasi oxhwalekileyo ekuwutsaleni kwakhe uvaleke umnatha wakhe.
10  Utyunyuziwe, uyaqubuda,Yaye umkhosi wabadakumbileyo umele uwele kwiinzipho zakhe ezomeleleyo.
11  Uthe entliziyweni yakhe: “UThixo ulibele.Ubufihlile ubuso bakhe.Ngokuqinisekileyo akasayi kuze abone.”
12  Vuka, Yehova. Owu Thixo, siphakamise isandla sakho.Musa ukubalibala abo baxhwalekileyo.
13  Kutheni lowo ungendawo engamhlonelanga uThixo?Uthe entliziyweni yakhe: “Akuyi kundiphendulisa.”
14  Kuba wena uyibonile inkathazo nengqumbo.Uqhubeka ukhangele, ukuze ubafake esandleni sakho.Uzinikela kuwe lowo unelishwa, inkwenkwe engenayise.Wena ungumncedi wayo.
15  Yaphula ingalo yalowo ungendawo nombi.Ngamana ungabuphanda ubungendawo bakhe de ungafumani nto.
16  UYehova nguKumkani kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo, nangonaphakade.Iintlanga zitshabalele emhlabeni wakhe.
17  Umnqweno wabalulamileyo ngokuqinisekileyo uya kuwuva, Yehova.Uya kuyilungisa intliziyo yabo.Uya kunikela ingqalelo ngendlebe yakho,
18  Ukuze uyigwebe inkwenkwe engenayise nalowo utyunyuziweyo,Ukuze umntu ofayo ongowasemhlabeni angabangeli ukungcangcazela kwakhona.
4  Xa ndibiza, ndiphendule, Thixo wam olilungisa.Ekubandezelekeni umele undenzele indawo ebanzi.Ndibabale uwuve umthandazo wam.
2  Nina bonyana babantu, koda kube nini na uzuko lwam luyinto yokuthukwa,Ngoxa niqhubeka nithanda izinto ezingento,Ngoxa niqhubeka nifuna ukufumana ubuxoki? Seʹlah.
3  Ngoko yazini ukuba ngokuqinisekileyo uYehova uya kumahlula onyanisekileyo wakhe;UYehova uya kuva xa ndimbiza.
4  Phazamisekani, kodwa ningoni.Thethani entliziyweni yenu, emandlalweni wenu, nize nithi cwaka. Seʹlah.
5  Bingelelani imibingelelo yobulungisa,Nize nikholose ngoYehova.
6  Baninzi abathi: “Ngubani na oya kusibonisa ukulunga?”Siphakamisele ukukhanya kobuso bakho, Yehova.
7  Ngokuqinisekileyo uya kuyinika imihlali intliziyo yamEmikhulu ngakumbi kunangexesha laxa ukudla kwabo okuziinkozo newayini yabo entsha iphuphuma.
8  Xa kukho uxolo ndiya kungqengqa ndize ndilale ngoxolo,Kuba nguwe wedwa, Yehova, ondenza ndihlale ndinqabisekile.
26  Ndigwebe, Yehova, kuba ndihambe engqibelelweni yam,Yaye ndikholose ngoYehova, ukuze ndingahexi.
2  Ndihlolisise, Yehova, undivavanye;Sulungekisa izintso zam nentliziyo yam.
3  Kuba ububele bakho bothando buphambi kwamehlo am,Yaye ndihambe enyanisweni yakho.
4  Andihlalanga namadoda angenanyaniso;Yaye andingeni kwabo bazifihlayo oko bakuko.
5  Ndilithiyile ibandla labenzi bobubi,Yaye andihlali nabangendawo.
6  Izandla zam ndiya kuzihlamba ngobumsulwa,Yaye ndiya kujikeleza isibingelelo sakho, Yehova,
7  Ukuze ndivakalise umbulelo ngokuvakalayo,Ndize ndivakalise yonke imisebenzi yakho emangalisayo.
8  Yehova, ndiyithandile indawo yokuhlala yendlu yakhoNendawo yokuhlala yozuko lwakho.
9  Musa ukuwuthabatha naboni umphefumlo wam,Nobomi bam namadoda anetyala legazi,
10  Ekukho ihambo evakalala ezandleni zawo,Nesandla sawo sokunene esizaliswe kukunyoba.
11  Ke mna, ndiya kuhamba engqibelelweni yam.Ndikhulule undibabale.
12  Ngokuqinisekileyo unyawo lwam luya kuma endaweni ethe tyaba;Phakathi kweendimbane ezihlanganiseneyo ndiya kumbonga uYehova.
11  Ndizimela kuYehova.Nina madoda nibuthabatha phi na ubuganga bokuthi emphefumlweni wam:“Sabela entabeni yenu njengentaka!
2  Kuba, khangela! abangendawo bayasigoba isaphetha,Bayalulungisa utolo lwabo kumtya wesaphetha,Ukuze batole kwisithokothoko sobumnyama abo baneentliziyo ezithe tye.
3  Xa iziseko zichithwa,Umele enze ntoni na olilungisa?”
4  UYehova usetempileni yakhe engcwele.UYehova—isemazulwini itrone yakhe.Amehlo akhe ayabona, amehlo akhe aqaqambileyo ahlolisisa oonyana babantu.
5  UYehova uhlolisisa lowo ulilungisa kwanalowo ungendawo,Yaye umphefumlo Wakhe umthiyile ngokuqinisekileyo nabani na othanda ugonyamelo.
6  Uya kunisela phezu kwabangendawo izabatha, umlilo nesalfureNomoya onolophu, njengesahlulo sendebe yabo.
7  Kuba uYehova ulilungisa; uyazithanda izenzo zobulungisa.Ngabathe tye abaya kububona ubuso bakhe.
132  Mkhumbulele, Yehova, uDavideKonke ukuthotywa kwakhe;
2  Indlela awafunga ngayo kuYehova,Indlela awabhambathisa ngayo kuLowo unaMandla kaYakobi wathi:
3  “Andizi kungena ententeni yendlu yam.Andizi kunyuka ndiye emandlalweni kwindawo yam yokuphumla ezukileyo,
4  Andizi kuwanika ubuthongo,Nokozela amehlo am aqaqambileyo,
5  Ndide ndimfumanele indawo uYehova,Umnquba ozukileyo waLowo unaMandla kaYakobi.”
6  Khangela! Sivile ngawo e-Efratha,Siwufumene emihlabeni yehlathi.
7  Masingene emnqubeni wakhe ozukileyo;Masiqubude esitulweni seenyawo zakhe.
8  Khawusukume, Yehova, uye endaweni yakho yokuphumla,Wena neTyeya yamandla akho.
9  Ababingeleli bakho mabambeswe ubulungisa,Nabanyanisekileyo bakho mabamemelele ngovuyo.
10  Ngenxa kaDavide umkhonzi wakho,Musa ukubujika ubuso bothanjisiweyo wakho.
11  UYehova ufungile kuDavide,Enyanisweni akayi kuhlehla kuko oko:“Owesiqhamo sesisu sakhoNdiya kumbeka etroneni yakho.
12  Ukuba oonyana bakho baya kuwugcina umnqophiso wamNezikhumbuzo zam endiya kubafundisa zona,Kwanoonyana babo ngonaphakadeBaya kuhlala etroneni yakho.”
13  Kuba uYehova unyule iZiyon;Uyilangazelele ukuba ibe yindawo yakhe yokuhlala:
14  “Yiyo le indawo yam yokuphumla ngonaphakade;Ndiya kuhlala apha, kuba ndiyilangazelele.
15  Isixhaso sayo ndiya kusisikelela nakanjani na.Amahlwempu ayo ndiya kuwanelisa ngesonka.
16  Nababingeleli bayo ndiya kubambesa ngosindiso;Nabanyanisekileyo bayo nakanjani na baya kumemelela ngovuyo.
17  Ndiya kulukhulisa apho uphondo lukaDavide.Lowo uthanjisiweyo wam ndimmisele ngolungelelwano isibane.
18  Iintshaba zakhe ndiya kuzambesa ngehlazo;Kodwa kuye isithsaba sakhe siya kuchuma.”
49  Yivani oku, nonke zizwana.Bekani indlebe, nonke bemi bale nkqubo yezinto,
2  Nina bonyana boluntu nani bonyana babantu,Nina bazizityebi nani bangamahlwempu ndawonye.
3  Umlomo wam uya kuthetha izinto zobulumko,Nokucamngca kwentliziyo yam kuya kuba kokwezinto zokuqonda.
4  Indlebe yam ndiya kuyithobela kwilizwi elingumzekeliso;Iqhina lam ndiya kulivula ngohadi.
5  Kutheni ndifanele ndoyike ngemihla yobubi,Xa ndingqongwe sisiphoso sabo bathabatha indawo yam?
6  Abo bakholose ngobuncwane babo,Nabaqhubeka beqhayisa ngobuninzi bobutyebi babo,
7  Akukho namnye kubo onokumkhulula nangayiphi na indlela umzalwana wakhe,Okanye anike uThixo intlawulelo ngaye;
8  (Yaye ixabiso lokubakhulula lixabisekileKangangokuba liphele ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo)
9  Ukuba ufanele aphile ngonaphakade angawuboni umhadi.
10  Kuba uyabona ukuba kwanosisilumko uyafa,Kunye nosisiyatha nalowo ungaqiqiyo uyatshabalala,Yaye bafanele babushiye kwabanye ubuncwane babo.
11  Umnqweno wabo ngaphakathi kukuba izindlu zabo zingama kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo,Iminquba yabo kwisizukulwana ukusa kwisizukulwana.Imihlaba yabo bayibiza ngamagama abo.
12  Sekunjalo umntu wasemhlabeni, nangona ebekwa, akanakuhlala;Eneneni ufana namarhamncwa atshatyalalisiweyo.
13  Le yindlela yabo baziziyatha,Nabo baza emva kwabo abakholiswa yintetho yomlomo wabo. Seʹlah.
14  Njengezimvu bamiselwe iShiyol;Ukufa kuya kubalusa;Yaye abathe tye baya kuba nobukhosi kubo kwakusasa,Nobume babo bumele bonakale;Ngamnye kubo uya kuya eShiyol kunakwindawo yokuhlala ephakamileyo.
15  Noko ke, uThixo uya kuwukhulula umphefumlo wam esandleni seShiyol,Kuba uya kundamkela. Seʹlah.
16  Musa ukoyika ngenxa yokuba umntu othile ezuza ubutyebi,Ngenxa yokuba uzuko lwendlu yakhe lusanda,
17  Kuba xa esifa akanakuthabatha nantoni na;Uzuko lwakhe aluyi kuhla naye.
18  Kuba ebudeni bokudla kwakhe ubomi waqhubeka ewusikelela umphefumlo wakhe;(Yaye abantu baya kukubonga ngenxa yokuba uzenzela okuhle)
19  Ekugqibeleni umphefumlo wakhe ufikelela kwisizukulwana sookhokho bakhe.Abasayi kuphinda bakubone ukukhanya.
20  Umntu wasemhlabeni, nangona ebekwa, akanakuqonda,Ngokwenene ufana namarhamncwa atshatyalalisiweyo.

2  IYerusalem—njengoko ijikelezwe ziintaba,Ngoko uYehova ubajikelezile abantu bakheUkususela ngoku kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo.

5  Waza wavelisa isikhumbuzo kwaYakobi,Wabeka umthetho kwaSirayeli,Izinto awaziyalela ookhokho bethu,Ukuze zaziwe ngoonyana babo;
6  Ukuze isizukulwana esizayo, oonyana ababeza kuzalwa, bazazi,Ukuze baphakame baze bazibalisele ababo oonyana,
7  Yaye babeke intembelo yabo kuThixoBangalulibali uqheliselo lukaThixo kodwa bagcine imiyalelo yakhe.
8  Bafanele bangabi njengookhokho babo,Isizukulwana esineenkani nesinemvukelo,Isizukulwana esingayilungisanga intliziyo yasoNesinomoya ongakholosekanga kuThixo.
9  Oonyana bakaEfrayim, nangona bengabatoli abaxhobileyo besaphetha,Babuya umva ngemini yomlo.
10  Abawugcinanga umnqophiso kaThixo,Yaye bala ukuhamba emthethweni wakhe.
11  Baza baqalisa nokuzilibala izenzo zakheNemisebenzi yakhe emangalisayo awayebangele bayibona.
12  Phambi kookhokho babo wayenze ngokumangalisayoElizweni laseYiputa, intsimi yaseTsowan.
13  Wahlukanisa ulwandle, ukuze abaweze,waza wabangela amanzi ema njengedama.
14  Waqhubeka ebakhokela ngelifu eminiYaye ubusuku bonke ngokukhanya komlilo.
15  Wahlukanisa amawa entlango,Ukuze awabangele asele okuninzi kanye njengamanzi anzongonzongo.
16  Kwaye wavelisa imisinga engxondorheniebangela amanzi ahle kanye njengemilambo.
17  Baqhubeka bemona ngakumbiNgokuvukela Oyena Uphakamileyo kummandla ongumqwebedu;
18  Baza bamvavanya uThixo entliziyweni yaboNgokucelela umphefumlo wabo into edliwayo.
19  Ngoko baqalisa ukuthetha nxamnye noThixo.Bathi: “Ngaba uThixo unako ukulungiselela itafile entlango?”
20  Khangela! Wabetha iliwaUkuze amanzi aqukuqele nemisinga iphuphume.“Ngaba uyakwazi nokunika isonka,Okanye ngaba unako ukulungiselela abantu bakhe isixhaso?”
21  Kungenxa yoko uYehova wevayo waza wavutha ngumsindo;Kwaza kwaphenjelwa uYakobi umlilo,Kwehla umsindo phezu koSirayeli.
22  Kuba abazange bakholwe kuThixo,Yaye abazange bakholose ngosindiso lwakhe.
23  Wayalela isibhakabhaka esinamafu phezulu,Waza wavula neengcango zezulu.
24  Waqhubeka ebanisela imana ukuba badle,Waza wabanika nokudla okuziinkozo kwezulu.
25  Abantu badla isonka sabanamandla;Umphako awabathumelela wona ukuze baneliseke.
26  Wabangela ukuba kuqhambuke umoya wasempuma emazulwiniWenza umoya wasezantsi uvuthuze ngamandla awo.
27  Waza wenza kwana isixhaso phezu kwabo njengemvula,Kwanezidalwa eziphaphazelayo ezinamaphiko njengentlabathi yolwandle.
28  Waqhubeka ezenza ziwe phakathi enkampini,Macala onke emnqubeni wakhe.
29  Baqhubeka besidla bezanelisa kakhulu,Wabanika oko babekunqwenela.
30  Babengawulahlanga umnqweno wabo,Ngoxa ukudla kwabo kwakusesemlonyeni wabo,
31  Ngoxa ingqumbo kaThixo yenyukayo nxamnye nabo.Waza waqhubeka ebabulala phakathi kwabomeleleyo babo;Nabafana bakwaSirayeli wabenza bathi folokohlo.
32  Phezu kwako konke oku bona ngakumbiBaza abakholwa emisebenzini yakhe emangalisayo.
33  Ngoko wayiphelisa imihla yabo ngokungathi ingumphunga kuphela,Neminyaka yabo ngokuphazamiseka.
34  Ngalo lonke ixesha ebabulala, babebuzisa ngaye,Baza babuya bamfuna uThixo.
35  Baza bakhumbula ukuba uThixo wayeLiliwa labo,Nokuba uThixo ongOyena Uphakamileyo wayenguMphindezeli wabo.
36  Kwaye bazama ukumqhatha ngomlomo wabo;Nangolwimi lwabo bazama ukumxokisa.
37  Nentliziyo yabo yayingaqinanga kuye;Yaye abazingqinanga bethembekile kumnqophiso wakhe.
38  Kodwa wayenenceba; wayezigubungela iziphoso aze angonakalisi.Izihlandlo ezininzi wayewubuyisa umsindo wakhe,Yaye wayengawuvuseleli umsindo wakhe.
39  Waqhubeka ekhumbula ukuba babeyinyama,Nokuba umoya uyaphuma ungabuyi.
40  Babemvukela ngokufuthi kangakanani entlango,Babemenza azive ebuhlungu entlango!
41  Izihlandlo ngezihlandlo babemvavanya uThixo,Bemenza buhlungu Lowo uyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.
42  Abasikhumbulanga isandla sakhe,Usuku awabakhulula ngalo kutshaba,
43  Indlela awayibeka ngayo imiqondiso yakhe eYiputaNemimangaliso yakhe entsimini yaseTsowan;
44  Nendlela awayitshintsha ngayo ibe ligazi imijelo yomNayile,Ukuze bangakwazi ukusela kwimisinga yabo.
45  Wabathumelela izibawu, ukuze zibadle;Namasele, ukuze abonakalise.
46  Waqalisa ukunikela imveliso yabo kumaphela,Nokubulaleka kwabo kwiinkumbi.
47  Imidiliya yabo wayibulala ngesichothoNemithi yabo yesikamore ngamatye esichotho.
48  Namaqegu abo wawanikela kwisichothoNemfuyo yabo wayinikela kumkhuhlane onjengomlilo.
49  Wabathumelela umsindo wakhe ovuthayo,Ukuvutha komsindo nesiqalekiso nokubandezeleka,Abathunywa abaziingelosi abazisa intlekele.
50  Wawulungiselela umendo umsindo wakhe.Akazange ayinqande imiphefumlo yabo ekufeni;Nobomi babo wabunikela kwindyikitya yokufa.
51  Ekugqibeleni wawaxabela onke amazibulo eYiputa,Ukuqala kwamandla abo okuvelisa inzala ezintenteni zikaHam.
52  Emva koko wabangela abantu bakhe bahamba njengomhlambi,Wabaqhuba njengomhlambi entlango.
53  Waqhubeka ebakhokela benqabisekile, kwaye abazange bankwantye;Nolwandle lwazigubungela iintshaba zabo.
54  Wabazisa kummandla wakhe ongcwele,Lo mmandla weentaba owazuzwa sisandla sakhe sokunene.
55  Ngenxa yabo wazigxotha iintlanga,Waza ngolutya lokulinganisa wababela ilifa,Ukuze abangele izizwe zakwaSirayeli zihlale emakhayeni azo.
56  Kwaye baqalisa ukumvavanya nokumvukela uThixo ongOyena Uphakamileyo,Nezikhumbuzo zakhe abazange bazigcine.
57  Kwakhona baqhubeka bephambuka besenza ngobuqhophololo njengookhokho babo;Bajika njengesaphetha esityeketyeke.
58  Yaye baqhubeka bemcaphukisa ngeendawo zabo eziphakamileyo,Nangemifanekiso yabo eqingqiweyo baqhubeka bemenza abe nekhwele.
59  Weva uThixo waza wavutha ngumsindo,Waza wamcekisa kakhulu uSirayeli.
60  Yaye ekugqibeleni wawushiya umnquba waseShilo,Intente awayehlala kuyo phakathi kwabantu basemhlabeni.
61  Kwaye wawanikela ekuthinjweni amandla akheNobuhle bakhe esandleni sotshaba.
62  Waqhubeka ebanikela ekreleni abantu bakhe,Wavutha umsindo wakhe kwilifa lakhe.
63  Abafana bakhe badliwa ngumlilo,Neentombi zakhe ezinyulu azizange zidunyiswe.
64  Ke bona ababingeleli bakhe, bawa ngekrele,Nabahlolokazi babo abazange balile.
65  Wandula ke uYehova wavuka ekulaleni kwakhe,Njengalowo unamandla xa eqabuka kwiwayini.
66  Wazixabela ngasemva iintshaba zakhe;Wazinika ungcikivo olusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
67  Wayigatya intente kaYosefu;Nesizwe sakwaEfrayim akazange asinyule.
68  Kodwa wanyula isizwe sakwaYuda,INtaba yeZiyon, awayithandayo.
69  Waqalisa ukuyakha njengeendawo eziphakamileyo ingcwele yakhe,Njengomhlaba awuseke ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
70  Ngoko wakhetha uDavide umkhonzi wakheWamthabatha kubuhlanti bomhlambi.
71  Wamthabatha ekulandeleni iimazi azanyisayoWamzisa ekubeni ngumalusi phezu koYakobi isizwana sakheNaphezu koSirayeli ilifa lakhe.
72  Kwaye waqalisa ukubalusa ngokwengqibelelo yentliziyo yakhe,Nangobuchule bezandla zakhe waqalisa ukubakhokela.
8  Owu Yehova Nkosi yethu, hayi indlela elinobungangamsha ngayo igama lakho emhlabeni wonke,Isidima sakho siphela sibaliswa ngaphezu kwamazulu!
2  Emilonyeni yabantwana nabanyayo useke amandla,Ngenxa yabo babonisa ubutshaba kuwe,Ukuze wenze uthsaba nalowo uziphindezelelayo ayeke.
3  Xa ndibona amazulu akho, imisebenzi yeminwe yakho,Inyanga neenkwenkwezi ozilungiseleleyo,
4  Uyintoni na umntu ofayo le nto umkhumbulayo,Nonyana womntu wasemhlabeni le nto umnyamekelayo?
5  Wamenza wangaphantsi kancinane kwabo banjengothixo,Waza wamthwesa ngozuko nobungangamsha.
6  Umenza alawule imisebenzi yezandla zakho;Yonke into uyibeke phantsi kweenyawo zakhe:
7  Amathole neenkabi zeenkomo, zonke,Kwanamarhamcwa asendle,
8  Iintaka zezulu neentlanzi zolwandle,Nantoni na edlula kwiindlela zeelwandle.
9  Owu Yehova Nkosi yethu, hayi indlela elinobungangamsha ngayo igama lakho emhlabeni wonke!
72  Owu Thixo, mnike ukumkani izigwebo zakho,Nobulungisa bakho unyana wokumkani.
2  Ngamana angaligweba ngobulungisa ityala labantu bakhoNelabaxhwalekileyo bakho ngemimiselo.
3  Iintaba mazibazisele uxolo abantu,Kwaneenduli, ngobulungisa.
4  Makabagwebe abaxhwalekileyo ebantwini,Makabasindise oonyana babo bangamahlwempu,Makamtyumze lowo uqhathayo.
5  Baya kukoyika logama nje kusekho ilanga,Naphambi kwenyanga isizukulwana emva kwesizukulwana.
6  Uya kuhlela phezu kwengca echetyiweyo njengemvula,Njengomvumbi omanzisa umhlaba.
7  Ngomhla wakhe uya kuhluma olilungisa,Nobuninzi boxolo ide ingabi sabakho inyanga.
8  Uya kuba nabalawulwa abasukela elwandle baye kufikelela elwandleBasukele eMlanjeni base eziphelweni zehlabathi.
9  Phambi kwakhe abemi bemimandla engenamanzi baya kuqubuda,Neentshaba zakhe ziya kukhotha uthuli.
10  Ookumkani baseTarshishe nabeziqithi—Baya kuhlawula unikelo.Ookumkani bakwaShebha nabakwaSebha—Baya kunikela isipho.
11  Yaye bonke ookumkani baya kuqubuda kuye;Ke zona zonke iintlanga ziya kumkhonza.
12  Kuba uya kumhlangula lowo ulihlwempu ukhalela uncedo,Kwanalowo uxhwalekileyo nabani na ongenamncedi.
13  Uya kuba nosizi ngesisweli nangehlwempu,Nemiphefumlo yabangamahlwempu uya kuyisindisa.
14  Uya kuwukhulula umphefumlo wabo kwingcinezelo nakugonyamelo.Negazi labo liya kuxabiseka emehlweni akhe.
15  Makaphile, aze anikwe nethile kwigolide yakwaShebha.Kuze kuthandazwe rhoqo ngenxa yakhe;Makabongwe imini yonke.
16  Kuya kubakho ukudla okuziinkozo okuninzi emhlabeni;Encotsheni yeentaba kuya kubakho ukuphuphuma.Isiqhamo sakhe siya kuba njengaseLebhanon,Nabo baphuma esixekweni baya kutyatyamba njengotyani bomhlaba.
17  Igama lakhe malifikelele kwixesha elingenammiselo;Malande phambi kwelanga igama lakhe,Mabazisikelele ngaye;Zonke iintlanga mazibhengeze ukuba unoyolo.
18  Makabongwe uYehova uThixo, uThixo kaSirayeli,Nguye yedwa owenza imisebenzi emangalisayo.
19  Malibongwe igama lakhe elizukileyo kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo,Nozuko lwakhe luzalise umhlaba wonke.Amen Amen.
20  Imithandazo kaDavide, unyana kaYese, ifikelele esiphelweni.
69  Ndisindise, Thixo, kumanzi afikelele emphefumlweni wam.
2  Nditshone eludakeni olunzulu, ekungekho mhlaba wokuma kulo.Ndingene emanzini anzulu,Yaye umsinga oqukuqelayo undikhukulisile.
3  Ndidiniwe kukumemeza;Umqala wam uyarhwexa.Amehlo am aphelelwe elindele kuThixo wam.
4  Abo bandithiye ngaphandle kwesizathu baninzi ngaphezu kweenwele zentloko yam.Abo bandithulisayo, beziintshaba zam ngaphandle kwesizathu, baninzi.Oko bendingakuthabathanga ngokukuphanga ndiyakubuyisela.
5  Owu Thixo, wena uyabazi ubudenge bam,Akufihlakalanga kuwe ukuba netyala kwam.
6  Owu ngamana abo bathembela ngawe abangebi neentloni ngenxa yam,Owu Nkosi enguMongami, Yehova wemikhosi.Owu ngamana abo bakufunayo abangethotywa ngenxa yam,Owu Thixo kaSirayeli.
7  Kuba ngenxa yakho ndiyinto yokungcikivwa,Ubuso bam bugutyungelwe kukuthotywa.
8  Ndahlukanisiwe kubantakwethu,Yaye ndingowasemzini koonyana bakama.
9  Kuba ukuzondelela indlu yakho ngokupheleleyo kundidlile,Ungcikivo lwabo bakungcikivayo luphezu kwam.
10  Ndaza ndaqalisa ukulila ngokuzila ukutya komphefumlo wam,Kodwa kwaba lungcikivo kum.
11  Ekwenzeni kwam amarhonya aba sisinxibo sam,Kubo ndaba ngumzekelo.
12  Abo bahlala esangweni baqalisa ukuzixhalabisa ngam,Ndaza ndaba yingoma yabaseli besiselo esinxilisayo.
13  Ke mna, bendithandaza kuwe, Yehova,Ngexesha elamkelekileyo, Thixo.Ngobuninzi bobubele bakho bothando ndiphendule ngenyaniso yosindiso lwakho.
14  Ndihlangule eludakeni, ukuze ndingatshoni.Owu ngamana ndingahlangulwa kwabo bandithiyileyo nasemanzini anzulu.
15  Owu ngamana umsinga oqukuqelayo wamanzi awungendikhukulisi,Neenzulu azingendiginyi,Lize nequla liwuvale kum umlomo walo.
16  Ndiphendule, Yehova, ngokuba bulungile ububele bakho bothando.Ngokobuninzi beenceba zakho buyela kum,
17  Yaye musa ukubufihla ubuso bakho kumkhonzi wakho.Kuba ndisezingxakini ezinkulu, ndiphendule ngokukhawuleza.
18  Sondela emphefumlweni wam, uwuhlangule;Ngenxa yeentshaba zam ndikhulule.
19  Wena ulwazi lonke ungcikivo lwam nehlazo lam nokuthotywa kwam.Bonke abo babonisa ubutshaba kum baphambi kwakho.
20  Ungcikivo luyaphule intliziyo yam, yaye inxeba alinyangeki.Ndiqhubeke ndinethemba lokuba kukho uthile oya kubonisa uvelwano, kodwa bekungekho namnye;Nokuba kuya kubakho abathuthuzeli, kodwa andafumana namnye.
21  Kodwa bandityise isityalo esinetyhefu,Ukuze ndithobe unxano bazame ukundinika iviniga.
22  Itafile yabo ephambi kwabo mayibe sisibatha.Nentlalo-ntle yabo ibe ngumgibe.
23  Mawabe mnyama amehlo abo ukuze bangaboni;Isinqe sabo sibangele sigexe rhoqo.
24  Phalazela isiqalekiso sakho phezu kwabo,Uze umsindo wakho ovuthayo ubafikele.
25  Mayiphanze inkampu yabo ebiyelwe ngodonga;Ezintenteni zabo kungabikho uhlalayo.
26  Kuba lowo wena umbethileyo bamsukele,Yaye iintlungu zabo bahlatyiweyo baqhubekile bezibalisa.
27  Yongeza isiphoso phezu kwesiphoso sabo,Bangangeni ebulungiseni bakho.
28  Mabacinywe encwadini yabaphilayo,Yaye kwanga abangebhalwa nabangamalungisa.
29  Kodwa ndixhwalekile yaye ndiyaqaqanjelwa.Owu Thixo, ngamana usindiso lwakho lungandikhusela.
30  Ndiya kulidumisa ngengoma igama likaThixo,Ndize ndimenze mkhulu ngombulelo.
31  Oku kuya kukholeka ngakumbi kuYehova kunenkunzi yenkomo,Ngaphezu kwethole lenkomo eliyinkunzi elineempondo, elinophuphu olucandekileyo.
32  Abalulamileyo baya kubona ngokuqinisekileyo; baya kuvuya.Nina bafuna uThixo, intliziyo yenu mayiqhubeke iphila.
33  Kuba uYehova uphulaphula abangamahlwempu,Yaye eneneni akayi kuwadelela amabanjwa akhe.
34  Malimdumise izulu nomhlaba,Iilwandle nayo yonke into enambuzelayo kuzo.
35  Kuba uThixo uya kuyisindisa iZiyonAze azakhe izixeko zakwaYuda;Kwaye ngokuqinisekileyo baya kuhlala apho baze bazidle ilifa.
36  Inzala yabakhonzi bakhe iya kuzidla ilifa,Baze abo bathanda igama lakhe bahlale kuzo.
30  Ndiya kukuphakamisa, Yehova, kuba unditsale ndenyukaYaye akuzivumelanga iintshaba zam zanemihlali phezu kwam.
2  Owu Yehova Thixo wam, ndikhalele uncedo kuwe, waza wandiphilisa.
3  Owu Yehova, uwukhuphile eShiyol umphefumlo wam;Undigcine ndiphila, ukuze ndingehli ndiye emhadini.
4  Mculeleni uncuthu lwengoma uYehova, nina banyanisekileyo bakhe,Bulelani isikhumbuzo sakhe esingcwele;
5  Ngenxa yokuba ukuba ngaphantsi komsindo wakhe kokomzuzwana,Ukuba ngaphantsi kwenkoliseko yakhe kokobomi bonke.Ngokuhlwa kusenokubakho ukulila, kodwa kusasa kukho intswahla yovuyo.
6  Ke mna, ndithe ekonwabeni kwam:“Andisayi kushukunyiswa.”
7  Owu Yehova, ngenkoliseko yakho intaba yam uyimise yanamandla.Ubufihlile ubuso bakho; ndaba ngulowo uphazamisekileyo.
8  Kuwe, Yehova, ndaqhubeka ndibiza;Yaye ndaqhubeka ndibongoza uYehova ndicela ubabalo.
9  Yiyiphi na ingenelo ekhoyo egazini lam xa ndisehlela emhadini?Ngaba uthuli luya kukubonga? Ngaba luya kukuxela ukuba nenyaniso kwakho?
10  Yiva, Yehova, undibabale.Owu Yehova, zingqine ungumncedi wam.
11  Ukuzila kwam ukutshintshe kwaba kukungqungqa;Ulikhulule irhonya lam, yaye undigcina ndibhinqe imihlali,
12  Ukuze uzuko lwam lukuculele uncuthu lwengoma lungathi cwaka.Owu Yehova Thixo wam, ndiya kukubonga ixesha elingenammiselo.
16  Ndigcine, Thixo, ngokuba ndisabela kuwe.
2  Ndithe kuYehova: “UnguYehova; ukulunga kwam, akwenzelwanga wena,
3  Kodwa kokwabo bangcwele emhlabeni.Bona, kwanabo banobungangamsha, ngabo abandiyolisayo.”
4  Ziba ninzi iintlungu kwabo bathi, xa kukho omnye umntu, bakhawuleze ukumsukela.Andisayi kuyithulula iminikelo yabo ethululwayo yegazi,Yaye andiyi kuwathwala ngemilebe yam amagama abo.
5  UYehova sisahlulo sesabelo endisinikiweyo nesendebe yam.Ulibambe waliqinisa iqashiso lam.
6  Izintya zokulinganisa zindiwele ezindaweni ezithandekayo.Eneneni, izinto zam zingqineke zikholekile kum.
7  Ndiya kumbonga uYehova, ondinike icebiso.Eneneni, ebudeni bobusuku izintso zam zindilungisile.
8  UYehova ndimbeka phambi kwam rhoqo.Ngenxa yokuba ungakwisandla sam sasekunene, andiyi kushukunyiswa.
9  Ngoko ke intliziyo yam inemihlali, nozuko lwam lutyekele ekuvuyeni.Nenyama yam iya kuhlala inqabisekile.
10  Kuba akuyi kuwushiya eShiyol umphefumlo wam.Akuyi kumvumela onyanisekileyo wakho abone umhadi.
11  Uya kundibangela ndiwubone umendo wobomi.Ebusweni bakho ndiba nemihlali ngokwaneleyo;Kwisandla sakho sasekunene kukho ubumnandi ngonaphakade.
96  Mvumeleni ingoma entsha uYehova.Mvumeleni uYehova, nonke nina bantu basemhlabeni.
2  Mvumeleni uYehova, nilibonge igama lakhe.Imihla ngemihla xelani iindaba ezilungileyo zosindiso lwakhe.
3  Vakalisani uzuko lwakhe phakathi kweentlanga,Phakathi kwezizwana zonke imisebenzi yakhe emangalisayo.
4  Kuba mkhulu uYehova yaye ngowokudunyiswa kakhulu.Uyoyikeka ngaphezu kwabo bonke abanye oothixo.
5  Kuba bonke oothixo bezizwana bangoothixo abangenaxabiso;Kodwa yena uYehova, wenze wona kanye amazulu.
6  Isidima nobungangamsha buphambi kwakhe;Amandla nobuhle busengcweleni yakhe.
7  Mnikeni uYehova, nina zintsapho zezizwana,Mnikeni uYehova uzuko namandla.
8  Mnikeni uYehova uzuko lwegama lakhe;Thwalani isipho, nize ezintendelezweni zakhe.
9  Qubudani kuYehova nihombe ngobungcwele;Yibani sezintlungwini eziqatha ngenxa yakhe, nonke nina bantu basemhlabeni.
10  Yithini phakathi kweentlanga: “UYehova ngukumkani.Nelizwe elinemveliso limiselwe ngokuqinileyo khon’ ukuze lingabi nakushukunyiswa.Uya kuligweba ityala lezizwana ngokuthe tye.”
11  Makabe nemihlali amazulu, nomhlaba uvuye.Malududume ulwandle noko kuluzalisileyo.
12  Mayigcobe intsimi nako konke okukuyo.Kwangaxeshanye yonke imithi yehlathi mayimemelele ngovuyo
13  Phambi koYehova. Kuba ufikile;Kuba uze kuwugweba umhlaba.Uya kugweba ilizwe elinemveliso ngobulungisaNezizwana ngokuthembeka kwakhe.
35  Owu Yehova, lichophele ityala lam kwabo bamelene nam;Yilwa nabo benza imfazwe nam.
2  Bamba ingweletshetshe nekhaka elikhulu,Uze uphakame undincede,
3  Uze urhole umkhonto nezembe elibukhali macala uhlangabeze abo bandisukelayo.Yithi kumphefumlo wam: “Ndilusindiso lwakho.”
4  Kwanga bangadana bathotywe abo bazingela umphefumlo wam.Kwanga bangajikwa badane abo bandicebela intlekele.
5  Ngamana banganjengomququ ngaphambi komoya,Ize ingelosi kaYehova ibatyhale.
6  Indlela yabo mayibe bubumnyama neendawo ezimtyibilizi,Ingelosi kaYehova ibasukele.
7  Kuba bandifihlele iminatha yabo ngaphandle kwesizathu;Ngaphandle kwesizathu bawumbele umphefumlo wam.
8  Makafikelwe kukonakala engazi,Umnatha wakhe awufihlileyo mawumbambe;Makawele kuwo onakale.
9  Kodwa owam umphefumlo mawuvuye kuYehova;Mawugcobe ngosindiso lwakhe.
10  Onke amathambo am mawathi:“Owu Yehova, ngubani na onjengawe,Omhlangulayo oxhwalekileyo kulowo unamandla kunaye,Noxhwalekileyo nalowo ulihlwempu kulowo umphangayo?”
11  Kuphakama amangqina anogonyamelo;Andibuza oko ndingakwaziyo.
12  Okulungileyo bandivuza ngokubi,Bexhwalekisa umphefumlo wam.
13  Ke mna, xa begula, isinxibo sam sasingamarhonya,Umphefumlo wam ndawuxhwalekisa ngokuzila ukutya,Yaye umthandazo wam wawubuyela esifubeni sam.
14  Ngokungathi liqabane lam nomntakwethu,Ndandihambahamba njengalowo uzilele unina.Ndibuhlungu, ndaqubuda.
15  Kodwa ekujingxeleni kwam baba nemihlali baza bahlanganisana ndawonye;Bahlanganisana ndawonye nxamnye nam,Bendibetha ngoxa ndingazi;Bandihlekeza baza abathi cwaka.
16  Phakathi kwabahleki abawexukileyo ngenxa yeqebengwanaBabenditshixizela amazinyo.
17  Owu Yehova, uya kukubona kude kube nini na?Wubuyise umphefumlo wam ekubhuqweni ngabo,Kwanalowo umnye kuphela kwiingonyama ezintsha ezinesingci.
18  Ndiya kukubonga ebandleni elikhulu;Ndiya kukudumisa phakathi kwesizwana esikhulu.
19  Owu ngamana abo baziintshaba zam ngaphandle kwesizathu bangangabi nemihlali ngam;Ke bona abo bandithiye ngaphandle kwesizathu, mabangaqobi iliso.
20  Kuba abathethi luxolo;Kodwa nxamnye nabo bathuleyo bomhlabaBaqhubeka beceba inkohliso.
21  Kwanemilomo yabo bandivulela ibe banzi.Bathe: “Heke! Heke! iliso lethu likubonile oku.”
22  Owu Yehova, ukubonile, musa ukuthi cwaka.Owu Yehova, musa ukuba kude nam.
23  Zivuselele uvuke ukuze undigwebele,Owu Thixo wam, Yehova, kwisimangalo sam.
24  Ndigwebe ngokobulungisa bakho, Yehova Thixo wam,Yaye ngamana bangangabi nemihlali ngam.
25  Owu ngamana bangangathi entliziyweni yabo: “Heke, umphefumlo wethu!”Ngamana bangangathi: “Simginyile.”
26  Mababe neentloni badane xa bebonkeAbo bayivuyelayo intlekele yam.Mabambeswe ihlazo nokuthotywa abo bazigwagwisayo kum.
27  Mabamemelele ngovuyo babe nemihlali abo bayoliswa bubulungisa bam,Baze bathi rhoqo:“UYehova makenziwe mkhulu, oyoliswayo luxolo lomkhonzi wakhe.”
28  Nolwimi maluvakalise ngelizwi eliphantsi ubulungisa bakho,Indumiso yakho imini yonke.
18  Ndiya kuba nomsa kuwe, Yehova mandla am.
2  UYehova yingxondorha yam negwiba lam noMsindisi wam.UThixo wam liliwa lam. Ndiya kusabela kuye,Ulikhaka lam nophondo lwam losindiso, indawo yam ephakamileyo nenqabisekileyo.
3  Ndiya kubiza kuLowo ungowokudunyiswa, uYehova,Yaye ndiya kusindiswa kwiintshaba zam.
4  Iintsontelo zokufa zindirhawule;Izikhukula zamadoda angamatshivela nazo zaqhubeka zindinkwantyisa.
5  Iintsontelo zeShiyol zandingqonga;Imigibe yokufa yajamelana nam.
6  Ekubandezelekeni kwam ndaqhubeka ndibiza kuYehova,Ndaqhubeka ndikhalela uncedo kuThixo wam.Esetempileni yakhe waliva ilizwi lam,Nokukhalela uncedo kwam phambi kwakhe kwafika ezindlebeni zakhe.
7  Yaye umhlaba waqalisa ukugungqa nokunyikima,Neziseko zeentaba zaphazamiseka,Zaqhubeka zihexa ngenxa yokuba wayecaphukile.
8  Kwenyuka umsi emathatheni akhe, yaye umlilo ophuma emlonyeni wakhe waqhubeka uqwenga;Amalahle aphuma kuye avutha.
9  Wawathoba ke amazulu waza wehla.Yaye ngaphantsi kweenyawo zakhe kwakukho intsunguzi yesithokothoko.
10  Weza ekhwele ikherubhi ephaphazela,Wafika ngesantya ekhwele emaphikweni omoya.
11  Wandula ke wenza ubumnyama baba yindawo yakhe yokuzifihla,Njengomnquba wakhe macala onke,Amanzi amnyama, iingqimba zamafu.
12  Ekuqaqambeni okuphambi kwakhe kwaphuma amafu akhe awayedlula,Isichotho namalahle avuthayo omlilo.
13  Waza uYehova waqalisa ukududuma esemazulwini,Yaye Oyena Uphakamileyo waqalisa ukukhupha ilizwi lakhe,Isichotho namalahle avuthayo omlilo.
14  Waqhubeka ethumela iintolo zakhe, ukuze abachithachithe;Yaye wathumela imibane, ukuze avuse isiphithiphithi phakathi kwabo.
15  Yaye imiphantsi yemisinga yamanzi yabonakala,Nemithombo yelizwe elinemveliso yatyhilekaNgenxa yokukhalima kwakho, Yehova, ngokufutha kwempefumlo yamathatha akho.
16  Wathumela ephezulu, wandithabatha,Wanditsala ndaphuma emanzini amaninzi.
17  Wandihlangula kutshaba lwam olomeleleyo,Nakwabo bandithiyileyo; ngenxa yokuba babomelele ngakumbi kunam.
18  Baqhubeka bendihlangabeza ngemini yentlekele yam,Kodwa uYehova wandixhasa.
19  Yaye wandikhuphela endaweni ebanzi;Wandihlangula, ngenxa yokuba wayeyoliswa ndim.
20  UYehova undivuza ngokobulungisa bam;Undibuyekeza ngokokuhlambuluka kwezandla zam.
21  Kuba ndizigcinile iindlela zikaYehova,Yaye andimkanga ngobungendawo kuThixo wam.
22  Kuba zonke izigwebo zakhe ziphambi kwam,Nemimiselo yakhe andiyi kuyishenxisa kum.
23  Ndiya kuzingqina ndingenasiphoso kuye,Ndizigcine ekwenzeni isiphoso.
24  Makandibuyekeze uYehova ngokobulungisa bam,Ngokokuhlambuluka kwezandla zam phambi kwamehlo akhe.
25  Kulowo unyanisekileyo uya kwenza ngokunyaniseka;Uya kuqhubana nendoda engenasiphoso, eyomeleleyo ngokungenasiphoso;
26  Kulowo uzigcina ehlambulukile uya kuzibonisa uhlambulukile;Kulowo unobugwenxa uya kuzibonakalisa ugwenxa;
27  Ngenxa yokuba wena uya kubasindisa abantu abaxhwalekileyo;Kodwa amehlo anekratshi uya kuwathoba.
28  Kuba wena, Yehova, uya kusikhanyisa isibane sam;UThixo wam uya kubenza bukhanye ubumnyama bam.
29  Kuba ngawe ndinokuwahlangabeza amatutu;Yaye ngoThixo wam ndinokulunyuka udonga.
30  Ke yena uTHIXO oyinyaniso, igqibelele indlela yakhe;Ilizwi likaYehova lisulungekile.Ulikhaka kubo bonke abo basabela kuye.
31  Kuba ngubani na uThixo ingenguye uYehova?Ngubani na iliwa ngaphandle koThixo wethu?
32  UTHIXO oyinyaniso nguLowo undibhinqisa ngokuqinileyo ngamandla,Yaye uya kuyenza igqibelele indlela yam,
33  Esenza iinyawo zam zibe njengezamaxhamakazi,Yaye undigcina ndimi ezindaweni eziphakamileyo kum.
34  Izandla zam uzifundisa imfazwe,Neengalo zam zigobe isaphetha sobhedu.
35  Uya kundinika ikhaka lakho losindiso,Yaye isandla sakho sasekunene siya kundixhasa,Ize eyakho intobeko indenze mkhulu.
36  Amanyathelo am uya kuwenzela indawo ebanzi ngokwaneleyo ngaphantsi kwam,Yaye ngokuqinisekileyo amaqatha am akayi kuhexa.
37  Ndiya kuzisukela ndizifumane iintshaba zam;Yaye andiyi kubuya zide zitshabalale.
38  Ndiya kuzitshitshisa ukuze zingakwazi ukuphakama kwakhona;Ziya kuwa phantsi kweenyawo zam.
39  Uya kundibhinqisa amandla ukuze ndilungele imfazwe;Abo bandivukelayo uya kubenza bathi folokohlo phantsi kwam.
40  Ke zona iintshaba zam, uya kuzenza zindinikele umva;Yaye abo bandithiye kakhulu, ndiya kubathulisa.
41  Bakhalela uncedo, kodwa akukho msindisi,Bakhala kuYehova, kodwa eneneni akabaphenduli.
42  Yaye ndiya kubaguba bacoleke njengothuli phambi komoya;Ndiya kubaphalaza njengodaka lwezitrato.
43  Uya kundisindisa ekuhlatyweni amadlala ngabantu.Uya kundimisela ndibe yintloko yeentlanga.Isizwana endingasazanga—siya kundikhonza.
44  Baya kundithobela ngondiva nje kuphela;Abasemzini baya kuza kum bekhokhoba.
45  Abasemzini baya kuphelelwa,Yaye baya kuphuma bengcangcazela kwiindonga zabo zokuzikhusela.
46  UYehova uyaphila, malibongwe ke iLiwa lam,Kwaye makaphakanyiswe uTHIXO wosindiso lwam.
47  UTHIXO oyinyaniso nguMniki wezenzo zempindezelo kum;Yaye izizwana uzithoba phantsi kwam.
48  Uyandisindisa kwiintshaba zam ezinomsindo;Uya kundiphakamisa ngaphezu kwabo bandivukelayo,Uya kundihlangula kwindoda yogonyamelo.
49  Ngenxa yoko ndiya kukubonga phakathi kweentlanga, Yehova,Negama lakho ndiliculele uncuthu lwengoma.
50  Wenzela ukumkani wakhe izenzo ezikhulu zosindisoYaye umenzela ububele bothando othanjisiweyo wakhe,UDavide nembewu yakhe kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo.
115  Akukho nto iyeyethu, Yehova, akukho nto iyeyethu,Kodwa nika igama lakho uzukoNgokobubele bakho bothando, ngokwenyaniso yakho.
2  Kutheni na ukuba iintlanga zithi:“Uphi na, ke, uThixo wabo?”
3  Kodwa uThixo wethu usemazulwini;Yonk’ into ayoliswa kukuyenza uyenzile.
4  Izithixo zabo ziyisilivere negolide,Umsebenzi wezandla zomntu wasemhlabeni.
5  Zinomlomo, kodwa azithethi;Zinamehlo, kodwa aziboni;
6  Zineendlebe, kodwa aziva.Zinempumlo, kodwa azisezeli.
7  Zinezandla, kodwa aziphathi.Zineenyawo, kodwa azihambi;Azivakalisi sandi ngomqala wazo.
8  Abo bazenzayo baya kuba njengazo kanye,Bonke abo bakholosa ngazo.
9  Owu Sirayeli, kholosa ngoYehova;Uluncedo lwabo nekhaka labo.
10  Nawe ndlu ka-Aron, kholosa ngoYehova;Uluncedo lwabo nekhakha labo.
11  Nina enoyika uYehova, kholosani ngoYehova;Uluncedo lwabo nekhaka labo.
12  UYehova usikhumbule; uya kusisikelela,Uya kuyisikelela indlu kaSirayeli,Uya kuyisikelela indlu ka-Aron.
13  Uya kubasikelela abo boyika uYehova,Abancinane kwakunye nabakhulu.
14  UYehova uya kunandisela nina,Nina noonyana benu.
15  Nina ningabasikelelweyo nguYehova,UMenzi wezulu nomhlaba.
16  Wona ke amazulu, ngamazulu kaYehova,Kodwa umhlaba uwunike oonyana babantu.
17  Abafileyo abamdumisi uYa,Bengenjinjalo nabo behlayo baye kwelokuthula.
18  Kodwa thina siya kumbonga uYaUkususela ngoku kuse phambili nokusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.Dumisani uYa!
17  Owu Yehova, kuve oko kububulungisa; nikela ingqalelo kwisikhalo sam sokubongoza;Wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam ongengowemilebe enenkohliso.
2  Ngamana umgwebo wam ungaphuma phambi kwakho;Ngamana amehlo akho angabona okuthe tye.
3  Uyigocagocile intliziyo yam, uyivelele ebusuku,Undisulungekisile; uya kufumanisa ukuba andicebanga nto.Umlomo wam awuyi kunxaxha.
4  Ngokuphathelele imisebenzi yabantu,Ngelizwi lemilebe yakho ndizilindile kwiindlela zomphangi.
5  Ukunyathela kwam makubambelele emkhondweni wakho,Amanyathelo am ngokuqinisekileyo angayi kushukunyiswa kuwo.
6  Mna ndiyakubiza, ngenxa yokuba uya kundiphendula, Thixo.Yithobele kum indlebe yakho. Live ilizwi lam.
7  Zenze zimangalise izenzo zakho zobubele obumangalisayo, Msindisi wabo bafuna indawo yokusabelaKwabo bavukelayo kwisandla sakho sasekunene.
8  Ndigcine njengokhozo lweliso lakho,Ngamana ungandifihla emthunzini wamaphiko akho,
9  Ngenxa yabangendawo abandiphangileyo.Iintshaba zomphefumlo wam zindivingcele.
10  Zithe fithi kukutyeba;Ngomlomo wazo zithethe ngekratshi;
11  Ngokubhekisele kumanyathelo ethu, ngoku zisingqongile;Amehlo azo ziwathambekisela emhlabeni.
12  Ufana nengonyama elangazelela ukuqwengaKwanengonyama entsha ehleli kwiindawo ezifihlakeleyo.
13  Phakama, Yehova; ujamelane naye ubuso ngobuso;Menze aqubude; wusindise umphefumlo wam kwabangendawo ngekrele lakho,
14  Kumadoda, ngesandla sakho, Yehova,Kumadoda ale nkqubo yezinto, asabelo sawo sikobu bomi,Nasisu sawo usizalisa ngobuncwane obufihliweyo,Anelisekileyo ngoonyanaNabekela abantwana bawo oko kushiyekileyo.
15  Ke mna, ngobulungisa ndiya kububona ubuso bakho;ndiya kwaneliswa xa ndivuka ukuze ndibone imbonakalo yakho.
106  Dumisani uYa!Bulelani kuYehova, kuba ulungile;Kuba ububele bakhe bothando bukho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
2  Ngubani na onokuthetha ngezenzo zamandla zikaYehova,Okanye onokuvakalisa yonke indumiso yakhe?
3  Banoyolo abo bagcina okusesikweni,Abenza ubulungisa lonke ixesha.
4  Ndikhumbule, Yehova, ngenkoliseko kubo abantu bakho.Ndinyamekele ngosindiso lwakho,
5  Ukuze ndibone ukulunga kwabanyuliweyo bakho,Ukuze ndibe nemihlali ngokuba nemihlali kohlanga lwakho,Ukuze ndiqhayise ngelifa lakho.
6  Sonile kanye ngokufana nookhokho bethu;Senze ububi; senze ngokungendawo.
7  Bona ke ookhokho bethu eYiputa,Abazange babonakalise nakuphi na ukuyiqiqa imisebenzi yakho emangalisayo.Abazange babukhumbule ububele bakho bothando obuninzi,Kodwa baziphatha ngemvukelo elwandle, kuLwandle Olubomvu.
8  Wabasindisa ngenxa yegama lakhe,Ukuze azise amandla akhe.
9  Ngako oko walukhalimela uLwandle Olubomvu, loma;Kwaye wabahambisa emanzini anzongonzongo kwanga kusentlango;
10  Waza ngoko wabasindisa esandleni salowo wayebathiyileWabahlangula esandleni sotshaba.
11  Amanzi azigubungela iintshaba zabo;Akuzange kusale namnye kuzo.
12  Ngoko bakholwa lilizwi lakhe;Bayivuma indumiso yakhe.
13  Bayilibala ngokukhawuleza imisebenzi yakhe;Abazange balindele icebo lakhe.
14  Kodwa babonisa umnqweno wabo wokuzingca entlangoBaza bamcikida uThixo enkqantosini.
15  Wabanika isicelo saboWaza wathumela isifo esiqhenqethayo emphefumlweni wabo.
16  Bammonela uMoses enkampini,NoAron ongcwele kaYehova.
17  Wandula ke umhlaba wavuleka waza waginya uDatan,Waza waligubungela ibandla lika-Abhiram.
18  Nomlilo watshisa phakathi kwendibano yabo;Ilangatye labaqwenga abo bangendawo.
19  Ngapha koko, benza ithole eHorebheBaza baqubuda kuwo umfanekiso otyhidiweyo,
20  Kangangokuba balwananisa uzuko lwamNgembonakaliso yenkunzi yenkomo, into edla utyani.
21  Bamlibala uThixo uMsindisi wabo,UMenzi wezinto ezinkulu eYiputa,
22  Imisebenzi emangalisayo kwilizwe lakwaHam,Izinto ezoyikekayo kuLwandle Olubomvu.
23  Wayesele eza kuthi mababhujiswe,Ukuba kwakungekho ngenxa kaMoses onyuliweyo wakhe,Owema ethubeni phambi kwakhe,Ukuze ubuye umsindo wakhe, angabonakalisi.
24  Balicekisa ilizwe elinqwenelekayo;Babengakholwa lilizwi lakhe.
25  Bamana bembombozela ezintenteni zabo;Abazange baliphulaphule ilizwi likaYehova.
26  Wasiphakamisa ke isandla sakhe efunga ngabo,Wathi uya kubawisa entlango,
27  Wayeya kuyiwisa inzala yabo phakathi kweentlanga,Wayeya kubachithachitha emazweni.
28  Bazibandakanya noBhahali wasePehoreBadla imibingelelo yabafileyo.
29  Njengoko babecaphukisa ngezenzo zabo,Ngoku bafikelwa sisibetho phakathi kwabo.
30  Xa uFinehasi wemayo waza wangenelela,Ngoko isibetho samiswa.
31  Kwabalelwa kuye njengobulungisa okoKwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
32  Ngokubhekele phaya, bacaphukisa emanzini aseMeribha,Kangangokuba uMoses wahlelwa bububi ngenxa yabo.
33  Kuba bawenza krakra umoya wakheWaza wathetha ngobutyhuthu-tyhuthu ngemilebe yakhe.
34  Abazange bazibhubhise izizwana,Njengoko uYehova wayetshilo kubo.
35  Baxubana neentlangaYaye bafunda imisebenzi yazo.
36  Bakhonza izithixo zazo,Zona ke ezi zaba ngumgibe kubo.
37  Babebingelela ngoonyana baboNangeentombi zabo kwiidemon.
38  Ngoko baphalaza igazi elimsulwa,Igazi loonyana babo neentombi zabo,Ababingelela ngazo kwizithixo zakwaKanan;Nelizwe langcoliswa luphalazo-gazi.
39  Baba ngabangahlambulukanga ngemisebenzi yaboBaba neentlobano zokuziphatha okubi ngezenzo zabo.
40  Wavutha umsindo kaYehova nxamnye nabantu bakhe,Walicekisa ilifa lakhe.
41  Ngokuphindaphindiweyo wabanikela esandleni seentlanga,Ukuze abo babathiyayo babalawule,
42  Nokuze iintshaba zabo zibacinezele,Nokuze bathotyelwe phantsi kwesandla sazo.
43  Izihlandlo ezininzi wayebahlangula,Kodwa bona babeziphatha ngemvukelo kwikhondo labo lokungathobeli,Babehliswa ngenxa yesiphoso sabo.
44  Wayekubona ukubandezeleka kwaboAkuva ukukhala kwabo bembongoza.

50  Lowo Ungokobuthixo, uThixo, uYehova, uthethile,Yaye ubiza umhlaba,Kususela ekuphumeni kwelanga de litshone.
2  EseZiyon, ubuhle obugqibeleleyo, uThixo uqaqambile.
3  UThixo wethu uya kuza yaye akanakuthi cwaka.Phambi kwakhe umlilo uyaqwenga,Yaye ujikelezwe sisaqhwithi esigqithiseleyo.
4  Ubiza emazulwini phezulu nasemhlabeniUkuze aphumeze umgwebo kubantu bakhe:
5  “Hlanganisela kum abanyanisekileyo bam,Abo benza umnqophiso wam ngombingelelo.”
6  Yaye amazulu axela ubulungisa bakhe,Kuba uThixo nguMgwebi. Seʹlah.
7  “Phulaphulani, bantu bam, ndiya kuthetha,Owu Sirayeli, ndiya kunikela ubungqina nxamnye nawe.NdinguThixo, uThixo wakho.
8  Andikohlwayi ngokuphathelele imibingelelo yakho,Nangokuphathelele iminikelo yakho etshiswa kuphele ephambi kwam ngamaxesha onke.
9  Andiyi kukhupha inkunzi yenkomo endlwini yakho,Nasebuhlanti bakho iinkunzi zeebhokhwe.
10  Kuba zezam zonke izilwanyana zasendle ezisehlathini,Amarhamncwa asezintabeni eziliwaka.
11  Ndizazi kakuhle zonke izidalwa ezinamaphiko ezisezintabeni,Nezilwanyana ezininzi ezisendle zikum.
12  Ukuba bendilambile, bendingayi kuxelela wena;Kuba ngowam umhlaba onemveliso nokuzala kwawo.
13  Ngaba ndiya kudla inyama yeenkunzi zeenkomo ezinamandla,Negazi leenkunzi zeebhokhwe ngaba ndiya kulisela?
14  Nikelani imibulelo njengedini lenu kuThixo,Nize nizifezekise kOyena Uphakamileyo izibhambathiso zenu;
15  Nindibize ngemini yokubandezeleka.Ndiya kunihlangula, yaye niya kundizukisa.”
16  Kodwa kulowo ungendawo uThixo kuya kufuneka athi:“Liliphi na ilungelo onalo lokubhengeza imimiselo yam,Nokuba uthwale umnqophiso wam emlonyeni wakho?
17  Kaloku, wena—uluthiyile uqeqesho,Namazwi am uqhubeka uwaphosela emva kwakho.
18  Xa sukuba ubona isela, ubukholiswa lilo;Yaye usabelana nabakrexezi.
19  Umlomo wakho uwuyekele kokubi,Nolwimi lwakho ulugcina lunamathele kwinkohliso.
20  Uyahlala uthethe kakubi ngomzalwana wakho,Nesiphoso sonyana kanyoko uyasidiza.
21  Ezi zinto uzenzile, ndaza ndathi cwaka.Ubucinga ukuba ndiya kuba njengawe ngokuqinisekileyo.Ndiza kukohlwaya, yaye izinto ndiya kuzimisa ngolungelelwano phambi kwamehlo akho.
22  Khanincede, niqonde oku nina bamlibalayo uThixo,Hleze ndiniqwenge kungabikho unihlangulayo.
23  Lowo unikela umbulelo njengombingelelo wakhe nguye ondizukisayo;Ke yena lowo ogcina indlela emiselweyo,Ndiya kumbangela alubone usindiso lukaThixo.”
129  “Sekulithuba elide ngokwaneleyo bebonakalisa ubutshaba kum ukususela ebutsheni bam,”Makatsho ke uSirayeli ngoku,
2  “Sekulithuba elide ngokwaneleyo bebonakalisa ubutshaba kum ukususela ebutsheni bam;Kanti abandoyisanga.
3  Abalimi balime emhlana kum;Bayandisile imijelo yabo.”
4  UYehova lilungisa.Uziqhawule iintsontelo zabo bangendawo.
5  Baya kuba neentloni baze babuye umva,Bonke abo bayithiyileyo iZiyon.
6  Baya kuba njengengca eluhlaza eluphahleni,Eye yoma ngaphambi kokuba inyothulwe,
7  Ovunayo akazalisi sandla sakhe ngayo,Naye nabani obopha izithungu akazalisi sifuba sakhe.
8  Nabo badlulayo abatshongo ukuthi:“Intsikelelo kaYehova mayibe phezu kwenu.Sinisikelele egameni likaYehova.”
109  Owu Thixo wendumiso yam, musa ukuthi cwaka.
2  Kuba bandivulele umlomo wongendawo nomlomo wenkohliso.Bathethe ngam ngolwimi lobuxoki;
3  Bandingqonge ngamazwi entiyo,Yaye balwa nam ngaphandle kwesizathu.
4  Ngenxa yothando lwam bayandichasa;Kodwa mna ndiyathandaza.
5  Endaweni yokulungileyo benza okubi kumNentiyo endaweni yothando lwam.
6  Misela ongendawo phezu kwakhe,Yaye ngamana umchasi angaqhubeka emi ngasesandleni sakhe sasekunene.
7  Ekugwetyweni kwakhe, makaphume enjengongendawo;Nomthandazo lowo wakhe mawube sisono.
8  Imihla yakhe mayibe mbalwa;Isigxina sakhe sobuveleli masithatyathwe ngomnye.
9  Oonyana bakhe mababe ngamakhwenkwe angenayiseNomfazi wakhe abe ngumhlolokazi.
10  Nakanjani na oonyana bakhe mababhadu-bhadule;Yaye bamele bangqibe,Kwaye bamele bafune ukutya bekwiindawo zabo eziphanzileyo.
11  Umbolekisi obiza inzuzo enkulu makakubekele izibatha konke anako,Nabasemzini mabayiphange imveliso yokuxhamleka kwakhe.
12  Makangabi naye omolulela ububele bothando,Angabi naye nobabala amakhwenkwe akhe angenayise.
13  Izizukulwana zakhe mazibe zezokunqunyulwa.Lisuswe igama lazo kwisizukulwana esilandelayo.
14  UYehova makasikhumbule isiphoso sookhokho bakhe,Nesono sikanina—ngamana asinakususwa.
15  Mababe phambi koYehova rhoqo;Yaya ngamana angakunqumla ukukhunjulwa kwabo emhlabeni;
16  Ngenxa yokuba engakukhumbulanga ukwenza ububele bothando,Kodwa wasukela umntu oxhwalekileyo nolihlwempuNalowo unentliziyo edakumbileyo, ukuba ambulale.
17  Wathanda isiqalekiso, kangangokuba samfikela;Akazange ayoliswe yintsikelelo,Kangangokuba yaba kude kuye;
18  Wambeswa ngesiqalekiso njengesambatho sakhe.Ngoko sangena phakathi kwakhe njengamanziNanjengeoli emathanjeni akhe.
19  Ngamana singanjengesambatho kuye eso azisongela ngasoNanjengombhinqo ahlala ewubhinqile rhoqo.
20  Nguwo lo umvuzo ovela kuYehova walowo undichasayoNowabo bathetha ububi ngomphefumlo wam.
21  Kodwa unguYehova iNkosi enguMongami.Qhubana nam ngenxa yegama lakho.Ngenxa yokuba ububele bakho bothando bulungile, ndihlangule.
22  Kuba ndixhwalekile yaye ndilihlwempu,Nentliziyo yam ihlatyiwe ngaphakathi kwam.
23  Njengethunzi xa linabayo, ndiyemka;Ndivuthululwe njengenkumbi.
24  Amadolo am ayagexa ngenxa yokuzila ukutya,Nenyama yam ibhityile, kungekho nayiphi na ioli.
25  Yaye kubo ndiye ndaba yinto esisingcikivo.Bayandibona—bahlunguzele intloko.
26  Ndincede, Yehova Thixo wam;Ndisindise ngokobubele bakho bothando.
27  Ngamana bangazi ukuba sisandla sakho esi;Ukuba wena, Yehova, ukwenzile oku.
28  Bona mabavakalise isiqalekiso,Kodwa wena ngamana ungavakalisa intsikelelo.Bavukile, kodwa mababe neentloni,Nomkhonzi wakho abe nemihlali.
29  Abo bandichasayo mabambeswe ngokuthotywa,Kwaye mabazisongele ngehlazo labo kanye njengokungathi kungesambatho esingenamikhono.
30  Ndiya kumbonga kakhulu uYehova ngomlomo wam,Naphakathi kwabantu abaninzi ndiya kumdumisa.
31  Kuba uya kuma ngasesandleni sokunene solihlwempu,Ukuze amsindise kwabo bagweba umphefumlo wakhe.
143  Owu Yehova, yiva umthandazo wam;Sibekele indlebe isibongozo sam.Ekuthembekeni kwakho ndiphendule ngobulungisa bakho.
2  Musa ukumsa ematyaleni umkhonzi wakho;Kuba phambi kwakho akukho bani uphilayo unokuba lilungisa.
3  Kuba utshaba lusukele umphefumlo wam;Lubutyumzele emhlabeni ubomi bam.Lundihlalise ezindaweni ezimnyama njengabo bafileyo ixesha elingenammiselo.
4  Nomoya wam utyhafile ngaphakathi kwam;Phakathi kwam intliziyo yam iba ndindisholo.
5  Ndikhumbule imihla yakudala;Ndicamngce ngawo wonke umsebenzi wakho;Ngokuzithandela ndihleli ndizixhalabisa ngomsebenzi wezandla zakho.
6  Ndolulele izandla zam kuwe;Umphefumlo wam unjengelizwe elibharhileyo kuwe. Seʹlah.
7  Khawuleza, undiphendule, Yehova.Umoya wam uphelile.Musa ukubufihla ubuso bakho kum,Okanye kungenjalo ndimele ndifane nabo behla baye emhadini.
8  Kusasa ndivise ububele bakho bothando,Kuba ndikholose ngawe.Ndazise indlela endifanele ndihambe ngayo,Kuba ndiwuphakamisele kuwe umphefumlo wam.
9  Ndihlangule ezintshabeni zam, Yehova.Ndizimele ngawe.
10  Ndifundise ukwenza ukuthanda kwakho,Kuba wena unguThixo wam.Umoya wakho ulungile;Ngamana ungandikhokelela elizweni labathe tye.
11  Ngenxa yegama lakho, Yehova, ngamana ungandigcina ndiphila.Ngobulungisa bakho ngamana ungawukhupha umphefumlo wam ekubandezelekeni.
12  Ngobubele bakho bothando ngamana ungazithulisa iintshaba zam;Kwaye umele ubatshabalalise bonke abo babonakalisa ubutshaba emphefumlweni wam,Kuba ndingumkhonzi wakho.
117  Dumisani uYehova, nonke nina zintlanga;Mncomeni, nonke nina zizwana.
2  Kuba bungqineke bunamandla kuthi ububele bakhe bothando;Nenyaniso kaYehova ikho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.Dumisani uYa!
110  Utsho uYehova eNkosini yam ukuthi:“Hlala ngasekunene kwamNdide ndizibeke iintshaba zakho njengesitulo seenyawo zakho.”
2  Intonga yamandla akho uYehova uya kuyithumela iphuma eZiyon, esithi:“Hamba usoyisa phakathi kweentshaba zakho.”
3  Abantu bakho baya kuzinikela ngokuvumayo ngemini yomkhosi wakho wamajoni.Ngobungangamsha bobungcwele, ekuphumeni kwesifingo,Uneqela lakho labantu abaselula kanye njengamathontsi ombethe.
4  UYehova ufungile (yaye akayi kuzisola), wathi:“Ungumbingeleli ukusa kwixesha elingenammiseloNgokohlobo lukaMelkitsedeki!”
5  UYehova ngasekunene kwakhoNgokuqinisekileyo uya kuqhekeza ookumkani ngemini yomsindo wakhe.
6  Uya kuphumeza umgwebo phakathi kweentlanga;Uya kubangela ukuba kuzale izidumbu.Ngokuqinisekileyo uya kumqhekeza lowo uyintloko kwilizwe elikhulu.
7  Uya kusela entlanjeni ngasendleleni.Kungenxa yoko le nto eya kuyiphakamisela phezulu intloko yakhe.
122  Ndaba nemihlali bakuthi kum:“Masiye endlwini kaYehova.”
2  Iinyawo zethu zemaNgaphakathi kwamasango akho, Yerusalem.
3  IYerusalem yakhiwe njengesixekoEsihlanganiswe ndawonye ngobunye,
4  Ezinyuke zaya kuso izizwe,Izizwe zikaYa,Njengesikhumbuzo kuSirayeliUkuba abulele egameni likaYehova.
5  Kuba apho bekuhleli iitrone zokugweba,Iitrone zendlu kaDavide.
6  Celelani iYerusalem uxolo.Abo bakuthandayo, sixekondini, abayi kuba naxhala.
7  Ngamana lungaqhubeka uxolo emseleni wakho,Ukungabi naxhala ngaphakathi kweenqaba zakho zokuhlala.
8  Ke kaloku ndiza kuthetha ngenxa yabazalwana bam namaqabane am ndithi:“Ngamana kungakho uxolo phakathi kwakho.”
9  Ngenxa yendlu kaYehova uThixo wethuNdiza kuqhubeka ndikufunela okulungileyo.
9  Ndiya kukubonga, Yehova, ngayo yonke intliziyo yam;Ndiya kuyivakalisa yonke imisebenzi yakho emangalisayo.
2  Ndiya kuba nemihlali ndize ndigcobe ngawe,Ndiya kulivumela uncuthu lwengoma igama lakho, wena ungOyena Uphakamileyo.
3  Xa intshaba zam zijika,Ziya kukhubeka zize zitshabalale phambi kwakho.
4  Kuba uwuphumezile umgwebo wam nebango lam;Uhleli etroneni ugweba ngobulungisa.
5  Ukhalimele iintlanga, umtshabalalisile ongendawo.Igama lazo ulisuse ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, nangonaphakade.
6  Owu lutshaba, iziphanziso zakho zifikelele esiphelweni sazo esingunaphakade,Nezixeko ozincothuleyo.Nokukhankanywa kwazo kuya kutshabalala.
7  Ke yena uYehova, uya kuhlala ixesha elingenammiselo,Amisele ngokuqinileyo itrone yakhe ukuze agwebe.
8  Kwaye yena uya kugweba ilizwe elinemveliso ngobulungisa;Uya kuchophela amatyala amaqela eentlanga ngokuthe tye.
9  UYehova uya kuba yindawo ephakamileyo enqabisekileyo kuye nabani na otyunyuziweyo,Indawo ephakamileyo enqabisekileyo ngamaxesha okubandezeleka.
10  Abo balaziyo igama lakho baya kukholosa ngawe,Kuba ngokuqinisekileyo akuyi kubashiya abo bakukhangelayo, Yehova.
11  Mculeleni uncuthu lwengoma, uYehova, ohlala eZiyon;Zixeleni phakathi kwezizwana izenzo zakhe.
12  Kuba, xa ekhangela uphalazo-gazi, ngokuqinisekileyo uya kubakhumbula abo;Ngokuqinisekileyo akayi kusilibala isikhalo sabaxhwalekileyo.
13  Ndibabale, Yehova; yibone inkxwaleko yam ngenxa yabo bandithiyileyo,Owu wena undiphakamisayo emasangweni okufa,
14  Ukuze ndizivakalise zonke izenzo zakho zokudunyiswaEmasangweni entombi yeZiyon,Ukuze ndivuye ngosindiso lwakho.
15  Iintlanga zitshone emhadini eziwenzileyo;Unyawo lwazo lubanjiswe ngumnatha ebeziwufihlile.
16  UYehova waziwa ngomgwebo awuphumezileyo.Ngomsebenzi wezandla zakhe ongendawo urhintyelwe.Higayoni. Seʹlah.
17  Abantu abangendawo baya kubuyela eShiyol,Kwanazo zonke iintlanga ezimlibalayo uThixo.
18  Kuba lowo ulihlwempu akayi kusoloko elityalwa,Nethemba lalowo ululamileyo aliyi kuze litshabalale ngonaphakade.
19  Vuka, Yehova! Umntu ofayo makangangqineki ongamile kuwe ngamandla.Mazigwetywe iintlanga phambi kobuso bakho.
20  Beka uloyiko kuzo, Yehova,Ukuze iintlanga zazi ukuba zingabantu abafayo. Seʹlah.
28  Ndiqhubeka ndibiza wena, Yehova.Owu Liwa lam, musa ukuba sisithulu kum,Ukuze ungathi cwaka kumUkuze kungafuneki ndifane nabo bahlela emhadini.
2  Live ilizwi lokubongoza kwam xa ndikhalela uncedo kuwe,Xa ndiphakamisela izandla zam kwelona gumbi lingaphakathi lendawo yakho engcwele.
3  Musa ukunditsala kunye nabantu abangendawo nabo baqhelisela oko kwenzakalisayo,Abo bathetha uxolo namaqabane abo kodwa ezintliziyweni zabo kukho okubi.
4  Banike ngokokwenza kwaboNangokobubi boqheliselo lwabo.Banike ngokomsebenzi wezandla zabo.Babuyisele ngokokwenza kwabo.
5  Kuba abayihloneli imisebenzi kaYehova,Nemisebenzi yezandla zakhe.Uya kubachitha angabakhi.
6  Makabongwe uYehova kuba elivile ilizwi lezibongozo zam.
7  UYehova ungamandla am nekhaka lam.Intliziyo yam ikholose ngaye,Yaye ndincediwe, ukuze intliziyo yam igcobe,Yaye ndiya kumbonga ngengoma yam.
8  UYehova ungamandla kubantu bakhe,Kwaye uligwiba losindiso oluzukileyo labathanjiswa bakhe.
9  Basindise abantu bakho, ulisikelele ilifa lakho;Ubaluse uze ubathwale ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
27  UYehova kukukhanya kwam nosindiso lwam.Ndiya koyika bani na?UYehova ligwiba lobomi bam.Ndiya kunkwantyiswa ngubani na?
2  Xa abenzi bobubi basondela kum ukuze badle inyama yam bayigqibe,Beziintshaba zam ngokobuqu,Bakhubeka bawa.
3  Nangona kuya kumiswa inkampu nxamnye nam,Intliziyo yam ayiyi koyika.Nangona kuya kuvuka imfazwe nxamnye nam,Kwanangoko ndiya kukholosa.
4  Inye into endiyicelileyo kuYehova—Ndiya kufuna yona,Ukuba ndihlale endlwini kaYehova yonke imihla yobomi bam,Ndibone ukuthandeka kukaYehovaNdize ndikhangele ngoxabiso etempileni yakhe.
5  Kuba uya kundifihla endaweni yakhe esithakeleyo ngomhla wentlekele;Uya kundifihla endaweni efihlakeleyo yentente yakhe;Uya kundibeka phezulu eliweni.
6  Ngoku intloko yam iya kuphakama ngaphezu kweentshaba zam ezindijikelezileyo;Yaye ndiya kubingelela ententeni yakhe imibingelelo yemikhwazo yovuyo;Ndiya kuvuma ndize ndiculele uYehova uncuthu lwengoma.
7  Ndive, Yehova, xa ndikubiza ngelizwi lam,Undibabale uze undiphendule.
8  Ithe intliziyo yam ngawe: “Funani ubuso bam.”Ubuso bakho, Yehova, ndiya kubufuna.
9  Musa ukubufihla ubuso bakho kum.Musa ukumjika umkhonzi wakho ngomsindo.Umele ube luncedo lwam.Musa ukundilahla yaye musa ukundishiya, Thixo wam wosindiso.
10  Nokuba ubawo noma bangandishiya,Ke yena uYehova uya kundithabatha.
11  Ndiyalele indlela yakho, Yehova,Undikhokele kumendo wokuthe tye ngenxa yeentshaba zam.
12  Ungandinikeli emphefumlweni weentshaba zam;Kuba ndiphakanyelwe ngamangqina obuxoki,Nangulowo utsawula ugonyamelo.
13  Ukuba bendingabanga nokholo ekuboneni ukulunga kukaYehova elizweni labo baphilileyo—!
14  Thembela ngoYehova; yiba nesibindi uze uvumele intliziyo yakho yomelele.Ewe, thembela ngoYehova.
63  Owu Thixo, unguThixo wam, ndihlala ndikufuna.Umphefumlo wam uyakunxanelwa.Inyama yam ityhafile kukulangazelela wenaEmhlabeni owomileyo nobharhileyo, ekungekho manzi kuwo.
2  Ngaloo ndlela ndikubonile endaweni engcwele,Ekuboneni amandla akho nozuko lwakho.
3  Ngenxa yokuba ububele bakho bothando bulunge ngakumbi kunobomi,Imilebe yam iya kukuncoma.
4  Ngaloo ndlela ndiya kukubonga ebudeni bexesha lokudla kwam ubomi;Igama lakho ndiya kuliphakamisela iintende zam.
5  Njengoko umphefumlo wam usaneliswa yeyona nxalenye ilungileyo, kwanakukutyeba,Nangemilebe ephuma intswahla yemivuyo umlomo wam unikela indumiso.
6  Xa ndikukhumbule esingqengqelweni sam,Ebudeni bemilindo yasebusuku ndicamngca ngawe.
7  Kuba ungqineke uluncedo kum,Yaye emthunzini wamaphiko akho ndimemelela ngovuyo.
8  Umphefumlo wam ukulandele ngokusondeleyo;Isandla sakho sasekunene sihlala sindibambe nkqi.
9  Abo ke bahlala befuna ukonakalisa umphefumlo wam,Baya kufika kwezona ndawo zisezantsi zomhlaba.
10  Baya kunikelwa emandleni ekrele;Baya kuba sisahlulo seempungutye.
11  Ukumkani uya kuba nemihlali ngoThixo.Wonke ubani ofunga ngaye uya kuqhayisa,Kuba umlomo wabo bathetha ubuxoki uya kuvingcwa.
7  Owu Yehova Thixo wam, ndisabela kuwe.Ndisindise kubo bonke abo banditshutshisayo uze undihlangule,
2  Ukuze kungabikho namnye uwuqwengayo umphefumlo wam njengoko isenza ingonyama,Andixhwile xa kungekho mhlanguli.
3  Owu Yehova Thixo wam, ukuba ndikwenzile oku,Ukuba kukho okungekho sikweni ezandleni zam,
4  Ukuba lowo undivuzayo ndimbuyekeze ngokubi,Okanye ukuba ndiphange nabani na obonisa ubutshaba kum andaphumelela,
5  Utshaba maluwusukele umphefumlo wamUze uluvumele lubufumane luze lubunyathelele emhlabeni ubomi bamLubangele uzuko lwam luhlale eluthulini. Seʹlah.
6  Sukuma, Yehova, emsindweni wakho;Ziphakamise ekudubulekeni kokuvutha komsindo wabo babonisa ubutshaba kum,Vuka ngenxa yam, ekubeni unikele umyalelo womgwebo.
7  Mayikungqonge indibano yamaqela eentlanga,Uze nxamnye nayo ubuye uphezulu.
8  UYehova uya kuwisa isigwebo kwizizwana.Ndigwebe, Yehova, ngokobulungisa bamNangokwengqibelelo ekum.
9  Mabuphele ububi babangendawo,Uze ummisele lowo ulilungisa;Yaye uThixo njengolilungisa uvavanya intliziyo nezintso.
10  Ikhaka lam likuThixo, uMsindisi wabo bathe tye entliziyweni.
11  UThixo nguMgwebi olilungisa,Yaye uThixo uqalekisa yonke imihla.
12  Ukuba nabani na akayi kubuya, ikrele Lakhe uya kulilola,Isaphetha sakhe uya kusigoba ngokuqinisekileyo, aze asilungiselele ukutola.
13  Yena umele azilungiselele izixhobo zokufa;Iintolo zakhe uya kuzenza zidangazele.
14  Khangela! Kukho lowo umithi okwenzakalisayo,Yaye ukhawule inkathazo kwaye umele azale ubuxoki.
15  Ugrumbe umhadi, waza wawumba;Kodwa uya kuwela emngxunyeni awenzileyo.
16  Inkathazo yakhe iya kubuyela entlokweni yakhe,Yaye ugonyamelo lwakhe luya kuhlela phezu kokakayi lwentloko yakhe.
17  Ndiya kumbonga uYehova ngenxa yobulungisa bakhe,Yaye ndiya kulivumela uncuthu lwengoma igama likaYehova Oyena Uphakamileyo.
55  Owu Thixo wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam;Ungazifihli kwisicelo sam sobabalo.
2  Nikela ingqalelo kum undiphendule.Ndigungqagungqiswa kukuxhalaba kwam,Ekuphela kwento endinokuyenza kukubonisa ukuphazamiseka,
3  Ngenxa yelizwi lotshaba, ngenxa yengcinezelo yalowo ungendawo.Kuba baqhubeka bendiphosela okwenzakalisayo,Yaye ngomsindo bandifukamela inzondo.
4  Intliziyo yam isezintlungwini ezigqithiseleyo kum,Nokothuka ngenxa yokufa kuphezu kwam.
5  Ukoyika, ewe, ukungcangcazela kundingene,Nokutyhwatyhwa kundigubungele.
6  Yaye ndihlala ndisithi: “Owu akwaba bendinamaphiko njengehobe!Bendiya kuphaphazela ndimke ndize ndihlale.
7  Khangela! bendiya kusaba ndiye kude;Bendiya kuhlala entlango.—Seʹlah—
8  Bendiya kungxama ukuya kwindawo yam yokubalekelaNdiwubaleke umoya obhudlayo, nesivuthuvuthu.”
9  Badide, Yehova, yahlula ulwimi lwabo,Kuba ndibone ugonyamelo nokuphikisana esixekweni.
10  Imini nobusuku bayasijikeleza ezindongeni zaso;Nokwenzakalisayo nenkathazo zikuso.
11  Ishwangusha likuso;Kwaye ingcinezelo nenkohliso azimki endaweni yaso yembutho.
12  Kuba asilotshaba olundingcikivayo;Ngapha koko bendinokukunyamezela.Yayingenguye ondithiye kakhulu owazigwagwisa nxamnye nam;Ngapha koko bendinokuzifihla kuye.
13  Kodwa yayinguwe, umntu ofayo umlingane owayelingana nam,Lowo wazana nam nendimqhelileyo,
14  Ngenxa yokuba besiqhele ukunandipha okumnandi ngokusondeleleneyo ndawonye;Siye endlwini kaThixo sihamba singumndilili.
15  Isiphanziso masibe phezu kwabo!Mabehlele eShiyol bephila;Kuba ebudeni bokuba ngabaphambukeli kwabo izinto ezimbi zazingaphakathi kubo.
16  Mna ke, ndiya kumemeza kuThixo;Yaye uYehova uya kundisindisa.
17  Ngokuhlwa nakusasa nasemini enkulu ndibonakalisa ukuxhalaba yaye ndiyadumzela,Ibe uyaliva ilizwi lam.
18  Ngokuqinisekileyo uya kundikhulula ekulweni nxamnye nam aze abeke umphefumlo wam eluxolweni,Kuba bayinkitha abanxamnye nam.
19  UThixo uya kubeva aze abaphendule,Yena kanye Lowo ohleli ebekwe etroneni njengakwixesha elidlulileyo—Seʹlah—Abo kungekho kutshintsha kuboNabangamoyikanga uThixo.
20  Wolule izandla zakhe nxamnye nabo baseluxolweni naye;Uwuhlambele umnqophiso wakhe.
21  Agude ngakumbi kunebhotolo amazwi omlomo wakhe,Kodwa intliziyo yakhe ityekele ekulweni.Amazwi akhe athambe ngakumbi kuneoli,Kodwa angamakrele arholiweyo.
22  Umthwalo wakho wulahlele kuYehova,Yaye yena wokuxhasa.Akayi kuliyekela ilungisa lishukunyiswe.
23  Kodwa wena ke, Thixo, uya kubehlisela kowona mhadi usezantsi.Ke abantu abanetyala legazi nabanenkohliso, abayi kuphila nesiqingatha semihla yabo.Mna ke, ndiya kukholosa ngawe.
51  Ndibabale, Thixo, ngokobubele bakho obunothando.Ngokobuninzi beenceba zakho kususe ukunxaxha kwam.
2  Ndihlambe ngokucokisekileyo kwisiphoso sam,Undihlambulule nakwisono sam.
3  Kuba ukunxaxha kwam ndiyakwazi,Nesono sam siphambi kwam rhoqo.
4  Ndone kuwe, kuwe wedwa,Ndenze okubi emehlweni akho,Ukuze uzingqine ulilungisa xa uthetha,Ukuze ube msulwa xa ugweba.
5  Khangela! Ngenimba ndazalelwa esiphosweni,Yaye uma wandikhawulela esonweni.
6  Khangela! Uyayoliswa kukuba nenyaniso ngaphakathi;Yaye kumntu ofihlakeleyo undibangela ndibazi ngokupheleleyo ubulumko.
7  Ngamana ungandisulungekisa esonweni ngehisope, ukuze ndihlambuluke;Ngamana ungandihlamba, ukuze ndibe mhlophe ngakumbi kunekhephu.
8  Ngamana ungandibangela ndive imigcobo nemihlali,Ukuze amathambo owatyumzileyo avuye.
9  Bufihle ubuso bakho ezonweni zam,Uzisuse zonke iziphoso zam.
10  Dala ngaphakathi kum intliziyo esulungekileyo, Thixo,Uze ufake ngaphakathi kum umoya omtsha, oqinileyo.
11  Musa ukundilahla phambi kobuso bakho;Nomoya wakho oyingcwele musa ukuwususa kum.
12  Buyisela kum ukugcoba ngosindiso lwakho,Yaye ngamana ungandixhasa ngomoya ovumayo.
13  Abanxaxhi ndiya kubafundisa iindlela zakho,Ukuze aboni babuyele kuwe.
14  Ndihlangule ekubeni netyala legazi, Thixo onguTHIXO wosindiso lwam,Ukuze ulwimi lwam lubuxele ngovuyo ubulungisa bakho.
15  Owu Yehova, ngamana ungayivula le milebe yam,Ukuze umlomo wam uxele indumiso yakho.
16  Kuba akuyoliswa yimibingelelo—ukuba bekunjalo bendiya kuyinikela;Akukholiswa yiminikelo etshiswa kuphele.
17  Imibingelelo kuThixo ngumoya owaphukileyo;Intliziyo eyaphukileyo netyumkileyo, Thixo, akuyi kuyidela.
18  Ngenkoliseko qhubana kakuhle neZiyon;Ngamana ungazakha iindonga zeYerusalem.
19  Ngaloo ndlela uya kuyoliswa yimibingelelo yobulungisa,Yimibingelelo etshiswayo nomnikelo opheleleyo;Ngako oko kuya kunikelwa iinkunzi zeenkomo esibingelelweni sakho.
34  Ndiya kumbonga uYehova ngamaxesha onke;Indumiso yakhe iya kuba semlonyeni wam rhoqo.
2  Uya kuqhayisa ngoYehova umphefumlo wam;Abalulamileyo baya kuva babe nemihlali.
3  Menzeni mkhulu uYehova kunye nam,Masiliphakamise kunye igama lakhe.
4  Ndabuza kuYehova, waza wandiphendula,Yaye wandihlangula kwizinto ezindothusayo.
5  Bakhangela kuye baza bakhazimla,Yaye ubuso babo babungenakuba nazintloni.
6  Lo uxhwalekileyo wabiza, waza uYehova weva.Yaye wamsindisa kuko konke ukubandezeleka kwakhe.
7  Ingelosi kaYehova imisa inkampu macala onke kwabo bamoyikayo,Ize ibahlangule.
8  Ngcamlani nibone ukuba uYehova ulungile;Inoyolo indoda eyomeleleyo esabela kuye.
9  Moyikeni uYehova, nina bangcwele bakhe,Kuba abasweli abo bamoyikayo.
10  Iingonyama ezintsha ezinesingci zinokuncinane yaye zilambile;Kodwa abo bafuna uYehova, abayi kuswela nantoni na elungileyo.
11  Yizani, bonyana, ndiphulaphuleni;Ndiya kunifundisa ukoyika uYehova.
12  Ngubani na indoda eyoliswayo bubomi,Ethanda imihla eyaneleyo ukuze ibone ukulunga?
13  Lulondoloze ulwimi lwakho kokubi,Nemilebe yakho ekuthetheni inkohliso.
14  Suka kokubi, wenze okulungileyo;Funa ukufumana uxolo, ulusukele.
15  Amehlo kaYehova akumalungisa,Neendlebe zakhe zibhekiswe ekukhaleleni kwawo uncedo.
16  Ubuso bukaYehova bunxamnye nabo benza okubi,Ukuze akunqumle ukukhankanywa kwabo emhlabeni.
17  Badanduluka, waza uYehova wabeva,Yaye kuko konke ukubandezeleka kwabo wabahlangula.
18  UYehova usondele kwabo baphuke intliziyo;Yaye abo bamoya utyumkileyo uyabasindisa.
19  Zininzi iintlekele ezihlela olilungisa,Kodwa uYehova ulihlangula kuzo zonke.
20  Uyawalinda onke amathambo alowo;Akukho nalinye kuwo elaphulwayo.
21  Intlekele iya kumbulala lowo ungendawo;Nabo bamthiyileyo olilungisa baya kugqalwa njengabanetyala.
22  UYehova uyawukhulula umphefumlo wabakhonzi bakhe;Yaye akukho namnye kwabo basabela kuye oya kugqalwa enetyala.
89  Ububele bothando bukaYehova ndiza kuvuma ngabo kude kube lixesha elingenammiselo.Kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana ndiya kwazisa ukuthembeka kwakho ngomlomo wam.
2  Kuba ndithe: “Ububele bothando buya kwakhiwa kude kube lixesha elingenammiselo;Wona ke amazulu, ukuthembeka kwakho ukumisela ngokuqinileyo kuwo.”
3  “Ndenze umnqophiso nonyuliweyo wam;Ndifungile kuDavide umkhonzi wam,
4  ‘Ndiya kuyimisela ngokuqinileyo imbewu yakho kude kube lixesha elingenammiselo,Yaye ndiza kuyakha itrone yakho ukusa kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.’” Seʹlah.
5  Amazulu aya kubonga isenzo sakho esimangalisayo, Yehova,Ewe, ukuthembeka kwakho ebandleni labangcwele.
6  Kuba ngubani na esibhakabhakeni onokuthelekiswa noYehova?Ngubani na onokufana noYehova phakathi koonyana bakaThixo?
7  UThixo makoyikwe phakathi kweqela lamakholwane abangcwele;Uzukile yaye uyoyikeka kubo bonke abo bamjikelezileyo.
8  Owu Yehova Thixo wemikhosi,Ngubani na onamandla njengawe, Ya?Nokuthembeka kwakho kukujikelezile.
9  Kulawula wena phezu kokukhukhumala kolwandle;Ekuwaphakamiseni kwalo amaza alo wena uyawazolisa.
10  Wena umtyumzile uRahabhi, wanjengobuleweyo.Uzichithachithile iintshaba zakho ngengalo yamandla akho.
11  Lelakho izulu, nomhlaba ikwangowakho;Ilizwe elinemveliso noko lizele kuko—wena waziseka ezo zinto.
12  Umntla nomzantsi—zadalwa nguwe;ITabhore neHermon—zimemelela ngovuyo egameni lakho.
13  Ingalo enamandla yeyakho,Isandla sakho somelele,Isandla sakho sasekunene siphakamile.
14  Ubulungisa nomgwebo yindawo emisiweyo yetrone yakho;Ububele bothando nenyaniso ziza phambi kobuso bakho.
15  Banoyolo abantu abayaziyo imikhwazo yovuyo.Bahamba ekukhanyeni kobuso bakho, Yehova.
16  Egameni lakho bayavuya imini yonkeBaphakame nangobulungisa bakho.
17  Kuba ububuhle bamandla abo;Nangenkoliseko yakho uphondo lwethu luphakamile.
18  Kuba ikhaka lethu lelikaYehova,Nokumkani wethu ngowaLowo Ungcwele kaSirayeli.
19  Ngelo xesha wathetha ngombono kwabo banyanisekileyo bakho,Wathi:“Ndibeke uncedo konamandla;Ndiphakamise onyuliweyo phakathi kwabantu.
20  Ndifumene uDavide umkhonzi wam;Ndimthambisile ngeoli yam engcwele,
21  Isandla sam esinaye siya kuqina,Nengalo yam iya kumomeleza.
22  Akukho lutshaba luya kubiza nto kuye,Naye nawuphi na unyana wentswela-bulungisa akayi kumxhwalekisa.
23  Yaye ndazityumza zaziingceba iintshaba zakhe phambi kwakhe,Nakwabo bamthiya kakhulu ndathumela izibetho.
24  Ukuthembeka kwam nobubele bam bothando bukunye naye,Kwaye egameni lam luphakamile uphondo lwakhe.
25  Isandla sakhe ndisibeke elwandleNasemilanjeni isandla sakhe sasekunene.
26  Yena undibiza ngokuthi, ‘UnguBawo,UThixo wam neLiwa lokusindiswa kwam.’
27  Kanjalo, mna ndiya kumbeka abe lizibulo,Oyena uphakamileyo kookumkani bomhlaba.
28  Ndiya kumgcinela ububele bam bothando ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo,Nomnqophiso wam uya kuthembeka kuye.
29  Ngokuqinisekileyo ndiya kuyimisa imbewu yakhe ngonaphakadeNetrone yakhe ibe njengemihla yezulu.
30  Ukuba oonyana bakhe bayawushiya umthetho wamBangahambi ngezigwebo zam,
31  Ukuba bayayihlambela imimiselo yamBangayigcini imiyalelo yam,
32  Ndimele ndiphethulele ingqalelo yam ekunxaxheni kwabo ngentongaNakwisiphoso sabo ngemivumbo.
33  Kodwa ububele bam bothando andiyi kubuqhawula kuye,Ndingayi kuxoka nangokubhekisele ekuthembekeni kwam.
34  Andiyi kuwuhlambela umnqopiso wam,Namazwi emilebe yam andiyi kuwatshintsha.
35  Ndakuba ndifungile ebungcweleni bam,Andiyi kumxokisa uDavide.
36  Imbewu yakhe iya kubakho de kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo,Netrone yakhe ibe njengelanga phambi kwam.
37  Iya kumiselwa ngokuqinileyo njengenyanga kangangexesha elingenammiselo,Nanjengengqina elithembekileyo esibhakabhakeni.” Seʹlah.
38  Kodwa wena—wena umlahlile yaye umcekisile;Wavutha umsindo wakho kothanjisiweyo wakho.
39  Uwucekisile umnqophiso womkhonzi wakho;Usihlambele isithsaba sakhe emhlabeni.
40  Uzidilizile zonke iintlanti zamatye;Uzenze amanxuwa iinqaba zakhe.
41  Bonke abo badlula ngendlela bamphangile;Uye waba lungcikivo kubamelwane bakhe.
42  Usiphakamisile isandla sasekunene sabo bamchasileyo;Uzenze zaba nemihlali zonke iintshaba zakhe.
43  Ngaphezu koko ikrele lakhe uliphatha njengotshaba,Wambangela ukuba angaqhubeli phambili edabini.
44  Uyiphelisile inkazimlo yakhe,Netrone yakhe uyiphose emhlabeni.
45  Uyifinyezile imihla yobutsha bakhe;Wamsongela ngehlazo. Seʹlah.
46  Kuya kude kube nini na, Yehova, uzifihlile? Lonke ixesha na?Uya kuqhubeka uvutha na umsindo wakho kanye njengomlilo?
47  Khumbula oko bukuko ubude bobomi bam.Ubadalele ilize na bonke oonyana babantu?
48  Yiyiphi na indoda eyomeleleyo ephilayo engayi kubona kufa?Ingawusindisa na umphefumlo wayo esandleni seShiyol? Seʹlah.
49  Ziphi na izenzo zakho zobubele bothando zangaphambili, Yehova,Owamfungela zona uDavide ngokuthembeka kwakho?
50  Khumbula, Yehova, ungcikivo olukubakhonzi bakho,Ukuthwala kwam esifubeni sam ungcikivo lwezizwana ezininzi,
51  Indlela ezingcikive ngayo iintshaba zakho, Yehova,Indlela ezingcikive ngayo imikhondo yothanjisiweyo wakho.
52  Makabongwe uYehova kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo. Amen, Amen.

62  Eneneni umphefumlo wam ulindele kuThixo uthule.Luvela kuye usindiso lwam.
2  Eneneni uliliwa lam nosindiso lwam, indawo yam ephakamileyo enqabisekileyo;Andiyi kushukunyiswa kakhulu.
3  Kuya kude kube nini na nisukela indulumbane umntu eningayi kumbulala?Nonke ninjengodonga oluthambekileyo, udonga lwamatye oludilikayo.
4  Eneneni banikela icebiso ukuze bamlukuhle ubani kwisidima sakhe;Bakholiswa bubuxoki.Bayasikelela ngomlomo wabo, kodwa ngaphakathi kubo bayaqalekisa. Seʹlah.
5  Eneneni lindela kuThixo uthe cwaka, mphefumlo wam,Kuba livela kuye ithemba lam.
6  Eneneni uliliwa lam nosindiso lwam, indawo yam ephakamileyo enqabisekileyo;Andiyi kushukunyiswa.
7  Usindiso lwam nozuko lwam lukuThixo.Iliwa lam elomeleleyo, indawo yam yokusabela ikuThixo.
8  Kholosani ngaye ngamaxesha onke, nina bantu.Phalazani intliziyo yenu phambi kwakhe.UThixo uyindawo yethu yokusabela. Seʹlah.
9  Eneneni oonyana babantu basemhlabeni bangumphunga,Oonyana babantu babubuxoki.Xa bebekwe ezikalini bebonke bakhaphukhaphu kunomphunga.
10  Musa ukukholosa ngenkqatho,Yaye ungabi lilize ngokuphanga kodwa.Ukuba kunokwenzeka ubuncwane buchume, musa ukubeka intliziyo yakho kubo.
11  UThixo uthethile kwaba kanye, oku ndikuve kwaba kabini,Ukuba amandla ngakaThixo.
12  Kwanobubele bothando bobakho, Yehova,Kuba wena ubuyisela ngamnye ngokomsebenzi wakhe.
73  Eneneni uThixo ulungile kuSirayeli, kwabo bantliziyo zihlambulukileyo.
2  Ke mna, iinyawo zam beziphantse zathi gu bucala,Ukunyathela kwam bekuphantse kwenziwa kwatyibilika.
3  Kuba ndabamonela abaqhayisi,Xa ndandibona uxolo lwabantu abangendawo.
4  Kuba abananimba ibulalayo;Nenteshe yabo ityebile.
5  Yaye abakho nasezinkathazweni zomntu ofayo,Ibe abakhathazwa ngokufanayo nabanye abantu.
6  Ukuziphakamisa kwabo kusebenze njengentsimbi yomqala kubo;Ugonyamelo lubagubungela njengesambatho.
7  Iliso labo lithe phuhlu ngenxa yokutyeba;Bayigqithile intelekelelo yentliziyo.
8  Bayagxeka baze bathethe okubi;Ngokuqhatha bathetha ngesimbo esiphakamileyo.
9  Umlomo wabo bawubeke emazulwini,Nolwimi lwabo luhambahamba emhlabeni.
10  Ngoko ke abantu bakhe ubabuyisela apha,Namanzi amaninzi ayakhanywa.
11  Yaye bathe: “Waze njani uThixo?Yaye ngaba unolwazi na Oyena Uphakamileyo?”
12  Khangela! Aba ngabangendawo, abahleli ngokukhululeka ngokungenammiselo.Babandisile ubuncwane babo.
13  Ngokuqinisekileyo kulilize ukuyihlambulula kwam intliziyo yamNokuhlamba kwam izandla zam ngobumsulwa.
14  Ndiye ndakhathazwa imini yonke,Yaye ndilungiswa intsasa nganye.
15  Ukuba bendithe: “Ndiya kuchaza ibali elinjalo,”Khangela! kwisizukulwana soonyana bakhoBendiya kuba ndenze ngobuqhophololo.
16  Yaye ndiye ndaqhubeka ndicinga ukuze ndikwazi oku;Bekuyinkathazo emehlweni am,
17  De ndafikelela kwingcwele ezukileyo kaThixo.Bendifuna ukuqonda ikamva labo.
18  Ngokuqinisekileyo ubabeka emhlabeni omtyibilizi.Ubenze bawa bonakala.
19  Owu hayi indlela abayinto yokukhwankqiswa ngayo njengephanyazo!Hayi indlela abafikelele esiphelweni sabo ngayo, bafikelele esiphelweni ngento enkwantyisa ngequbuliso!
20  Njengephupha emva kokuvuka, Yehova,Ngoko xa uzivuselele uya kuwudela umfanekiso wabo.
21  Kuba intliziyo yam yenziwa muncuNdaza ndahlabeka ezintsweni zam,
22  Yaye ndandingaqiqi yaye ndandingenakwazi;Ndafana nesilo nje kuphela ngokwembono yakho.
23  Kodwa ndinawe rhoqo;Usibambile isandla sam sasekunene.
24  Uya kundikhokela ngecebo lakho,Emva koko uya kundithabatha undinike uzuko.
25  Ngubani na endinaye emazulwini?Ngaphandle kwakho ayikho enye into endiyolisayo emhlabeni.
26  Inyama yam nentliziyo yam iphelelwe.UThixo uliliwa lentliziyo yam nesabelo sam ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
27  Kuba, khangela! abo badedela kude nawe baya kutshabalala.Ngokuqinisekileyo uya kuthulisa bonke abo bakushiya ngokuziphatha okubi.

138  Ndiya kukubonga ngentliziyo yam yonke.Phambi kwabanye oothixo ndiya kukuculela uncuthu lwengoma.
2  Ndiya kuqubuda ngasetempileni yakho engcwele,Kwaye ndiya kulibonga igama lakho,Ngenxa yobubele bakho bothando nangenxa yenyaniso yakho.Kuba ulenze likhulu ilizwi lakho nangaphezu kwegama lakho lonke.
