7  Ukuba ndingahamba phakathi kokubandezeleka, uya kundilondoloza.Ngenxa yomsindo weentshaba zam uya kolula isandla sakho,Yaye isandla sakho sasekunene siya kundisindisa.
8  UYehova uya kundiphelelisela okwam.Owu Yehova ububele bakho bothando bukho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.Musa ukuyishiya imisebenzi yezandla zakho.
97  UYehova uthe waba ngukumkani! Mawuvuye umhlaba.Iziqithi ezininzi mazibe nemihlali.
2  Ujikelezwe ngamafu nesithokothoko;Ubulungisa nomgwebo yindawo ekumiswe kuyo itrone yakhe.
3  Kuhamba umlilo phambi kwakhe,Yaye udla iintshaba zakhe macala onke.
4  Imibane yakhe ikhanyise ilizwe elinemveliso;Umhlaba ubonile waza waba sezintlungwini eziqatha.
5  Iintaba zanyibilika kanye njengomthwebeba ngenxa kaYehova,Ngenxa yeNkosi yomhlaba uphela.
6  Amazulu abuxelile ubulungisa bakhe,Nazo zonke izizwana zibubonile ubuqaqawuli bakhe.
7  Mababe neentloni bonke abo bakhonza nawuphi na umfanekiso oqingqiweyo,Abo baqhayisa ngoothixo abangenaxabiso.Qubudani kuye, nonke nina bothixo.
8  IZiyon ivile yaza yanemihlali,Needolophu eziphantsi kwayo zakwaYuda zavuyaNgenxa yezigwebo zakho, Yehova.
9  Kuba wena, Yehova, ungOyena Uphakamileyo phezu komhlaba wonke;Uphakame kakhulu ekunyukeni kwakho ngaphezu kwabo bonke abanye oothixo.
10  Nina nithanda uYehova, kuthiyeni okubi.Uyayilinda imiphefumlo yabanyanisekileyo bakhe;Uyabahlangula esandleni sabangendawo.
11  Ukukhanya kulibengezelele ilungisa,Nemihlali kwabo bathe tye entliziyweni.
12  Yibani nemihlali ngoYehova, nina malungisa,Nize nibulele isikhumbuzo sakhe esingcwele.
148  Dumisani uYa!Dumisani uYehova emazulwini,Mdumiseni ezindaweni eziphakamileyo.
2  Mdumiseni, nonke nina zingelosi zakhe.Mdumiseni, nonke nina mkhosi wakhe.
3  Mdumiseni, nina langa nenyanga.Mdumiseni, nonke nina zinkwenkwezi ezikhanyayo.
4  Mdumiseni, nina mazulu awo amazulu,Nani manzi angaphezu kwamazulu.
5  Mazilidumise igama likaYehova;Kuba yena wayalela, zona zadalwa.
6  Yaye uzigcina zimile ngonaphakade, ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.Unikele ummiselo, kwaye awuyi kudlula.
7  Dumisani uYehova emhlabeni,Nina zilo zikhulu zaselwandle nani nonke manzi anzongonzongo,
8  Wena mlilo nesichotho, khephu nawe ntshinyela yomsi,Wena moya uvuthuzayo, ufeza ilizwi lakhe,
9  Nina zintaba nani nonke zinduli,Nina mithi yeziqhamo nani nonke misedare,
10  Nina zilwanyana zasendle nani nonke zilwanyana zasekhaya,Nina zinto zirhubuluzayo neentaka ezinamaphiko,
11  Nina bokumkani bomhlaba nani nonke maqela eentlanga,Nina zinkosana nani nonke bagwebi bomhlaba,
12  Nina bafana kwanani zintombi ezinyulu,Nina madoda amakhulu kunye namakhwenkwe.
13  Mabalidumise igama likaYehova,Kuba ligama lakhe lodwa eliphakame ngokungenakufikeleleka.Isidima sakhe siphezu komhlaba nezulu.
14  Yaye uya kuluphakamisa uphondo lwabantu bakhe,Indumiso yabo bonke abanyanisekileyo bakhe,Yoonyana bakaSirayeli, abantu abakufuphi kuye.Dumisani uYa!
45  Intliziyo yam ivuselelekile ngumbandela olungileyo.Ndithi: “Imisebenzi yam iphathelele ukumkani.”Ngamana ulwimi lwam lungaba lusiba lomkhupheli olichule.
2  Eneneni uyinzwana ngaphezu koonyana babantu.Emilebeni yakho kugalelwe umtsalane.Kungenxa yoko le nto uThixo ekusikelele ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
3  Bhinqa ikrele lakho ethangeni lakho, wena unamandla,Ngesidima nobungangamsha bakho.
4  Ngobungangamsha bakho singa empumelelweni;Phalisa endleleni yenyaniso nentobeko nobulungisa,Yaye isandla sakho sasekunene siya kukuyalela izinto ezoyikekayo.
5  Iintolo zakho zibukhali—izizwana ziyaqhubeka zisiwa ngaphantsi kwakho—Entliziyweni yeentshaba zokumkani.
6  UThixo uyitrone yakho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, nangonaphakade;Intonga yobukhosi yobukumkani bakho yintonga yobukhosi yokuthe tye.
7  Ubuthandile ubulungisa waza wabuthiya ubungendawo.Kungenxa yoko le nto uThixo, uThixo wakho, ekuthambise ngeoli yemigcobo ngaphezu kwamaqabane akho.
8  Zonke izambatho zakho ziyimore nekhala nekasiya;Ebhotweni elizukileyo leempondo zendlovu imirhubhe ikwenze wanemihlali.
9  Phakathi kwabafazi bakho abaxabisekileyo kukho iintombi zookumkani.Iqabane elingukumkanikazi limi esandleni sakho sasekunene negolide yakwaOfire.
10  Phulaphula, ntombi, ubone, uze uyithobe indlebe yakho;Uze ubalibale abantu bakowenu nendlu kayihlo.
11  Yaye ukumkani uya kubulangazelela ubuhle bakho,Kuba uyinkosi yakho,Ngoko qubuda kuye.
12  Intombi yaseTire nayo inesipho—Abazizityebi phakathi kwabantu baya kukubongoza.
13  Intombi yokumkani izukile yonke endlwini;Isinxibo sayo sinezakhelo zegolide.
14  Iya kuziswa kukumkani inezivatho ezilukiweyo.Iintombi ezinyulu eziyilandelayo njengamaqabane ayo ziziswa kuwe.
15  Ziya kuziswa ngemihlali nokuvuya;Ziya kungena ebhotweni lokumkani.
16  Esikhundleni sookhokho bakho iya kuba ngoonyana bakho,Oya kubamisela njengeenkosana emhlabeni wonke.
17  Ndiya kulikhankanya igama lakho kuzo zonke izizukulwana ezizayo.Kungenxa yoko le nto izizwana ziya kukubonga ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, nangonaphakade.
52  Kutheni uqhayisa ngento embi, wena unamandla?Ububele bothando bukaThixo bukho imini yonke.
2  Ulwimi lwakho luceba intlekele, lulolwe njengencakuba,Lusebenza inkohliso.
3  Okubi ukuthande ngaphezu kokulungileyo,Ubuxoki ngaphezu kokuthetha ubulungisa. Seʹlah.
4  Uwathande onke amazwi aqwengayo,Owu lulwimi lunenkohliso.
5  UThixo uya kukudilizela phantsi ngonaphakade;Uya kukungqula phantsi aze akuncothule ententeni yakho,Yaye ngokuqinisekileyo uya kukuncothula elizweni labaphilayo. Seʹlah.
6  Yaye abangamalungisa baya kukubona boyike,Yaye baya kumhleka.
7  Nantsi indoda eyomeleleyo engamenzi inqaba yayo uThixo,Kodwa ekholosa ngobuninzi bobutyebi bayo,Ezikhuselayo kwiinkxwaleko ezibangelwe yiyo.
8  Kodwa ndiya kuba njengomthi womnquma onabileyo endlwini kaThixo;Ndikholosa ngobubele bothando bukaThixo ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, ngonaphakade.
9  Ndiya kukubonga ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, kuba uthabathe isenzo;Yaye ndiya kuthembela ngegama lakho, ngenxa yokuba lilungile, phambi kwabanyanisekileyo bakho.
71  Ndisabela kuwe, Yehova.Owu akwaba andingebi nazintloni.
2  Ngamana ungandihlangula ngobulungisa bakho undisindise.Ndithobele indlebe yakho undisindise.
3  Yiba yinqaba eliliwa kum endiya kungena kuyo rhoqo.Umele uyalele ukuba ndisindiswe,Kuba uyingxondorha yam negwiba lam.
4  Owu Thixo wam, ndisindise esandleni sabangendawo,Entendeni yalowo wenza ngokungekho sikweni nocinezelayo.
5  Kuba ulithemba lam, Nkosi enguMongami Yehova, endithembele ngaye kususela ebutsheni.
6  Bendizixhasa ngawe kususela ndisesiswini;UnguLowo undahlukanisayo nezibilini zikama.Ndikudumisa rhoqo.
7  Kubantu abaninzi ndinjengommangaliso;Kodwa wena uyindawo yam yokusabela eyomeleleyo.
8  Umlomo wam uzaliswe yindumiso yakho,Bubuhle bakho imini yonke.
9  Musa ukundilahla ngexesha lobudala;Xa amandla am ephela, musa ukundishiya.
10  Kuba iintshaba zam zithe ngam,Nabo balinda umphefumlo wam ngokumanyeneyo bacebisene,
11  Besithi: “UThixo umshiyile.Msukuleni nimbambe, ngokuba akukho mhlanguli.”
12  Owu Thixo, musa ukuchasela kum.Owu Thixo wam, khawuleza ukuza kundinceda.
13  Ngamana bangaba neentloni, baphele, abachasa umphefumlo wam.Ngamana bangazigqubuthela ngongcikivo nokuthotywa abo bandifunela intlekele.
14  Kodwa ke mna, ndiya kulinda rhoqo,Ndize ndongeze kwindumiso yakho yonke.
15  Umlomo wam uya kubalisa ubulungisa bakho,Imini yonke usindiso lwakho,Kuba andilazi inani labo.
16  Ndiya kufika ngamandla azukileyo, Nkosi enguMongami Yehova;Ndiya kubukhankanya ubulungisa bakho, obakho wedwa.
17  Owu Thixo, undifundise ukususela ebutsheni bam,Yaye kude kube ngoku ndiqhubeka ndixela imisebenzi yakho emangalisayo.
18  Owu Thixo, musa ukundishiya ndide ndibe mdala ndibe nezimvi,De ndixelele izizukulwana ngengalo yakho,Kubo bonke abo baza kuza, ngamandla akho.
19  Ubulungisa bakho, Thixo, bufikelela kwindawo ephakamileyo;Ngokuphathelele izinto ezinkulu ozenzileyo,Owu Thixo, ngubani na onjengawe?
20  Ngenxa yokuba undenze ndabona ukubandezeleka neentlekele ezininzi,Kwanga ungandivuselela kwakhona;Uze undikhuphe emanzini anzongonzongo omhlaba.
21  Ngamana ungabandisa ubukhulu bam,Yaye kwanga ungandingqonga undithuthuzele.
22  Nam, ndiya kukubonga ngohlobo oluthile lomrhubhe,Ngokuphathelele ukuba yinyaniso kwakho, Thixo wam.Ndiya kukuculela uncuthu lwengoma ngohadi, Wena uyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.
23  Imilebe yam iya kumemelela ngovuyo xa ndityekele ekukuculeleni uncuthu lwengoma,Kwanomphefumlo wam owukhululeyo.
24  Kwanolwimi lwam, luya kubuvakalisa ngesandi esiphantsi ubulungisa bakho, imini yonke,Kuba baneentloni, kuba badanile, abo bafuna ndehlelwe yintlekele.
128  Unoyolo wonk’ ubani omoyikayo uYehova,Ohamba ngeendlela zakhe.
2  Kuba uya kudla ukubulaleka kwezandla zakho.Uya kuba noyolo yaye kuya kuba kuhle kuwe.
3  Umfazi wakho uya kuba njengomdiliya othwala isiqhamoKwezona nxalenye zingaphakathi zendlu yakho.Oonyana bakho baya kuba njengezithole zomnquma bajikeleze itafile yakho.
4  Khangela! Leyo yindlela eya kusikelelwa ngayo indoda eyomeleleyoEmoyikayo uYehova.
5  UYehova uya kukusikelela eZiyon.Khawubone okulungileyo kwaseYerusalem yonke imihla yobomi bakho,
6  Ubone noonyana boonyana bakho.Ngamana kungakho uxolo phezu koSirayeli.
76  UThixo uyaziwa kwaYuda;KwaSirayeli igama lakhe likhulu.
2  Indawo yakhe esekusithekeni iseSalem,Nendawo yakhe yokuhlala iseZiyon.
3  Wayaphula apho imiphini enombane yesaphetha,Ikhaka nekrele nedabi. Seʹlah.
4  Ugutyungelwe kukukhanya, okunobungangamsha ngaphezu kweentaba zexhoba.
5  Abo baneentliziyo ezomeleleyo baphangiwe,Bozele ebuthongweni babo,Yaye akukho namnye kuwo onke amadoda anobukroti ozifumeneyo izandla zabo.
6  Kukhalimelo lwakho, Thixo kaYakobi, umqhubi wenqwelo nehashe balele yoyi.
7  Wena—uyoyikeka,Ngubani onokuma phambi kwakho ngenxa yamandla omsindo wakho?
8  Usemazulwini wabangela imbambano yomthetho yeviwa;Umhlaba woyika waza wazola
9  Xa uThixo waphakamayo ukuze agwebe,Asindise bonke abalulamileyo bomhlaba. Seʹlah.
10  Kuba umsindo womntu uya kukubonga;Umsindo oseleyo uya kuwubhinqa.
11  Yenzani isibhambathiso nize nisifezekise kuYehova uThixo wenu, nonke nina bamjikelezileyo.Mabamzisele isipho besoyika.
12  Uya kuwuthoba umoya weenkokeli;Uyoyikeka kookumkani bomhlaba.
23  UYehova ngumaLusi wam.Andiyi kuswela nto.
2  Undilalisa kumadlelo anengca;Undikhaphelela kwiindawo zokuphumla ezinamanzi amaninzi.
3  Uyawuhlaziya umphefumlo wam.Undikhokelela kumkhondo wobulungisa ngenxa yegama lakhe.
4  Nangona ndihamba kwintlambo yethunzi elimnyama,Andoyiki nto imbi,Kuba unam wena;Intonga yakho nomsimelelo wakho ziyandithuthuzela.
5  Ulungiselela phambi kwam itafile phambi kwabo babonisa ubutshaba kum.Intloko yam uyithambise ngeoli;Indebe yam iyaphuphuma.
6  Ngokuqinisekileyo ukulunga nobubele bothando buya kundisukela yonke imihla yobomi bam;Yaye ndiya kuhlala endlwini kaYehova imihla emide.
42  Njengexhamakazi elilangazelela imisinga yamanzi,Ngoko umphefumlo wam ulangazelela wena, Thixo.
2  Eneneni umphefumlo wam unxanelwe uThixo, uThixo ophilayo.Ndiya kuza nini na ndibonakale phambi koThixo?
3  Kum iinyembezi zam zikukutya imini nobusuku,Ngoxa besithi kum imini yonke: “Uphi na uThixo wakho?”
4  Ezi zinto ndiya kuzikhumbula, yaye ndiya kuwuphalazela kuwe umphefumlo wam.Kuba ndandidla ngokudlula nomndilili,Ndandidla ngokuhamba ndicotha phambi kwabo ndisiya endlwini kaThixo,Ngelizwi lentswahla yovuyo nombulelo,Lesihlwele esibhiyozela umthendeleko.
5  Kutheni na uphelelwe lithemba, mphefumlo wam,Kutheni na uxokozela ngaphakathi kum?Lindela kuThixo,Kuba ndisaya kumbonga njengosindiso oluzukileyo lwam siqu.
6  Owu Thixo wam, umphefumlo wam uphelelwe lithemba ngaphakathi kum.Kungenxa yoko ndikukhumbula,Ukusuka kwilizwe laseYordan ukusa kwiincopho zeHermon,Ukusuka kwintaba encinane.
7  Amanzi anzongonzongo abiza amanzi anzongonzongoKwakuvakala isandi somtshizo wamanzi akho.Onke amaza akho—Adlule phezu kwam.
8  Emini uYehova uya kuyalela ububele bakhe bothando,Kwaye ebusuku ingoma yakhe iya kuba nam;Kuya kubakho umthandazo woThixo wobomi bam.
9  Ndiya kuthi kuThixo oyingxondorha yam:“Undilibaleleni na?Kutheni na ndihamba ndibuhlungu ngenxa yengcinezelo yotshaba?”
10  Abo babonisa ubutshaba kum bandingcikiva befuna ukubulala amathambo am,Ngoxa imini yonke besithi kum: “Uphi na uThixo wakho?”
11  Kutheni na uphelelwe lithemba, mphefumlo wam,Kutheni na uxokozela ngaphakathi kum?Lindela kuThixo,Kuba ndisaya kumbonga njengosindiso oluzukileyo lwam siqu nanjengoThixo wam.
91  Nabani na ohleli kwindawo efihlakeleyo yOyena UphakamileyoUya kuzifumanela indawo yokulalisa emthunzini waLowo unguSomandla.
2  Ndiza kuthi kuYehova: “Uyindawo yam yokusabela negwiba lam,Thixo wam, endiza kukholosa ngaye.”
3  Kuba yena uya kukuhlangula kwisibatha sombambisi weentaka,Nakwindyikitya yokufa ebangela iinkxwaleko.
4  Ngeentsiba zakhe uya kuthintela kungasondeli nto kuwe,Wena uya kusabela phantsi kwamaphiko akhe.Inyaniso yakhe iya kuba likhaka elikhulu nesikhuselo.
5  Akuyi koyika nantoni na eyoyikekayo ebusuku,Nalutolo luphaphazelayo emini,
6  Nandyikitya yokufa ehamba esithokothokweni,Nantshabalalo iphangayo emini emaqanda.
7  Kuya kuwa iwaka ecaleni kwakhoNeshumi lamawaka ngasesandleni sakho sokunene;Kuwe akuyi kusondela nto.
8  Uya kukhangela kuphela ngamehlo akhoUze ubone impindezelo kwabo bangendawo.
9  Ngenxa yokuba uthe: “UYehova uyindawo yam yokusabela,”Wenze Oyena Uphakamileyo waba yindawo yakho yokuhlala;
10  Akukho ntlekele iya kukuhlela,Nesibetho asiyi kusondela ententeni yakho.
11  Kuba iingelosi zakhe uya kuzinika umyalelo ngawe,Ukuba zikulinde ezindleleni zakho zonke.
12  Ziya kukuthwala ngezandla zazo,Ukuze ungabetheki ngonyawo lwakho kulo naliphi na ilitye.
13  Uya kunyathela phezu kwengonyama entsha nephimpi;Uya kunyathelela phantsi ingonyama entsha enesingci nenyoka enkulu.
14  Ngenxa yokuba ebonise umsa wakhe kum,Nam ndiya kumsindisa.Ndiya kumkhusela ngenxa yokuba elazi igama lam.
15  Uya kubiza kum, yaye ndiya kumphendula.Ndiya kuba naye ekubandezelekeni.Ndiya kumhlangula ndize ndimzukise.
16  Ndiya kumanelisa ngemihla emide,Yaye ndiya kumbangela akubone ukusindisa kwam.
22  Thixo wam, Thixo wam, undishiyeleni na?Kutheni na ukude ukuba ungandisindisa,Kumazwi okugcuma kwam?
2  Owu Thixo wam, ndiqhubeka ndikubiza emini, kodwa akuphenduli;Nasebusuku, yaye andithuli.
3  Kodwa ungcwele,Uhlala kwiindumiso zakwaSirayeli.
4  Oobawo babekholose ngawe;Babekholosile, yaye waqhubeka ubasindisa.
5  Badanduluka kuwe, baza basinda;Bakholosa ngawe, yaye abazange badane.
6  Kodwa ke ndingumbungu, andingomntu,Ndilungcikivo ebantwini nodelekileyo ebantwini.
7  Abo bandibonayo, bayandigculela;Baqhubeka beyivula ibe banzi imilomo yabo, baqhubeka behlunguzela intloko yabo besithi:
8  “Uzinikele kuYehova. Makamsindise!Makamhlangule, ngenxa yokuba uyoliswa nguye!”
9  Kuba unguLowo wandikhuphayo esiswini,Lowo undenza ndikholose ngoxa ndisemabeleni kama.
10  Ndaphuma esibelekweni ndaphoselwa kuwe;Kususela esiswini sikama ubunguThixo wam.
11  Musa ukuba kude nam, ngenxa yokuba ukubandezeleka kukufuphi,Ngenxa yokuba akakho omnye umncedi.
12  Maninzi amathole eenkomo aziinkunzi andingqongileyo;Abanamandla bakwaBhashan bandijikelezile.
13  Zindivulele imilomo yazo,Njengengonyama eqwengayo negqumayo.
14  Ndiphalazwe njengamanzi,Yaye onke amathambo am ahlukanisiwe.Intliziyo yam ifana nomthwebeba;Inyibilikile ngaphakathi kum.
15  Amandla am omile njengeceba lengqayi,Nolwimi lwam lunamatheliswe ezintsinini zam;Yaye wena undibeka eluthulini lokufa.
16  Kuba ndingqongwe zizinja;Indibano yabenzi bobubi indivingcele.Injengengonyama ezandleni nasezinyaweni zam.
17  Ndingawabala onke amathambo am.Bona bayakhangela, bayandondela.
18  Izambatho zam bahlulelana ngazo,Isinxibo sam benza amaqashiso ngaso.
19  Kodwa wena, Yehova, musa ukuba kude kum.Wena ungamandla am, khawuleza uze kundinceda.
20  Wuhlangule kwikrele umphefumlo wam,Okuphela kwawo kwithupha lenja;
21  Ndisindise emlonyeni wengonyama,Nakwiimpondo zenqu umele undiphendule undisindise.
22  Ndiya kulivakalisa kubazalwana bam igama lakho;Phakathi ebandleni ndiya kukudumisa.
23  Nina boyika uYehova, mdumiseni!Nina nonke mbewu kaYakobi, mzukiseni!Nothuke ngenxa yakhe, nonke nina mbewu kaSirayeli.
24  Kuba akadelangaEngazothekanga ngenkxwaleko yoxhwalekileyo;Ibe ubuso bakhe akabufihlanga kuye,Yaye xa ekhalela uncedo kuye umvile.
25  Wena uya kundizukisa ebandleni elikhulu;Izibhambathiso zam ndiya kuzifezekisa phambi kwabo bamoyikayo.
26  Abalulamileyo baya kudla banele;Abo bamfunayo baya kumdumisa uYehova.Ngamana iintliziyo zenu zingaphila ngonaphakade.
27  Zonke iziphelo zomhlaba ziya kukhumbula zibuyele kuYehova.Nazo zonke iintsapho zeentlanga ziya kuqubuda phambi kwakho.
28  Kuba ubukumkani bobukaYehova,Yaye ulawula iintlanga.
29   Bonke abatyebileyo bomhlaba baya kutya baze baqubude;Phambi kwakhe bonke abo bahlela eluthulini baya kugoba,Yaye akukho namnye uya kuze awugcine uphila umphefumlo wakhe.
30  Imbewu iya kumkhonza;Iya kuvakalisa ngoYehova kwisizukulwana.
31  Baya kuza baxele ubulungisa bakheKubantu abaza kuzalwa, ukuba nguye owenze oku.
135  Dumisani uYa!Dumisani igama likaYehova,Nikelani indumiso, nina bakhonzi bakaYehova,
2  Nina nimiyo endlwini kaYehova,Ezintendelezweni zendlu yoThixo wethu.
3  Dumisani uYa, kuba uYehova ulungile.Liculeleni uncuthu lwengoma igama lakhe, kuba liyathandeka.
4  Kuba uYa uzinyulele uYakobi kanye,USirayeli ukuba abe yinqobo kuye.
5  Kuba mna ndiyazi ukuba uYehova mkhulu,Yaye iNkosi yethu ingaphezu kwabo bonke abanye oothixo.
6  Yonk’ into uYehova ayoliswe kukuyenza uyenzileEmazulwini nasemhlabeni, kwiilwandle nasemanzini onke anzongonzongo.
7  Unyusa umphunga eziphelweni zomhlaba;Imvula uyenzele imijelo;Ukhupha umoya koovimba bakhe,
8  Lowo waxabela amazibulo aseYiputa,Kokubini umntu nesilo.
9  Wathumela imiqondiso nemimangaliso phakathi kwakho, Yiputa,KuFaro nakubakhonzi bakhe bonke;

11  KwanoSihon ukumkani wama-AmoriNo-Ogi ukumkani waseBhashanNazo zonke izikumkani zakwaKanan,
12  Nowanikela ilizwe labo laba lilifa,Ilifa kuSirayeli abantu bakhe.
13  Owu Yehova, igama lakho likho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.Owu Yehova, isikhumbuzo sakho sikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.
14  Kuba uYehova uya kuligweba ityala labantu bakhe,Kwaye uya kuzisola nangenxa yabakhonzi bakhe.
15  Izithixo zeentlanga yisilivere negolide,Umsebenzi wezandla zomntu wasemhlabeni.
16  Zinomlomo, kodwa azithethi;Zinamehlo, kodwa aziboni;

18  Abo bazenzayo baya kuba njengazo,Wonk’ ubani okholosa ngazo.

127  Ngaphandle kokuba uYehova uyayakha indlu,Kulilize ukusebenza nzima kwabakhi bayo kuyo.Ngaphandle kokuba uYehova uyasilinda isixeko,Kulilize ukuhlala komlindi ephaphile.
2  Kulilize ukuvuka kwenu ekuseni,Ukungahlali kwenu phantsi kude kuhlwe,Ukutya kwenu ukutya nisezintlungwini.Kanye ngolu hlobo uyinika ubuthongo intanda yakhe.

5  Inoyolo indoda eyomeleleyo ezalise umphongolo wayo ngabo.Abayi kuba neentloni,Kuba baya kuthetha neentshaba esangweni.
38  Owu Yehova, ungandohlwayi ucaphukile,Undilungise unomsindo.
2  Kuba iintolo zakho zingene zatshona kum,Nesandla sakho sehlele phezu kwam.
3  Akukho ndawo iphilileyo enyameni yam ngenxa yesiqalekiso sakho.Uxolo alukho emathanjeni am ngenxa yesono sam.
4  Kuba iziphoso zam zidlule phezu kwentloko yam;Njengomthwalo onzima zinzima kakhulu kum.
5  Amanxeba am anuka kakubi, ayachiza,Ngenxa yobudenge bam.
6  Ndiphazamisekile, ndithobe ngomlinganiselo ogqithileyo;Imini yonke ndihambahamba ndibuhlungu.
7  Kuba isinqe sam sizaliswe kukutshisa,Yaye akukho ndawo iphilileyo enyameni yam.
8  Ndisuke ndandindisholo yaye ndityumke ngomlinganiselo ogqithileyo;Ndiyagcuma ngenxa yokugcuma kwentliziyo yam.
9  Owu Yehova, uphambi kwakho wonke umnqweno wam,Yaye ukuncinwa kwam akufihlwanga kuwe.
10  Intliziyo yam ingongoza kakhulu, amandla am andishiyile,Nokukhanya kwamehlo am akukho kum.
11  Ke zona izithandwa zam, namaqabane am, aqhubeka emele kude nesibetho sam,Abo ndibaqhele ngokusondeleyo bame mgama.
12  Kodwa abo bafuna umphefumlo wam bandibekele izibatha,Abo basebenzela ukundenzela intlekele bathethe ngamashwangusha,Baqhubeka bedumzela inkohliso imini yonke.
13  Ke mna, njengalowo usisithulu, ndandingaphulaphuli;Nanjengalowo ungathethiyo, ndandingawuvuli umlomo wam.
14  Ndaba njengomntu ongevayo,Yaye emlonyeni wam kwakungekho ngxoxo yakuziphendulela.
15  Kuba ndandilindele kuwe, Yehova;Wena wandiphendula, Yehova Thixo wam.
16  Kuba ndithe: “Kungenjalo baya kuba nemihlali ngam;Xa unyawo lwam lutyibilika, bayazigwagwisa kum.”
17  Kuba ndandilungele ukujingxela,Nentlungu yam yayiphambi kwam rhoqo.
18  Kuba ndasixela isiphoso sam;Ndaqalisa ukuxhalaba ngenxa yesono sam.
19  Neentshaba zam eziphilayo zaba namandla,Nabo bandithiyileyo ngaphandle kwesizathu baba baninzi.
20  Ngokulungileyo babendivuza ngokubi;Baqhubeka bendixhathisa ngenxa yokusukela kwam okulungileyo.
21  Musa ukundishiya, Yehova.Owu Thixo wam, musa ukuba kude nam.
22  Khawuleza ukuza kundinceda,Owu Yehova lusindiso lwam.

2  Imisebenzi kaYehova mikhulu,
3  Umsebenzi wakhe usisidima nobungangamsha,

86  Ndithobele indlebe yakho, Yehova. Ndiphendule,Kuba ndixhwalekile kwaye ndilihlwempu.
2  Linda umphefumlo wam, ngokuba ndinyanisekile.UnguThixo wam—msindise umkhonzi wakho—okholose ngawe.
3  Ndibabale, Yehova,Kuba ndibiza kuwe imini yonke.
4  Wenze ube nemihlali umphefumlo womkhonzi wakho,Kuba ndiwuphakamisela kuwe, Yehova, umphefumlo wam.
5  Kuba wena, Yehova, ulungile yaye ukulungele ukuxolela;Buninzi ububele bakho bothando kubo bonke abo babiza kuwe.
6  Wuphulaphule, Yehova, umthandazo wam;Unikele ingqalelo kwilizwi lezibongozo zam.
7  Ngemini yokubandezeleka kwam ndiya kubiza kuwe,Kuba uya kundiphendula.
8  Akukho unjengawe phakathi koothixo, Yehova,Yaye akukho misebenzi injengeyakho.

10  Kuba umkhulu yaye wenza izinto ezimangalisayo;UnguThixo, wena wedwa.
11  Ndiyalele, Yehova, ngendlela yakho.Ndiya kuhamba enyanisweni yakho.Yenze imanyane intliziyo yam ukuba iloyike igama lakho.
12  Ndiyakubonga, Yehova Thixo wam, ngayo yonke intliziyo yam,Kwaye ndiya kulizukisa igama lakho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo,
13  Kuba bukhulu ububele bakho bothando kum,Yaye uwuhlangule umphefumlo wam eShiyol, emazantsi ayo.
14  Owu Thixo, abakhukhumeleyo bandivukele;Nendibano yabo bangoozwilakhe ifuna umphefumlo wam,Yaye abakubekanga phambi kwabo.
15  Kodwa wena, Yehova, unguThixo onenceba nobabalo,Ozeka kade umsindo nonobubele bothando obuninzi nenyaniso.
16  Buyela kum undibabale.Mnike amandla akho umkhonzi wakho,Umsindise unyana wekhobokazana lakho.

32  Unoyolo lowo imvukelo yakhe ixolelweyo, isono sakhe esigutyungelweyo.
2  Unoyolo umntu uYehova angasibaleli kuye isiphoso,Nekungekho nkohliso kumoya wakhe.
3  Ndithi ndakuthi cwaka aphele amathambo am kukugcuma kwam imini yonke.

6  Ngenxa yoku bonke abanyanisekileyo baya kuthandaza kuweNgelo xesha kuphela xa unokufunyanwa.Ke sona isikhukula samanzi amaninzi, asiyi kumchukumisa.

10  Zininzi iintlungu anazo ongendawo;Kodwa lowo ukholosa ngoYehova, ungqongwe bububele bothando.

6  Owu Yehova, ungandohlwayi usemsindweni,Ungandilungisi ucaphukile.
2  Ndibabale, Yehova, kuba ndiyaphelelwa.Ndiphilise, Yehova, kuba amathambo am aphazamisekile.

4  Buya, Yehova, uwuhlangule umphefumlo wam;Ndisindise ngenxa yobubele bakho obunothando.
5  Kuba ekufeni akukhankanywa;EShiyol ngubani na oya kukubonga?
6  Ndityhafile kukuncwina kwam;Ubusuku bonke ndiyasidadisa isingqengqelo sam;Umandlalo wam ndiwenza uphuphume iinyembezi zam.

31  Ndisabela kuwe, Yehova.Owu ngamana andingeze ndidaniswe.Ndisindise ngobulungisa bakho.

25  Owu Yehova, ndiwuphakamisela kuwe umphefumlo wam.
2  Owu Thixo wam, ndikholose ngawe;Ngamana ndingangadani.Ngamana iintshaba zam azingendivuyeleli.
3  Akukho namnye kwabo bathembela ngawe oya kudana.Baya kudana abo benza ngobuqhophololo ngaphandle kwempumelelo.

18  Yibone inkxwaleko yam nenkathazo yam,Uze uzixolele zonke izono zam.

20  Wulinde umphefumlo wam undihlangule.Ngamana ndingangadaniswa, kuba ndisabela kuwe.
21  Ingqibelelo nokutye tye makundilondoloze,Kuba ndithembela kuwe.

92  Kulungile ukubulela kuYehovaNokuculela igama lakho uncuthu lwengoma, wena ungOyena Uphakamileyo;

113  Dumisani uYa!Nikelani indumiso, nina bakhonzi bakaYehova,Dumisani igama likaYehova.

14  Lowo ungenangqiqo uthe entliziyweni yakhe:“Akakho uYehova.”Benze ngokonakala, ziyacekiseka izenzo zabo.Akukho namnye owenza okulungileyo.

145  Ndiza kukuphakamisa, Thixo wam Kumkani,Yaye ndiza kulibonga igama lakho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, ewe, ngonaphakade.

140  Ndihlangule, Yehova, kubo abantu ababi;Ngamana ungandilondoloza nasemntwini wezenzo zogonyamelo,
2  Abo baceba izinto ezimbi entliziyweni yabo,Abaqhubeka behlasela imini yonke njengasezimfazweni.
3  Balulolile ulwimi lwabo njengolo lwenyoka;Ubuhlungu berhamba elineempondwana buphantsi kwemilebe yabo. Seʹlah.

60  Owu Thixo, usilahlile, usityhobozile,Unomsindo. Ufanele usibuyise.
2  Uwubangele wanyikima umhlaba, uwucandile.Philisa iintanda zawo, kuba ushukumile.

4  Ubanike umqondiso abo bakoyikayoUkuba basabe ngokugosogoso ngenxa yesaphetha. Seʹlah.
5  Ukuze bahlangulwe abathandekayo bakho,Sisindise ngesandla sakho sasekunene uze usiphendule.
6  UThixo uthethile ebungcweleni bakhe wathi:“Ndiza kugcoba, ndinikele ngeShekem njengesahlulo;Nentili yaseSukoti ndiya kuyilinganisa.
7  UGiliyadi ngowam noManase ngowam,UEfrayim uyinqaba yalowo uyintloko kum;UYuda ngumsimelelo womyaleli wam.
8  UMowabhi yimbiza yam yokuhlambela.Ndiya kuyiphosa phezu koEdom imbadada yam.Naphezu kwelamaFilisti ndiya kuduma ngoloyiso.”
9  Ngubani na oya kundizisa kwisixeko esingqingiweyo?Ngubani na oya kundikhokelela kwaEdom ngokuqinisekileyo?
10  Asinguwe na, Thixo, osilahlileyoNongahambiyo nemikhosi yethu njengoThixo?
11  Sinike uncedo ekubandezelekeni,Ekubeni usindiso lomntu wasemhlabeni lungento yanto.
12  KuThixo siya kuzuza amandla,Yaye yena uya kuzinyathela iintshaba zethu.
53  Lowo ungenangqiqo uthe entliziyweni yakhe:“Akakho uYehova.” Benze ngokonakala yaye benze ngokucekisekayo ngentswela-bulungisa;Akukho namnye owenza okulungileyo.
2  Ke yena uThixo, ukhangele phantsi koonyana babantu esezulwini,Ukuze abone enoba kukho nabani na onengqiqo, nabani na ofuna uYehova.
3  Bonke babuyele emva, bonke bonakele ngokufanayo;Akukho namnye owenza okulungileyo,Nokuba abe mnye.
4  Ngaba akukho namnye kwabo baqhelisela okwenzakalisayo onolwazi,Badla abantu bam njengoko besidla isonka?Abambizanga noYehova.
5  Apho bazaliswa lunkwantyo olukhulu,Apho kwakungqineke kungekho kunkwantya;Kuba uThixo uya kuwachithachitha ngokuqinisekileyo amathambo akhe nabani na omisa inkampu nxamnye nawe.Uya kubahlazisa ngokuqinisekileyo, kuba uYehova ubagatyile.
6  Owu akwaba usindiso oluzukileyo lukaSirayeli beluseZiyon!Ekubuyiseni kukaYehova abantu bakhe abathinjiweyo.Makavuye uYakobi, abe nemihlali uSirayeli.
39  Ndathi: “Ndiya kuzilinda iindlela zamUkuze ndilugcine ulwimi lwam lungoni.Ndiya kubeka isicheme njengomlindi emlonyeni wam,Logama nje kukho ongendawo phambi kwam.”
2  Ndathula andathetha;Ndathi cwaka kokulungileyo,Yacinezelwa intlungu yam.
3  Intliziyo yam yaba shushu ngaphakathi kum;Ekuncwineni kwam umlilo waqhubeka uvutha.Ndathetha ngolwimi lwam ndathi:
4  “Owu Yehova, ndibangele ndisazi isiphelo sam,Nomlinganiselo weentsuku zam—uyintoni na,Ukuze ndazi ukuba bufutshane kangakanani na ubomi bam.
5  Khangela! Iintsuku zam uzenze zambalwa;Nobude bobomi bam abunto phambi kwakho.Ngokuqinisekileyo bonke abantu basemhlabeni, nangona bemi ngokuqinileyo, bangumphunga nje kuphela. Seʹlah.
6  Ngokuqinisekileyo umntu uhambahamba njengesithunzi.Ngokuqinisekileyo baxokozela ngelize.Umntu ufumba izinto engazi ukuba ngubani na oya kuzihlanganisa.
7  Owu Yehova, bendithembe ntoni na?Ndilindele kuwe.
8  Ndihlangule kuko konke ukunxaxha kwam.Musa ukundenza ungcikivo kulowo ungenangqiqo.
9  Ndiqhubeke ndingathethi; ndingenakuwuvula umlomo wam,Kuba oko kwenziwe nguwe.
10  Sisuse kum isibetho sakho.Ngenxa yobutshaba besandla sakho ndifikelele esiphelweni.
11  Umntu umlungise ngokumohlwayela isiphoso,Izinto zakhe ezinqwenelekayo uzidla njengoko lisenza inundu.Ngokuqinisekileyo bonke abantu basemhlabeni bangumphunga. Seʹlah.
12  Wuve umthandazo wam, Yehova,Uze ukubekele indlebe ukukhalela kwam uncedo.Kwiinyembezi zam musa ukuthi cwaka.Kuba ndingumphambukeli kuwe,Umfiki ngokufanayo nabo bonke ookhokho bam.
13  Jonga kude kum, ukuze ndiqaqambeNgaphambi kokuba ndimke ndingabikho.”
56  Ndibabale, Thixo, ngenxa yokuba umntu ofayo undingqavule.Esilwa imini yonke, uqhubeka endicinezela.
2  Iintshaba zam ziqhubeka zindingqavula imini yonke,Kuba baninzi abalwa nam beziphakamisile.
3  Nokuba ndoyika ngaluphi na usuku, mna ndiya kukholosa ngawe.
4  Ndikunye noThixo ndiya kulidumisa ilizwi lakhe.Ndikholose ngoThixo; andiyi koyika.Inokundenza ntoni na inyama?
5  Imini yonke baqhubeka bephazamisa imicimbi yam yobuqu;Zonke iingcinga zabo zibububi nxamnye nam.
6  Bayahlasela, bayazifihla,Bona baqhubeka bejonge amanyathelo am,Ngoxa belindele umphefumlo wam.
7  Bakhahlele ngenxa yokwenzakalisa kwabo.Ngomsindo  zihlise izizwana, Thixo.
8  Ukubhaca kwam wena ukuxelile.Iinyembezi zam zifake kwintsuba yakho.Ngaba azikho encwadini yakho?
9  Ngelo xesha iintshaba zam ziya kubuya, ngosuku endibiza ngalo;Oku ndikwazi kakuhle, ukuba uThixo ungowam.
10  Ndikunye noThixo ndiya kulidumisa ilizwi lakhe;Ndikunye noYehova ndiya kulidumisa ilizwi lakhe.
11  Ndikholosa ngoThixo. Andiyi koyika.Unokundenza ntoni na umntu wasemhlabeni?
12  Owu Thixo, ziphezu kwam izibhambathiso zakho.Ndiya kwenza umbulelo kuwe.
13  Kuba uwuhlangule umphefumlo wam ekufeni—Ngaba akuzihlangulanga iinyawo zam ekukhubekeni?—Ukuze ndihambahambe phambi koThixo ekukhanyeni kwabo baphilayo.
134  Mbongeni uYehova,Nonke nina bakhonzi bakaYehova,Nina enimi endlwini kaYehova ebudeni bobusuku.
2  Phakamisani izandla zenu ebungcweleniNize nibonge uYehova.
3  Ngamana uYehova anganisikelela eZiyon,Yena onguMenzi wezulu nomhlaba.
142  Ngelizwi lam, ndamemeza kuYehova ndicela uncedo;Ngelizwi lam, ndakhala kuYehova ndifuna ubabalo.
2  Ndakuphalazela kuye ukuxhalaba kwam;Ndaqhubeka ndikuxela kuye ukubandezeleka kwam,
3  Ekutyhafeni komoya wam ngaphakathi kwam.Wandula ke wena wayazi indlela yam.Emendweni endihamba ngawoBandifihlele isibatha.
4  Khangela ngasekunene uze uboneUkuba akukho bani unikela nayiphi na ingqalelo kum.Indawo yam yokusabela itshabalele kum;Akukho bani ubuzisayo ngomphefumlo wam.
5  Ndimemeze kuwe, Yehova, ndicela uncedo.Ndathi: “Uyindawo yam yokusabela,Isabelo sam elizweni labaphilayo.”
6  Nikela ingqalelo kwisikhalo sam sokubongoza,Kuba ndihlwempuzeke kakhulu.Ndihlangule kubatshutshisi bam,Kuba bomelele ngakumbi kunam.
7  Wukhuphe entolongweni umphefumlo wamUkuze ndibonge igama lakho.Mandiphahlwe ngamalungisa,Ngenxa yokuba undiphatha ngokufanelekileyo.
133  Khangela! Hayi indlela ekulunge nekuthandeka ngayoUkuba abazalwana bahlale ndawonye ngomanyano!
2  Kunjengeoli elungileyo entloko,Ehla ezindevini,Ezindevini zika-Aron,Ehla ngomphetho wezambatho zakhe.
3  Kunjengombethe weHermonOhla phezu kweentaba zaseZiyon.Kuba uYehova wayalela ukuba kubekho intsikelelo apho,Kwanobomi ukusa kwixesha elingenasiphelo.
119  Banoyolo abo bandlela yabo ingenasiphoso,Abo bahamba emthethweni kaYehova.
2  Banoyolo abo bagcina izikhumbuzo zakhe;Bamfune ngentliziyo yonke.
3  Ngokwenene abaqheliseli ntswela-bulungisa.Bahambe ngeendlela zakhe.
4  Wena ngokuyalelayo unikele imiyalelo yakhoUkuba igcinwe ngenyameko.
5  Owu akwaba iindlela zam bezimiselwe ngokuqinileyoUkugcina imimiselo yakho!
6  Ngoko ke bendingayi kuba nazintloni,Xa ndikhangela kuyo yonke imiyalelo yakho.
7  Ndiya kukubonga ngentliziyo ethe tye,Ekuzifundeni kwam izigwebo zakho zobulungisa.
8  Ndiyaqhubeka ndiyigcina imimiselo yakho.Owu musa ukundishiya ngokupheleleyo.
9  Umfana uya kuwuhlambulula njani na umendo wakhe?Ngokuzilinda ngokwelizwi lakho.
10  Ndikufune ngentliziyo yam iphela.Musa ukundibangela ndihambe ndibhadula emiyalelweni yakho.
11  Ndiligcine entliziyweni yam ilizwi lakho,Ukuze ndingakoni.
12  Ungowokubongwa wena, Yehova.Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.
13  Ngemilebe yam ndizivakalisileZonke izigwebo zomlomo wakho.
14  Endleleni yezikhumbuzo zakho ndiye ndagcoba,Kanye njengakuzo zonke izinto zexabiso.
15  Ndiza kuzixhalabisa ngemiyalelo yakho,Kwaye ndiza kukhangela umendo wakho.
16  Ndiya kubonisa ukuyithanda imimiselo yakho.Andiyi kulilibala ilizwi lakho.
17  Yenza ngokufanelekileyo kumkhonzi wakho, ukuze ndiphileNokuze ndigcine ilizwi lakho.
18  Vula amehlo am, ukuze ndikhangeleKwizinto ezimangalisayo ezisemthethweni wakho.
19  Ndingumphambukeli elizweni.Musa ukuyifihla kum imiyalelo yakho.
20  Umphefumlo wam utyumkile ngokulangazelelaIzigwebo zakho ngalo lonke ixesha.
21  Ubakhalimele abo bakhukhumeleyo abaqalekisiweyo,Abashenxayo emiyalelweni yakho.
22  Susa kum ungcikivo nokudelwa,Kuba ndizigcinile izikhumbuzo zakho.
23  Kwaneenkosana zihleli; zathetha omnye komnye ngam.Yena ke umkhonzi wakho, uzixhalabisa ngemimiselo yakho.
24  Ndiyazithanda izikhumbuzo zakho,Njengamadoda ecebo lam.
25  Umphefumlo wam ubunamathele eluthulini.Ndigcine ndiphila ngokwelizwi lakho.
26  Ndivakalise iindlela zam, ukuze undiphendule.Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.
27  Ndiqondise indlela yemiyalelo yakho,Ukuze ndizixhalabise ngemisebenzi yakho emangalisayo.
28  Umphefumlo wam ubungalali ngenxa yentlungu.Ndivuse ngokwelizwi lakho.
29  Shenxisa kum indlela yobuxoki,Uze undibabale ngomthetho wakho.
30  Ndinyule indlela yokuthembeka.Izigwebo zakho ndizigqale njengezifanelekileyo.
31  Ndinamathele kwizikhumbuzo zakho.Owu Yehova, ungandenzi ndihlazeke.
32  Ndiya kubaleka ngendlela yemiyalelo yakho,Ngenxa yokuba uyenze yabanzi intliziyo yam.
33  Ndiyalele, Yehova, endleleni yemimiselo yakho,Ukuze ndiyigcine kude kuse ekupheleni.
34  Ndiqondise, ukuze ndigcine umthetho wakhoNokuze ndiwugcine ngentliziyo iphela.
35  Ndinyathelise kuwo umendo wemiyalelo yakho,Kuba ndiyayoliswa nguwo.
36  Intliziyo yam yithobele kwizikhumbuzo zakho,Kungekhona kwingeniso.
37  Dlulisa amehlo am angaboni oko kungento yanto;Ndigcine ndiphila ngokwendlela yakho.
38  Phumeza kumkhonzi wakho ilizwi lakhoElo likhokelela ekubeni akoyike.
39  Dlulisa ungcikivo lwam, endiloyikayo,Kuba izigwebo zakho zilungile.
40  Khangela! Ndiyilangazelele imiyalelo yakho.Ndigcine ndiphila ngobulungisa bakho.
41  Ngamana ububele bakho bothando bungeza kum, Yehova,Usindiso lwakho ngokwelizwi lakho,
42  Ukuze ndimphendule ngelizwi lowo undingcikivayo,Kuba ndikholose ngelizwi lakho.
43  Kwaye musa ukulisusa emlonyeni wam ngokupheleleyo ilizwi lenyaniso,Kuba ndilindele izigwebo zakho.
44  Ndiza kuwugcina rhoqo umthetho wakho,Ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, ewe ngonaphakade.
45  Ndiza kuhambahamba kwindawo ebanzi,Kuba ndiyifunile imiyalelo yakho.
46  Ndiza kuthetha ngezikhumbuzo zakho phambi kookumkani,Andiyi kuba nazintloni.
47  Ndiya kubonisa ukuyithanda imiyalelo yakhoLeyo ndiyithandayo.
48  Ndiya kuyiphakamisela izandla zam imiyalelo yakho endiyithandayo,Kwaye ndiza kuzixhalabisa ngemimiselo yakho.
49  Khumbula ilizwi kumkhonzi wakho,Elo undenze ndalilindela.
50  Yiyo le intuthuzelo yam kwinkxwaleko endikuyo,Kuba ilizwi lakho lindigcine ndiphila.
51  Abakhukhumeleyo baye bandigculela ngokugqithileyo.Andiphambukanga emthethweni wakho.
52  Ndizikhumbule izigwebo zakho ukususela kwixesha elingenammiselo, Yehova,Yaye ndizifumanela intuthuzelo.
53  Ndibanjwe kukuvutha ngumsindo ngenxa yabangendawo,Abawushiyayo umthetho wakho.
54  Imimiselo yakho iye yaba luncuthu lweengoma kumEndlwini yokuhlala kwam njengomphambukeli.
55  Ebusuku ndilikhumbule igama lakho, Yehova,Ukuze ndigcine umthetho wakho.
56  Nako oku kuye kwaba kokwam,Ngenxa yokuba ndiyigcinile imiyalelo yakho.
57  UYehova sisabelo sam;Ndithembise ukuwagcina amazwi akho.
58  Ndikubongozile ngayo yonke intliziyo yam.Ndibabale ngokwelizwi lakho.
59  Ndiziqwalasele iindlela zam,Ukuze ndibe nokubuyisela iinyawo zam kwizikhumbuzo zakho.
60  Ndikhawulezile, andalibazisaUkugcina imiyalelo yakho.
61  Zona kanye iintsontelo zabangendawo zindingqongile.Umthetho wakho andiwulibalanga.
62  Ezinzulwini zobusuku ndiyavuka ndibulele kuweNgenxa yezigwebo zakho zobulungisa.
63  Ndiliqabane labo bonke abo bakoyikayo,Nelabo bagcina imiyalelo yakho.
64  Ububele bakho bothando, Yehova, buzalise umhlaba.Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.
65  Eneneni uqhubene kakuhle nomkhonzi wakho,Yehova, ngokwelizwi lakho.
66  Ndifundise ukulunga, ingqiqo nokwazi,Kuba ndibonise ukholo kwimiyalelo yakho.
67  Phambi kokuba ndixhwaleke ndandisona ngempazamo,Kodwa ngoku ndigcine ilizwi lakho.
68  Ulungile yaye wenza okulungileyo.Ndifundise imiyalelo yakho.
69  Abakhukhumeleyo bandidyobhe ngobuxoki.Mna ke, ndiya kuyigcina imiyalelo yakho ngentliziyo yam yonke.
70  Intliziyo yabo ayinamvakalelo kanye njengamanqatha.Mna ke ndiwuthandile umthetho wakho.
71  Kundilungele okokuba ndiye ndaxhwaleka,Ukuze ndifunde imimiselo yakho.
72  Ulungile kum umthetho womlomo wakho,Ulunge ngakumbi kunamawaka amaqhosha egolide nesilivere.
73  Izandla zakho zindenzile, zandilungisa ngokuqinileyo.Ndiqondise, ukuze ndifunde imiyalelo yakho.
74  Abo bakoyikayo ngabo abaya kundibona baze babe nemihlali,Kuba ndilindele ilizwi lakho.
75  Ndazi kakuhle, Yehova, ukuba izigwebo zakho zibubulungisaNokuba undixhwalekise ngokuthembeka.
76  Ngamana ububele bakho bothando, bunganceda bunithuthuzele,Ngokwelizwi lakho kumkhonzi wakho.
77  Iinceba zakho mazize kum, ukuze ndiqhubeke ndiphila;Kuba ndiyawuthanda umthetho wakho.
78  Abakhukhumeleyo mababe neentloni, kuba baye bandilahlekisa ngaphandle kwesizathu.Mna ke, ndizixhalabisa ngemiyalelo yakho.
79  Abo bakoyikayo mababuyele kum,Nabo bazaziyo izikhumbuzo zakho.
80  Intliziyo yam mayingqineke ingenasiphoso kwimimiselo yakho,Ukuze ndingabi neentloni.
81  Umphefumlo wam ulangazelela usindiso lwakho;Ndilindele ilizwi lakho.
82  Amehlo am alangazelela ilizwi lakho,Ngoxa ndisithi: “Uya kundithuthuzela nini na?”
83  Kuba ndiye ndanjengentsuba emsini.Imimiselo yakho andiyilibalanga.
84  Zingaphi na iintsuku zomkhonzi wakho?Uya kuwuphumeza nini na umgwebo kwabo banditshutshisayo?
85  Abakhukhumeleyo bandimbele imigibe ukuze bandifumane,Abo bangavumelaniyo nomthetho wakho.
86  Yonke imiyalelo yakho ikukuthembeka.Banditshutshisile ngaphandle kwesizathu. Khawundincede.
87  Ngethuba elincinane ngebenditshabalalisile emhlabeni;Kodwa mna andiyishiyanga imiyalelo yakho.
88  Ngokobubele bakho bothando ndigcine ndiphila,Ukuze ndigcine isikhumbuzo somlomo wakho.
89  Ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, Yehova,Ilizwi lakho limile emazulwini.
90  Ukuthembeka kwakho kukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.Uwuzinzise ngokuqinileyo umhlaba, ukuze uqhubeke umile.
91  Ngokwezigwebo zakho ezo zinto zimile kude kube namhlanje,Kuba zonke zingabakhonzi bakho.
92  Ukuba bendingawuthandi umthetho wakho,Ngoko ngenditshabalele kwinkxwaleko yam.
93  Andiyi kuyilibala imiyalelo yakho kude kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo,Ngenxa yokuba undigcine ndiphila ngayo.
94  Ndingowakho, khawundisindise,Ngenxa yokuba ndiyifunile imiyalelo yakho.
95  Abangendawo bandilindele, ukuze banditshabalalise.Ndiyaqhubeka ndinikela ingqalelo kwizikhumbuzo zakho.
96  Ndisibonile isiphelo sako konke ukugqibelela.Umyalelo wakho ubanzi kakhulu.
97  Hayi indlela endiwuthanda ngayo umthetho wakho!Imini le yonke ndiwuxhalabele.
98  Umyalelo wakho undenza ndilumke ngakumbi kuneentshaba zam,Ngenxa yokuba ngowam ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
99  Ndiye ndaba nengqiqo ngakumbi kunabafundisi bam bonke,Ngenxa yokuba ndixhalabele izikhumbuzo zakho.
100  Ndiziphatha ngokuqonda ngakumbi kunamadoda amakhulu,Ngenxa yokuba ndiyigcinile imiyalelo yakho.
101  Ndizithintele iinyawo zam kuwo wonke umendo wobubi,Ngenjongo yokuba ndigcine ilizwi lakho.
102  Andiphambukanga kwizigwebo zakho,Kuba wena undiyalele.
103  Hayi indlela agude ngayo amazwi akho enkalakahleni yam,Agude ngakumbi kunobusi emlonyeni wam!
104  Ngenxa yemiyalelo yakho ndiziphatha ngokuqonda.Kungenxa yoko le nto ndiwuthiyile wonke umendo wobuxoki.
105  Ilizwi lakho lisisibane elunyaweni lwam,Nokukhanya endleleni yam.
106  Ndenze isifungo, yaye ndiza kusigcina,Ukuba ndigcine izigwebo zakho zobulungisa.
107  Ndixhwaleke ngokomkhamo omkhulu.Owu Yehova, ndigcine ndiphila ngokwelizwi lakho.
108  Nceda uyoliswe yiminikelo yokuzithandela yomlomo wam, Yehova,Uze undifundise izigwebo zakho.
109  Umphefumlo wam usentendeni yam rhoqo;Kodwa umthetho wakho andiwulibalanga.
110  Abangendawo bandibekele isibatha,Kodwa andibhadulanga emiyalelweni yakho.
111  Ndizidle ilifa izikhumbuzo zakho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo,Kuba zikukugcoba kwentliziyo yam.
112  Intliziyo yam ndiyithobele ekwenzeni imimiselo yakhoUkusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, kude kuse ekupheleni.
113  Abantliziyo imbaxa ndibathiyile,Kodwa umthetho wakho ndiwuthandile.
114  Uyindawo yam yokuzifihla nekhaka lam.Ndilindele ilizwi lakho.
115  Mkani kum, nina benzi-bubi,Ukuze ndigcine imiyalelo kaThixo wam.
116  Ndixhase ngokwelizwi lakho, ukuze ndiqhubeke ndiphila,Ungandihlazisi ngethemba lam.
117  Ndixhase, ukuze ndisindiswe,Yaye ndiya kondela imimiselo yakho rhoqo.
118  Ubalahlile bonke abo balahlekayo emimiselweni yakho;Kuba inkohliso yabo ibubuxoki.
119  Ubaphelisile bonke abangendawo bomhlaba njengentlenge.Ngoko ke ndizithandile izikhumbuzo zakho.
120  Inyama yam iye yankwantya ngokunkwantyiswa kuwe;Nangenxa yezigwebo zakho ndiye ndoyika.
121  Ndiphumeze umgwebo nobulungisa.Musa ukundinikela kwabo bandiqhathayo!
122  Yiba ngummeli womkhonzi wakho ngenxa yokulungileyo.Ngamana abakhukhumeleyo bangangandiqhathi.
123  Wona kanye amehlo am alangazelela usindiso lwakhoNelizwi lakho lobulungisa.
124  Yenza kumkhonzi wakho ngokobubele bakho bothando,Undifundise imimiselo yakho.
125  Ndingumkhonzi wakho. Ndiqondise,Ukuze ndizazi izikhumbuzo zakho.
126  Lixesha lokuba uYehova asebenze.Bawaphule umthetho wakho.
127  Kungenxa yoko le nto ndiyithandile imiyalelo yakhoNgaphezu kwegolide, ewe, igolide esulungekisiweyo.
128  Kungenxa yoko le nto ndiyigqale njengelungileyo yonke imiyalelo yazo zonke izinto;Wonke umendo wobuxoki ndiwuthiyile.
129  Izikhumbuzo zakho ziyamangalisa.Kungenxa yoko le nto umphefumlo wam uzigcinile.
130  Kona kanye ukutyhila kwamazwi akho kunika ukukhanya,Kuqondisa abangenamava.
131  Ndiwuvule wabanzi umlomo wam, ukuze ndikhefuzele,Ngenxa yokuba ndiyilangazelele imiyalelo yakho.
132  Jikela kum, undibabale,Ngokwesigwebo sakho kwabo bathanda igama lakho.
133  Wazinzise ngokuqinileyo amanyathelo am elizwini lakho,Yaye ngamana ndingangalawulwa lulo naluphi na uhlobo lwento eyenzakalisayo.
134  Ndikhulule kuye nabani na oqhathayo woluntu,Kwaye ndiza kuzigcina imimiselo yakho.
135  Khanyisa ubuso bakho kumkhonzi wakho,Undifundise imimiselo yakho.
136  Kuhla imisinga yamanzi emehlweni amNgenxa yokuba abawugcinanga umthetho wakho.
137  Ulilungisa, Yehova,Nezigwebo zakho zithe tye.
138  Uyalele izikhumbuzo zakho ngobulungisaNangokuthembeka okugqithiseleyo.
139  Ikhwele lam lindigqibile,Ngenxa yokuba iintshaba zam ziwalibele amazwi akho.
140  Ilizwi lakho lisulungekisiwe kakhulu,Yaye umkhonzi wakho uyalithanda.
141  Andibalulekanga yaye ndidelekile.Imiyalelo yakho andiyilibalanga.
142  Ubulungisa bakho bubulungisa ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo,Nomthetho wakho uyinyaniso.
143  Ukubandezeleka nobunzima bandifumana.Imiyalelo yakho ndayithanda.
144  Ubulungisa bezikhumbuzo zakho bukho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.Ndiqondise, ukuze ndiqhubeke ndiphila.
145  Ndibize ngentliziyo yam iphela. Ndiphendule, Yehova.Imimiselo yakho ndiza kuyigcina.
146  Ndibize kuwe. Khawundisindise!Yaye ndiza kuzigcina izikhumbuzo zakho.
147  Ndivuke kwangoko ekuzeni kokusa, ukuze ndikhalele uncedo.Ndilindele amazwi akho.
148  Amehlo am ayandulele imilindo yasebusuku,Ukuze ndizixhalabise ngelizwi lakho.
149  Live ilizwi lam ngokobubele bakho bothando.Owu Yehova, ndigcine ndiphila ngokwesigwebo sakho.
150  Abo basukela ihambo evakalala basondele;Bashenxele kude emthethweni wakho.
151  Ukufuphi, Yehova,Yaye yonke imiyalelo yakho iyinyaniso.
152  Kwakudala bendizazi ezinye zezikhumbuzo zakho,Kuba waziseka kwixesha elingenammiselo.
153  Khawubone inkxwaleko yam, undihlangule;Kuba andiwulibalanga umthetho wakho.
154  Khawuchophele ityala lam uze undihlangule;Ndigcine ndiphila ngokuvumelana nelizwi lakho.
155  Usindiso lukude kwabo bangendawo,Kuba abayifunanga imimiselo yakho.
156  Zininzi iinceba zakho, Yehova.Ngokwezigwebo zakho, ndigcine ndiphila.
157  Baninzi abatshutshisi bam neentshaba zam.Andiphambukanga kwizikhumbuzo zakho.
158  Ndibabonile abo benza ngobuqhophololo,Yaye ndiziva ndizothekile, ngenxa yokuba abaligcinanga ilizwi lakho.
159  Khawubone ukuba ndiyithandile imiyalelo yakho.Owu Yehova, ndigcine ndiphila ngokobubele bakho bothando.
160  Lonke ilizwi lakho liyinyaniso,Nazo zonke izigwebo zakho zikho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
161  Iinkosana zinditshutshisile ngaphandle kwesizathu,Kodwa intliziyo yam inkwantyiswa ngamazwi akho.
162  Ndiyagcoba ngelizwi lakhoKanye njengoko ubani esenjenjalo akufumana amaxhoba amaninzi.
163  Ndibuthiyile ubuxoki, yaye ndiyaqhubeka ndibucekisa.Umthetho wakho ndiwuthandile.
164  Ndikudumise izihlandlo ezisixhenxe ngosukuNgenxa yezigwebo zakho zobulungisa.
165  Uxolo oluninzi lolwabo bathanda umthetho wakho,Yaye kubo akukho mqobo usisikhubekiso.
166  Ndithembe usindiso lwakho, Yehova,Ndiyenzile imiyalelo yakho.
167  Umphefumlo wam uzigcinile izikhumbuzo zakho,Kwaye ndizithanda ngokugqithiseleyo.
168  Ndiyigcinile imiyalelo yakho nezikhumbuzo zakho,Kuba zonke iindlela zam ziphambi kwakho.
169  Ngamana isikhalo sam sokubongoza singasondela phambi kwakho, Yehova.Ngokwelizwi lakho, khawundiqondise.
170  Ngamana ukucela kwam ubabalo kungangena phambi kwakho.Ngokwelizwi lakho, khawundihlangule.
171  Ngamana imilebe yam ingampompoza indumiso,Kuba undifundisa imimiselo yakho.
172  Ngamana ulwimi lwam lungavuma ilizwi lakho,Kuba yonke imiyalelo yakho ibubulungisa.
173  Ngamana isandla sakho singandinceda,Ngenxa yokuba ndinyule imiyalelo yakho.
174  Ndilangazelele usindiso lwakho, Yehova,Nomthetho wakho ndiyawuthanda.
175  Ngamana umphefumlo wam ungaqhubeka uphila yaye ukudumisa,Kwaye ngamana izigwebo zakho zingandinceda.
176  Ndiye ndabhadula njengemvu elahlekileyo. Khawumkhangele umkhonzi wakho,Kuba andiyilibalanga imiyalelo yakho.
141  Owu Yehova, ndibize kuwe.Khawuleza uze kum.Libekele indlebe ilizwi lam ekubizeni kwam kuwe.
2  Ngamana umthandazo wam ungalungiselelwa njengempepho phambi kwakho,Ukuphakanyiswa kwezandla zam zam kube njengomnikelo wokudla okuziinkozo wangokuhlwa.
3  Wubekele umlindi, Yehova, umlomo wam;Wubekele umlindi umnyango wemilebe yam.
4  Intliziyo yam musa ukuyithobela nantoni na embi,Ukuba iqhubeke nezenzo ezibi ngobungendawoKunye nabantu abaqhelisela okwenzakalisayo,Ukuze ndingadli izinto zabo ezimnandi.
5  Ukuba ilungisa lingandibetha, bekuya kuba bububele bothando obo;Yaye ukuba lingandohlwaya, bekuya kuba yioli oko entloko,Nto leyo intloko yam ibingayi kufuna ukuyala.Kuba bekusaya kubakho umthandazo wam nasebudeni beentlekele zabo.
6  Abagwebi babo baphoswe phantsi emacaleni engxondorha,Kodwa bawavile amazwi am, ukuba ayathandeka.

2  Masize phambi kwakhe sinombulelo;Masidume ngoloyiso kuye ngoncuthu lwengoma.

139  Owu Yehova, undigocagocile, yaye uyandazi.
2  Wena uyakwazi ukuhlala kwam nokuvuka kwam.Uziqwalasele iingcamango zam ukude.
3  Ukuhamba kwam nokulala kwam ndinabile ukulinganisile,Kwaye uye waqhelana nazo zonke iindlela zam.
4  Kuba akukho lizwi elulwimini lwam,Kodwa, khangela! Owu Yehova, sele ukwazi konke.
5  Ngasemva nangaphambili, undingqingile;Yaye ubeka isandla sakho phezu kwam.

8  Ukuba ndinganyukela ezulwini, ubuya kuba lapho;Nokuba ndingandlala isingqengqelo sam eShiyol, khangela! ubuya kuba lapho.

13  Kuba wena wavelisa izintso zam;Wandibiyela esiswini sikama.

18  Ukuba bendingazama ukuzibala, zininzi ngakumbi kunentlabathi.Ndivukile, ukanti ndisekunye nawe.

20  Abathetha izinto ngawe ngokwengcinga yabo;Bathabathe igama lakho ngendlela engento yanto—iintshaba zakho.

19  Amazulu avakalisa uzuko lukaThixo;Yaye isibhakabhaka sixela umsebenzi wezandla zakhe.
2  Usuku emva kolunye usuku lubangela ukumpompoza kwentetho,Yaye ubusuku emva kobunye ubusuku bubonakalisa ulwazi.
3  Akukho ntetho, yaye akukho mazwi;Aliviwa ilizwi lawo.
4  Ulutya lwawo lokulinganisa luphume lwaya emhlabeni wonke,Namazwi awo aya esiphelweni somhlaba onemveliso.Ulimisele kuwo ilanga intente,
5  Kwaye lifana nomyeni xa ephuma egumbini lakhe lomsitho womtshato;Ligcoba njengokuba isenza indoda enamandla ukuze ibaleke emendweni.

7  Umthetho kaYehova ugqibelele, ubuyisa umphefumlo.Isikhumbuzo sikaYehova sikholosekile, simenza abe nobulumko ongenamava.

2  Ndiza kwenza ngokunengqiqo ngendlela engenasiphoso.Uya kuza nini na kum?Ndiya kuhamba ngengqibelelo yentliziyo yam ngaphakathi endlwini yam.

4  Intliziyo egwenxa iyemka kum;Into embi andiyazi.
5  Nabani na onyelisa iqabane lakhe emfihlekweni,Yena ndiyamthulisa.Nabani na onamehlo anekratshi nonentliziyo ekhukhumeleyo,Yena andinakumnyamezela.
6  Amehlo am akwabo bathembekileyo bomhlaba,Ukuba bahlale kunye nam.Ohamba ngendlela engenasiphoso,Nguye oya kuba ngumlungiseleli wam.
7  Akayi kuhlala ngaphakathi endlwini yam umsebénzi wenkohliso.Yena ke nabani na othetha ubuxoki, akayi kumiselwa ngokuqinileyoPhambi kwamehlo am.
8  Ntsasa nganye ndiya kubathulisa abo bangendawo bomhlaba,Ukuze ndibanqumle esixekweni sikaYehova bonke abo baqhelisela okwenzakalisayo.
44  Owu Thixo, sivile ngeendlebe zethu,Ookhokho bethu basibaliseleUmsebenzi owawenzayo ngemihla yabo,Ngemihla yakudala.
2  Wena wazigxotha iintshaba ngesandla sakho,Waza esikhundleni soko wabatyala.Wawaphula amaqela eentlanga waza wawandulula.
3  Kuba abazange balidle ilifa ilizwe ngenxa yekrele labo,Yaye babengasindiswanga yingalo yabo.Kuba kwakungesandla sakho sokunene nengalo yakho nokukhanya kobuso bakho,Kuba wakholiswa ngabo.
4  Wena unguKumkani wam, Thixo.Yalela usindiso oluzukileyo kuYakobi.
5  Ngawe siya kuzityhala iintshaba zethu;Egameni lakho siya kubanyathela abo basivukelayo.
6  Kuba andizange ndiqhubeke ndikholose ngesaphetha samYaye asilokrele lam elalindisindisa.
7  Kuba wasisindisa kwiintshaba zethu,Nabo basithiye kakhulu wabahlazisa.
8  Siya kumdumisa uThixo imini yonke,Yaye ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo siya kubonga igama lakho. Seʹlah
9  Kodwa ngoku usilahlile yaye uqhubeka usithoba,Ibe akuphumi nemikhosi yethu.
10  Uqhubeka usenza sijike phambi kotshaba,Kanye abo basithiya kakhulu basiphangile.
11  Usiyekela njengezimvu, njengento edliwayo,Kwaye usisasazile phakathi kweentlanga.
12  Abantu bakho akubathengisi ngexabiso,Yaye akuzuzanga ndyebo ngexabiso labo.
13  Usimisa njengongcikivo kubamelwane bethu,Njengento yokugxekwa nokugculelwa kwabo basijikelezileyo.
14  Usimisa njengomzekelo phakathi kweentlanga,Abokuhlunguzelelwa intloko phakathi kwamaqela eentlanga.
15  Ukuthotywa kwam kuphambi kwam imini yonke,Nehlazo lobuso bam lindigubungele,
16  Ngenxa yelizwi lalowo ungcikivayo notshabhisayo,Ngenxa yotshaba nalowo uziphindezelelayo.
17  Konke oku koko kusifikeleyo, yaye asikulibalanga,Yaye asenzanga ngobuxoki kumnqophiso wakho.
18  Intliziyo yethu ayibuyanga umva ngokungabi nalukholo,Namanyathelo ethu akaphambuki emendweni wakho.
19  Kuba usityumzele endaweni yoodyakalashe,Yaye usigubungela ngethunzi elimnyama.
20  Ukuba sililibele igama loThixo wethu,Okanye sazolulela kuthixo wumbi izandla zethu,
21  Ngaba uThixo akayi kukufuna oku?Kuba uyaziqonda iimfihlelo zentliziyo.
22  Kodwa ngenxa yakho sibulewe imini yonke;Sigqalwe njengezimvu zokuxhelwa.
23  Zivuselele. Ulaleleni na Yehova?Vuka. Musa ukusilahla ngonaphakade.
24  Kutheni na uqhubeka ubufihlile ubuso bakho?Kutheni ukulibala ukuxhwaleka kwethu nengcinezelo yethu?

26  Vuka usincedeUsikhulule ngenxa yobubele bakho bothando.
47  Qhwabani izandla, nonke zizwana.Dumani ngoloyiso kuThixo ngesandi sentswahla yovuyo.
2  Kuba uYehova, ongOyena Uphakamileyo, uyoyikeka,UKumkani omkhulu emhlabeni wonke.
3  Uya kuzithobela ngaphantsi kwethu izizwanaNamaqela eentlanga ngaphantsi kweenyawo zethu.
4  Uya kusinyulela ilifa lethu,Iqhayiya likaYakobi, amthandileyo. Seʹlah.
5  UThixo unyukile ngemikhwazo yovuyo,UYehova ngesandi sesigodlo.
6  Mculeleni uncuthu lwengoma uThixo, mculeleni uncuthu lwengoma.Mculeleni uncuthu lwengoma uKumkani wethu, mculeleni uncuthu lwengoma.

88  Owu Yehova, THIXO wosindiso lwam,Emini ndiye ndadanduluka kuwe,nasebusuku phambi kwakho.
2  Uza phambi kwakho umthandazo wakho.Kuthobele indlebe ukukhala kwam ndibongoza.
3  Umphefumlo wam wanele ziintlekele,Yaye ubomi bam bufikile eShiyol.
4  Ndibalwa phakathi kwabo behla baye emhadini;Ndinjengendoda eyomeleleyo engenamandla,
5  Ndikhululekile phakathi kwabafileyo,Njengababuleweyo abalele kwindawo yokungcwaba,OngasabakhumbuliyoNabahluliweyo kwisandla sakho esiluncedo.
6  Undibeke emhadini enzulwini,Kwiindawo ezimnyama, kwinzonzobila enkulu.
7  Umsindo wakho undihlasele,Yaye ngamaza akho undixhwalekisile mna. Seʹlah.
8  Ubashenxisele kude kum abandiqhelileyo;Undibeke ndayinto ecekisekayo kubo.Ndithintelekile yaye andinakuya phambili.
9  Iliso lam lidangele ngenxa yokuxhwaleka kwam.Owu Yehova, imini yonke ndikubizile;Izandla zam ndizolulele kuwe.
10  Uya kubenzela na abo bafileyo into emangalisayo?Okanye baya kuvuka na abo bangenamandla ekufeni,Baya kukubonga na? Seʹlah.
11  Buya kuvakaliswa kwindawo yokungcwaba na ububele bakho bothando,Ukuthembeka kwakho kwindawo yentshabalalo na?
12  Uya kwaziwa na ebumnyameni ummangaliso wakho,Okanye ubulungisa bakho kwilizwe lokulibala na?
13  Ukanti mna ke, Yehova, ndikhale kuwe ndicela uncedo,Nakusasa umthandazo wam uyakuhlangabeza.
14  Kutheni na, Yehova, ukuze ulahle umphefumlo wam?Kutheni na wamana ubufihla ubuso bakho kum?
15  Ndixhwalekile, ndingosele eza kubhubha ukususela ebukhwenkweni bam kuse phambili;Ndithwele izinto ezothusa kakhulu ezivela kuwe.
16  Ukuvutha komsindo wakho kudlule phezu kwam;Unkwantyo lwakho lundenze ndathi cwaka.
17  Lundingqongile njengamanzi imini yonke;Zindivingcele zonke ngaxeshanye.
18  Umshenxisele kude kum umhlobo neqabane;Abo ndibaqhelileyo bayindawo emnyama.
48  UYehova mkhulu yaye ngowokudunyiswa kakhuluKwisixeko soThixo wethu, entabeni yakhe engcwele.
2  Intle ukuphakama kwayo, ugcoba ngayo wonke umhlaba,INtaba yeZiyon kumacala athe qelele asentla,Idolophu yoKumkani Ozukileyo.
3  Kwiinqaba zayo zokuhlala uThixo waziwa njengendawo ephakamileyo enqabisekileyo.
4  Kuba, khangela! ookumkani bahlanganisene ngedinga,Badlule kunye.
5  Babonile; baza bathi manga.Baphazamiseka, babaleka ngokuphakuzela.
6  Bafikelwe kukungcangcazela,Inimba efana naleyo yomfazi ozalayo.

8  Kanye njengokuba sivile, sibonileKwisixeko sikaYehova wemikhosi, kwisixeko soThixo wethu.UThixo uya kusimisela ngokuqinileyo ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo. Seʹlah.
9  Sibuphononongile, Thixo, ububele bakho bothandoPhakathi etempileni yakho.

14  Kuba lo Thixo nguThixo wethu ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo, nangonaphakade.Yena uya kusikhokela de sife.
59  Ndihlangule kwiintshaba zam, Thixo wam;Kwabo bandivukelayo ngamana ungandikhusela.
2  Ndihlangule kwabo baqhelisela okwenzakalisayo,Nakumadoda anetyala legazi ndisindise.

6  Bayaqhubeka bebuya ngokuhlwa;Baqhubeka bekhonkotha njengenja baze bajikeleze isixeko.
7  Khangela! Bayampompoza ngomlomo wabo;Emilebeni yabo kukho amakrele,Kuba ngubani na ophulaphuleyo?
8  Kodwa wena, Yehova, uya kubahleka;Uya kuzigculela zonke iintlanga.
9  Owu Mandla am, ndiya kulinda kuwe;Kuba uThixo yindawo yam ephakamileyo enqabisekileyo.
10  UTHIXO wobubele bothando kum uya kundikhawulela;UThixo uya kundibangela ndikhangele iintshaba zam.
11  Musa ukubabulala, ukuze abantu bam bangalibali.Ngamandla akho benze babhadule,Ubahlise, khaka lethu Yehova,

13  Baphelise ngomsindo;Baphelise, ukuze bangabikho;Yaye ngamana bangazi ukuba uThixo ulawula kwaYakobi ukusa eziphelweni zomhlaba. Seʹlah.
14  Baze babuye ngokuhlwa;Bakhonkothe njengenja bajikekeleze isixeko.

107  Bulelani kuYehova, kuba ulungile;Kuba ububele bakhe bothando bukho ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo.
2  Mabatsho njalo abo bahlangulweyo nguYehova,Abo abahlanguleyo esandleni sotshaba,
3  Nabo abaqokelele ndawonye bevela emazweni,Empumalanga nasentshonalanga,Emntla nasemzantsi.

15  Abantu mabambulele uYehova ngobubele bakhe bothandoNangemisebenzi yakhe emangalisayo koonyana babantu.

18  Umphefumlo wabo wacekisa lonke uhlobo lokutya,Yaye babefika emasangweni okufa.

26  Benyuka baye emazulwini,Bayehla baye emazantsi.Ngenxa yentlekele wona kanye umphefumlo wabo uzifumana unyibilika.

31  Abantu mabambulele uYehova ngobubele bakhe bothandoNangemisebenzi yakhe emangalisayo koonyana babantu.
32  Mabambonge ebandleni labantu;Mabamdumise kwindawo yokuhlala yamadoda akhulileyo.

74  Kutheni, Thixo, usilahle ngonaphakade?Kutheni umsindo wakho uqhubeka uvutha emhlambini wedlelo lakho?
2  Yikhumbule indibano yakho owayizuza kudala,Isizwe owasikhulula njengelifa lakho,Le Ntaba yaseZiyon ohlala kuyo.
3  Phakamisa amanyathelo akho uye kwiziphanziso ezihlala zihleli.Yonke into utshaba oluyiphathe kakubi endaweni engcwele.
4  Abo babonisa ubutshaba kuwe bayagquma phakathi endaweni yokuhlangana.Bamisele eyabo imiqondiso njengemiqondiso.
5  Udume kakubi lowo unjengalowo uphakamisela intshinyela yemithi izembe.
6  Ngoku ke kwanemikrolo yalo, xa iyonke, bayixabela ngezenjana nomqadi onencam yentsimbi.
7  Ingcwele yakho bayifake emlilweni.Umnquba wegama lakho bawuhlambele emhlabeni.

9  Imiqondiso yethu asiyibonanga; akusekho mprofeti,Kuthi akukho bani waziyo ukuba kuya kude kube nini na.
10  Kuya kude kube nini na, Thixo, utshaba luqhubeka lungcikiva?Ngaba utshaba luya kuqhubeka luliphatha ngokungenantlonelo ngonaphakade igama lakho?

14  Wena uzityumze zaziingceba iintloko zeLeviyatan.Waza wayinika abantu njengokutya, abo bahleli kwimimandla enamanzi.
15  Nguwe owahlukanisa umthombo nomsinga;Wena womisa imilambo engatshiyo.
16  Yeyakho imini; nobusuku bobakho.Nguwe owalungiselela isikhanyiso, kwanelanga.
17  Yayinguwe owamisela yonke imida yomhlaba;Ihlobo nobusika—nguwe owazenzayo.
18  Khumbula oku: Utshaba lungcikivile, Yehova,Nabantu abangenangqiqo baliphathe ngokungenantlonelo igama lakho.
19  Musa ukuwunikela kwirhamncwa umphefumlo wehobe lasendle.Musa ukubulibala ubomi babo baxhwalekileyo bakho.
20  Wukhangele umnqophiso,Kuba iindawo ezimnyama zomhlaba zizaliswe ziindawo zokuhlala zogonyamelo.
21  Owu kwanga lowo utyunyuziweyo akangebuyi ethotyiwe.Kwanga lowo uxhwalekileyo nalowo ulihlwempu bangalidumisa igama lakho.
22  Sukuma, Thixo, sichophele isimangalo sakho.Kukhumbule ukungcikivwa kwakho ngulowo ungenangqiqo imini yonke.
23  Ungalilibali ilizwi labo babonisa ubutshaba kuwe.Ingxolo yabo bakuvukelayo iyenyuka rhoqo.
5  Wabekele indlebe amazwi am, Yehova;Kuqonde ukuncwina kwam.
2  Nikela ingqalelo kwisandi sokukhalela kwam uncedo,Kumkani wam noThixo wam, ngenxa yokuba ndithandaza kuwe.
3  Owu Yehova, kusasa uya kuliva ilizwi lam;Kusasa ndiya kubhekisa kuwe ndize ndilinde.
4  Kuba akungoThixo oyoliswayo bubungendawo;Akukho namnye onobubi onokuhlala nexeshana nawe.
5  Akukho mqhayisi unokuma phambi kwamehlo akho.Ubathiyile bonke abo baqhelisela okwenzakalisayo;
6  Uya kubatshabalalisa abo bathetha ubuxoki.Umntu ophalaza igazi nonenkohliso uYehova uyamcekisa.
7  Ke mna, ngobubele bakho obunothando obuninziNdiya kungena endlwini yakho,Ndiya kuqubuda etempileni yakho engcwele ngenxa yokoyika wena.

9  Kuba emlonyeni wabo akukho nto kunokukholoswa ngayo;Umbilini wabo yinkxwaleko ngokwenene.Umqala wabo yindawo yokungcwaba evulekileyo;Basebenzisa ulwimi olugudileyo.
10  UThixo uya kubagqala njengabanetyala ngokuqinisekileyo;Baya kuwa ngenxa yecebo labo.Ngobuninzi bokunxaxha kwabo mabasasazwe,Ngenxa yokuba bakuvukele.
11  Kodwa bonke abo basabela kuwe baya kuba nemihlali;Baya kumemelela ngovuyo kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo.Uya kuyithintela indlela esondela kubo,Yaye abo bathanda igama lakho baya kugcoba ngawe.
12  Kuba uya kumsikelela nabani na olilungisa, Yehova;Ngokungathi kungekhaka elikhulu, uya kubangqonga ngenkoliseko.
36  Ilizwi lokunxaxha kulowo ungendawo liphakathi entliziyweni yakhe;Ukoyika uThixo akukho phambi kwamehlo akhe.
2  Kuba wenze ngokugudileyo kakhulu emehlweni akheUkuze afumane isiphoso sakhe ukuze asithiye.

79  Owu Thixo, iintlanga zingene kwilifa lakho;Ziyenze inqambi itempile yakho engcwele;IYerusalem ziyenze imfumba yamanxuwa.
2  Isidumbu sabakhonzi bakho basinikele kwiintaka zamazulu njengokudla,Inyama yabanyanisekileyo bakho bayinika amarhamncwa omhlaba.

150  Dumisani uYa!Dumisani uThixo endaweni yakhe engcwele.Mdumiseni esibhakabhakeni samandla akhe.
2  Mdumiseni ngenxa yemisebenzi yakhe yamandla.Mdumiseni ngokobuninzi bobukhulu bakhe.

75  Siyakubulela, Thixo; siyakubulela,Negama lakho likufuphi.Abantu bamele bavakalise imisebenzi yakho emangalisayo.

61  Owu Thixo, sive isikhalo sam sokubongoza.Nikela ingqalelo kumthandazo wam.
2  Ndiya kukhala ndisesiphelweni somhlaba, kuwe, xa intliziyo yamisiba buthathaka.Ngamana ungandikhokelela eliweni eliphakame ngakumbi kunam.

103  Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam,Nayo yonk’ into engaphakathi kwam, igama lakhe elingcwele.
2  Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam,Ungakulibali ukwenza kwakhe konke,
3  Yena oxolela sonke isiphoso sakho,Ophilisa zonke izifo zakho,
4  Ohlangula ubomi bakho emhadini,Okuthwesa ububele bothando neenceba,

13  Njengoyise obenzela inceba oonyana bakhe,UYehova ubenzele inceba abo bamoyikayo.
14  Kuba yena uyakwazi ukuyilwa kwethu,Ekhumbula ukuba siluthuli.
15  Yena ke umntu ofayo, imihla yakhe injengaleyo yengca eluhlaza;Indlela atyatyamba ngayo injengeyentyatyambo yasendle.

41  Unoyolo nabani na onikela ingqalelo kwisisweli;Ngomhla wentlekele uYehova uya kumsindisa.
2  UYehova uya kumlinda amgcine ephila.Uya kubhengezwa enoyolo emhlabeni;Yaye akunakumnikela emphefumlweni weentshaba zakhe.

5  Ke zona iintshaba zam, zithetha okubi ngam:“Uya kufa nini na negama lakhe litshabalale?”
6  Yaye ukuba ubani uyeza kundibona, intliziyo yakhe iya kuthetha okungeyonyaniso;Uya kuzibuthela into eyenzakalisayo;Uya kuphuma; athethe ngayo ngaphandle.

15  Owu Yehova, ngubani na oya kuba lundwendwe ententeni yakho?Ngubani na oya kuhlala entabeni yakho engcwele?
2  Ngulowo uhamba ngokungenasiphoso eqhelisela ubulungisaYaye ethetha inyaniso ngentliziyo yakhe.

20  Ngamana uYehova angakuphendula ngomhla wokubandezeleka.Ngamana igama loTHIXO kaYakobi lingakukhusela.

68  Makasukume uThixo, iintshaba zakhe mazichithachithwe,Abo bamthiye kakhulu mabasabe ngenxa yakhe.
2  Njengoko umsi uphetshethwa umke, ngamana ungabaphephetha bemke;Njengoko umthwebeba unyibilika ngenxa yomlilo,Mabatshabalale phambi koThixo abangendawo.
3  Ke bona abangamalungisa, mababe nemihlali,Mababe nochulumanco phambi koThixo,Bagcobe ngemihlali.
4  Mvumeleni uThixo, niliculele uncuthu lwengoma igama lakhe;Mculeleni ingoma Lowo ukhweleyo ehamba ethafeni eliyinkqantosiNgoYa, ligama lakhe elo; nize nigcobe phambi kwakhe;

10  Abantu bakho abahlala ezintenteni—baye bahlala kulo;Ngokulunga kwakho walilungiselela lowo uxhwalekileyo, Thixo.
11  NguYehova onikela eli lizwi;Abafazi abavakalisa iindaba ezilungileyo bangumkhosi omkhulu.
12  Kwanookumkani bemikhosi bayasaba, bayasaba.Ke yena lowo uhlala ekhaya, ufumana isabelo sexhoba.
13  Nangona naqhubeka nilele phakathi kweemfumba zothuthu ezisenkampini,Kuya kubakho amaphiko ehobe egqunywe ngesilivereNeentsiba zalo ngegolide eluhlaza bulubhelu.
14  Xa Lowo unguSomandla wabachithachitha ngokubanzi kulo ookumkani,Kwaqalisa ukuwa ikhephu eTsalmon.

18  Unyukele phezulu;Uthabathe abathinjwa;Uthabathe izipho ezingabantu,Ewe, kwanabo baneenkani, ukuze uhlale phakathi kwabo, wena Ya, Thixo.
19  Makabongwe uYehova osithwalela umthwalo mihla le,UTHIXO oyinyaniso wosindiso lwethu. Seʹlah.
20  UTHIXO oyinyaniso kuthi unguThixo wezenzo zokusindisa;Yaye zezikaYehova iNkosi enguMongami iindlela zokuphuma ekufeni.
21  Eneneni uThixo uya kuyiqhekeza intloko yeentshaba zakhe,Ukakayi lweenwele zentloko yakhe nabani na ohambahamba enetyala.
22  UYehova uthe: “Ndiya kubabuyisa eBhashan,Ndiya kubabuyisa ezinzulwini zolwandle,
23  Ukuze uluhlambe egazini unyawo lwakho,Ukuze ulwimi lwezinja zakho lufumane isabelo salo ezintshabeni.”
24  Bayibonile imingcelele yakho, Thixo,Imingcelele yoThixo wam, uKumkani wam, isiya endaweni engcwele.
25  Iimvumi zihamba phambili, emva kwazo ingabadlali bomrhubhe;Phakathi iziintombi ezibetha iintambula.
26  Mbongeni uThixo kwiindimbane ezihlanganiseneyo,Yehova, wena uphuma kuMthombo kaSirayeli.
27  Nanko uBhenjamin omncinane ezoyisa,Iinkosana zakwaYuda nesihlwele sazo esikhwazayo,Iinkosana zakwaZebhulon, neenkosana zakwaNafetali.
28  UThixo wakho uwabekele umyalelo amandla akho.Bonisa amandla, Thixo, wena usisebenzeleyo.
29  Ngenxa yetempile yakho eYerusalem,Ookumkani baya kukuzisela izipho.
30  Khalimela irhamncwa leengcongolo, indibano yeenkunzi zeenkomo,Ngamathole ezizwana, ngalinye linyathela amaqhosha esilivere.Uzichithachithile izizwana eziyoliswa yimilo.
31  Izinto ezenziwe ngobhedu ziya kufika zivela eYiputa;UKushe uya kukhawuleza olule isandla sakhe sinezipho zikaThixo.
32  Owu nina zikumkani zomhlaba, vumelani uThixo,Mculeleni uncuthu lwengoma uYehova—Seʹlah—
33  Lowo ukhwele izulu lamandulo lamazulu.Khangela! Uvakalisa ngelizwi lakhe, ilizwi elomeleleyo.
34  Mnikeni amandla uThixo.Ubuhandiba bakhe buphezu koSirayeli namandla akhe asemafini akhe.

2  Ngaphambi kokuba neentaba zizalwe,Okanye uzise ngokungathi kungenimba umhlaba nelizwe elinemveliso,Ukususela kwixesha elingenammiselo ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo wena unguThixo.
3  Umntu ofayo umbuyisela eluthulini,Kwaye uthi: “Buyani, nyana babantu.”
4  Kuba iminyaka eliwaka emehlweni akho injengemini yezolo xa idlulile,Nanjengomlindo ebudeni bobusuku.
5  Uye wabatshayela; baba bubuthongo nje;Kusasa banjengengca le itshintshayo.
6  Kusasa iyatyatyamba yaye imele itshintshe;Ngokuhlwa iyabuna ize ngokuqinisekileyo yome.
7  Kuba siyaphela ngumsindo wakho,Nangobushushu bakho siphazamisekile.
8  Ubeke iziphoso zethu kanye phambi kwethu,Izinto zethu ezifihlakeleyo phambi kobuso bethu obuqaqambileyo.
9  Kuba yonke imihla yethu ifikelele ekupheleni kwayo ngokuvutha komsindo wakho;Siyigqibile iminyaka yethu kanye njengokusebeza.
10  Imihla yeminyaka yethu yiminyaka engamashumi asixhenxe;Yaye ukuba ithe ngenxa yamandla akhethekileyo yangamashumi asibhozo,Ukuzingisa kwayo kusenkathazweni nakwizinto ezenzakalisayo;Kuba imele idlule ngokukhawuleza, siphaphazele simke.
11  Ngubani na owaziyo amandla omsindo wakhoNokuvutha komsindo wakho ngokokoyikeka kwakho?
12  Sibonise kanye indlela yokubala imihla yethu ngendlelaYokuba sizuze intliziyo yobulumko.
13  Buya, Yehova! Kuya kude kube nini na?Zisole ngenxa yabakhonzi bakho.
14  Sanelise kusasa ngobubele bakho bothando,Ukuze sibe nokumemelela ngovuyo size sibe nemihlali ebudeni bayo yonke imihla yethu.
15  Senze sibe nemihlali ngokulinganayo nemihla owasixhwalekisa ngayo,Iminyaka esibone ngayo intlekele.
16  Ngamana umsebenzi wakho ungabonakala kubakhonzi bakhoNobungangamsha bakho koonyana babo.
17  Ukuthandeka kukaYehova uThixo wethu makube phezu kwethu,Nomsebenzi wezandla zethu wumisele ngokuqinileyo phezu kwethu.Ewe, umsebenzi wezandla zethu, wumisele ngokuqinileyo.
146  Dumisani uYa!Dumisa uYehova, mphefumlo wam.
2  Ndiza kumdumisa uYehova ebudeni bexesha lokudla kwam ubomi.Ndiza kumculela uncuthu lwengoma uThixo wam lo gama ndisekho.
3  Musani ukukholosa ngezidwangube,Nangonyana womntu wasemhlabeni, lowo ungenalo usindiso.
4  Uyaphuma umoya wakhe, abuyele yena emhlabeni wakhe;Ngaloo mini ziyatshabalala iingcamango zakhe.
5  Unoyolo lowo unoncedo olunguTHIXO kaYakobi,Othemba lakhe likuYehova uThixo wakhe,
6  UMenzi wezulu nomhlaba,Wolwandle, nowazo zonke izinto ezikuzo,Lowo ugcina inyaniso ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo,
7  Lowo uphumezela abaqhathiweyo umgwebo,Lowo unika abalambileyo isonka.UYehova ukhulula abo babotshiweyo.
8  UYehova uvula amehlo eemfama;UYehova uphakamisa abo baqubudileyo;UYehova uthanda abo bangamalungisa.
9  UYehova ulinda abaphambukeli;Ukhulula inkwenkwe engenayise nomhlolokazi,Kodwa indlela yabangendawo uyenza ibe gwenxa.
10  UYehova uya kuba ngukumkani ukusa kwixesha elingenammiselo,UThixo wakho, Ziyon, kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.Dumisani uYa!
130  Ndisezinzulwini ndibize kuwe, Yehova.
2  Owu Yehova, live ilizwi lam.Ngamana iindlebe zakho zingaliphulaphula ilizwi lesibongozo sam.
3  Ukuba ubulinda iziphoso, Ya,Owu Yehova, ngubani na obenokuma?
4  Kuba ukuxolela kokwenyaniso kukuwe,Ukuze woyikwe.
5  Bendinethemba, Yehova, umphefumlo wam ubunethemba,Yaye ndilindele ilizwi lakhe.
6  Umphefumlo wam ulindele kuYehovaNgaphezu kwabalindi bakusasa,Belindele intsasa.
7  USirayeli makaqhubeke elindele kuYehova.Kuba ububele bothando bukuYehova,Yaye ininzi inkululo yakhe.
8  Yaye yena uya kumkhulula uSirayeli kuzo zonke iziphoso zakhe.
83  Owu Thixo, musa ukuthula;Musa ukuqhubeka ungathethi, yaye musa ukuthi cwaka, Wena Ungokobuthixo.
2  Kuba, khangela! iintshaba zakho ziyaxokozela;Nabo bakuthiye kakhulu bayiphakamisile intloko yabo.
3  Ngobuqhokolo bagqugula ngabantu bakho;Yaye babenzela amayelenqe abafihliweyo bakho.
4  Bathe: “Yizani masibatshayeleni njengohlanga,Ukuze igama likaSirayeli lingabuyi likhunjulwe.”
5  Kuba bacebisene ngokumanyeneyo ngentliziyo;Benza umnqophiso nxamnye nawe,
6  Iintente zikaEdom nezamaIshamayeli, uMowabhi namaHagri,
7  UGebhali noAmoni noAmaleki,ElamaFilisti kunye nabemi baseTire.
8  KwaneAsiriya izihlanganise nabo;Bayingalo koonyana bakaLote. Seʹlah.
9  Yenza kubo njengakwiMidiyan, njengakuSisera,NjengakuYabhin entlanjeni yaseKishon.
10  Babhujiswa e-Endore;Baba ngumgquba womhlaba.
11  Ke zona izidwangube zabo, ezi zenze zibe njengo-Orebhi noZehebhe,NanjengoZebha nanjengoTsalmuna zonke iindwalutho zabo,
12  Abathe: “Masizidle ilifa iindawo zokuhlala zikaThixo ngokwethu.”
13  Owu Thixo wam, benze babe njengesivuthe-vuthe sameva,Njengeendiza ngaphambi komoya.
14  Njengomlilo otshisa ihlathiNanjengedangatye elitshisa iintaba,
15  Ngamana ungabasukela ngaloo ndlela kanye njengesivuthuvuthuYaye ngamana ungabaphazamisa ngomoya wakho wesaqhwithi.
16  Buzalise ngehlazo ubuso babo,Ukuze abantu balifune igama lakho, Yehova.
17  Owu ngamana bangaba neentloni baphazamiseke ngamaxesha onke,Yaye ngamana bangadana batshabalale;
18  Ukuze abantu bazi ukuba wena, ogama linguYehova,Nguwe wedwa Oyena Uphakamileyo phezu komhlaba wonke.
65  Owu Thixo, iza kuwe indumiso—ukuthula—Thixo, eZiyon;Yaye isibhambathiso siya kufezekiswa kuwe.
2  Owu mphulaphuli wemithandazo, abantu bayo yonke inyama baya kuza kuwe.
3  Izinto ezisisiphoso zingqineke zinamandla kunam.Ke kona ukunxaxha kwethu, uya kukugubungela.
4  Unoyolo lowo umkhethayo uze umbangele asondele,Ukuze ahlale ezintendelezweni zakho.Ngokuqinisekileyo siya kwaneliswa kukulunga kwendlu yakho,Indawo engcwele yetempile yakho.
5  Uya kusiphendula ngezinto ezoyikekayo ngobulungisa,Thixo wosindiso lwethu,INkoloseko yayo yonke imida yomhlaba nabo bakude elwandle.
6  Umisela ngokuqinileyo iintaba ngamandla akhe;Eneneni ubhinqe ukomelela.
7  Uthulisa ingxolo yeelwandle,Ingxolo yamaza azo nengxokozelo yamaqela eentlanga.
8  Abemi bezona nxalenye ziseziphelweni baya kuyoyika imiqondiso yakho;Ukuphuma kwentsasa nokuhla ukubangela kumemelele ngovuyo.
9  Uyiphethulele emhlabeni ingqalelo yakho, ukuze uwunike intabalala;Uwutyebisa kakhulu.Umsinga ovela kuThixo uzele ngamanzi.Ulungisa ukudla kwabo okuziinkozo,Kuba leyo yindlela owulungisa ngayo umhlaba.
10  Kukho ukuzaliswa ngamanzi kwemijelo yawo, ukulungelelaniswa kwamafu awo;Uwuthambisa ngomvumbi; uyawasikelela amahlumelo awo.
11  Unyaka uwuthwese ukulunga kwakho,Yaye umkhondo wakho uthontsiza ukutyeba.
12  Amadlelo asentlango aqhubeka ethontsiza,Yaye iinduli zibhinqa uvuyo.
13  Amadlelo ambeswe imihlambi,Iintili zigutyungelwe kukudla okuziinkozo.Ziduma ngoloyiso, ewe, ziyacula.
70  Owu Thixo, khawuleza ukuza kundihlangula,Owu Yehova, khawuleza ukuza kundinceda.
2  Mababe neentloni badane abo bafuna umphefumlo wam.Mababuye umva bathotywe abo bayoliswa yintlekele yam.
3  Mababuyele emva ngenxa yokuhlazeka abo bathi: “Heke, heke!”
4  Ngamana bangagcoba babe nemihlali ngawe, bonke abo bakufunayo,Yaye ngamana rhoqo bangathi: “Thixo yenziwa mkhulu!”—abo bathanda usindiso lwakho.
5  Kodwa ndixhwalekile yaye ndilihlwempu.Owu Thixo, ndikhawulezisele.Uluncedo lwam noMsindisi wam.Owu Yehova, musa ukulibala kakhulu.
12  Ndisindise, Yehova, kuba lowo unyanisekileyo ufikelele esiphelweni;Kuba abantu abathembekileyo bathe shwaka phakathi koonyana babantu.
2  Bayaqhubeka bethetha okungeyonyaniso omnye komnye;Ngomlebe ogudileyo bayaqhubeka bethetha nangentliziyo embaxa.
3  UYehova uya kuyinqumla yonke imilebe egudileyo,Ulwimi oluthetha izinto ezinkulu,
4  Abo bathe: “Ngolwimi lwethu siya koyisa.Imilebe yethu ikuthi. Ngubani na oya kuba yinkosi  kuthi?”
5  “Ngenxa yokuphangwa kwabo baxhwalekileyo, ngenxa yokuncwina kwabo bangamahlwempu,Ngesi sihlandlo ndiya kuvuka,” utsho uYehova.“Ndiya kumbeka endaweni ekhuselekileyo kuye nabani na omfuthelayo.”
6  Amazwi kaYehova ngamazwi asulungekileyo,Njengesilivere esulungekiswe kwiziko lokunyibilikisa lomhlaba, yacikizwa kasixhenxe.
7  Wena, Yehova, uya kubalinda;Uya kugcina ngamnye kwesi sizukulwana kuse kwixesha elingenammiselo.
8  Abangendawo bahambahamba macala onke,Ngenxa yokuba ububi buyaphakanyiswa phakathi koonyana babantu.
